caitanyadevaṃ bhagavantam āśraye śrīvaiṣṇavānāṃ pramude'ñjasā likhan
āvaśyakaṃ karma vicārya sādhubhiḥ sārdhaṃ samāhṛtya samastaśāstrataḥ
bhakter vilāsāṃś cinute prabodhānandasya śiṣyo bhagavatpriyasya
gopālabhaṭṭo raghunāthadāsaṃ saṃtoṣayan rūpasanātanau ca
mathurānāthapādābjapremabhaktivilāsataḥ
jātaṃ bhaktivilāsākhyaṃ tadbhaktāḥ śīlayantv imam
jīyāsur ātyantikabhaktiniṣṭhāḥ śrīvaiṣṇavā māthuramaṇḍale'tra
kāśīśvaraḥ kṛṣṇavane cakāstu śrīkṛṣṇadāsaś ca salokanāthaḥ
ādau sakāraṇaṃ lekhyaṃ śrīgurvāśrayaṇaṃ tataḥ
guruḥ śiṣyaḥ parīkṣādir bhagavān manavo 'sya ca
mantrādhikārī siddhyādiśodhanaṃ mantrasaṃskriyāḥ
dīkṣā nityaṃ brāhmakāle śubhotthānaṃ pavitratā
prātaḥ smṛtyādi kṛṣṇasya vādyādaiś ca prabodhanam
nirmālyottāraṇādyādau maṅgalārātrikaṃ tataḥ
maitrādikṛtyaṃ śaucācamanaṃ dantasya dhāvanam
snānaṃ tāntrikasandhyādi devasadmādisaṃskriyā
tulasyādyāhṛtir gehasnānam uṣṇodakādikam
vastraṃ pīṭhaṃ cordhvapuṇḍraṃ śrīgopīcandanādikam
cakrādimudrā mālā ca gṛhasandhyārcanaṃ guroḥ
māhātmyaṃ cātha kṛṣṇasya dvāraveśmāntarārcanam
pūjārthāsanam arghyādisthāpanaṃ vighnavāraṇam
śrīgurvādinatir bhūtaśuddhiḥ prāṇaviśodhanam
nyāsamudrāpañcakaṃ ca kṛṣṇadhyānāntarārcane
pūjā padāni śrīmūrtiśālagrāmaśilās tathā
dvārakodbhavacakrāṇi śuddhayaḥ pīṭhapūjanam
āvāhanādi tanmudrā āsanādisamarpaṇam
snapanaṃ śaṅkhaghaṇṭādivādyaṃ nāmasahasrakam
purāṇapāṭho vasanam upavītaṃ vibhūṣaṇam
gandhaḥ śrītulasīkāṣṭhacandanaṃ kusumāni ca
patrāṇi tulasī cāṅgopāṅgāvaraṇapūjanam
dhūpo dīpaś ca naivedyaṃ pānaṃ homo balikriyā
avagaṇḍūṣādyāsyavāso divyagandhādikaṃ punaḥ
rājopacārā gītādi mahānīrājanaṃ tathā
śaṅkhādivādanaṃ sāmbuśaṅkhanīrājanaṃ stutiḥ
natiḥ pradakṣiṇā karmādyarpaṇaṃ japayācane
āgaḥkṣamāpaṇaṃ nānāgāṃsi nirmālyadhāraṇam
śaṅkhāmbutīrthaṃ tulasīpūjā tanmṛttikādi ca
dhātrīsnānaniṣedhasya kālo vṛtter upārjanam
madhyāhne vaiśadevādiśrāddhaṃ cānarpyam acyute
vinārcām aśane doṣās tathānarpitabhojane
naivedyabhakṣaṇaṃ santaḥ satsaṅgo 'sadasaṅgatiḥ
asadgatir vaiṣṇavopahāsanindādiduṣphalam
satāṃ bhaktir viṣṇuśāstraṃ śrīmadbhāgavataṃ tathā
līlākathā ca bhagavaddharmāḥ sāyaṃ nijakriyāḥ
karmapātaparīhāras trikālārcā viśeṣataḥ
naktaṃ kṛtyānyatho pūjāphalasiddhyādidarśanam
viṣṇvarthadānaṃ vividhopacārā nyūnapūraṇam
śayanaṃ mahimārcāyāḥ śrīmannāmnas tathādbhutaḥ
nāmāparādhā bhaktiś ca premāthāśrayaṇādayaḥ
pakṣeṣv ekādaśī sāṅgā śrīdvādaśyaṣṭakaṃ mahat
kṛtyāni mārgaśīrṣādimāseṣu dvādaśeṣv api
puraścaraṇakṛtyāni mantraṃ siddhasya lakṣaṇam
mūrtyāvirbhāvanaṃ mūrtipratiṣṭhā kṛṣṇamandiram
jīrṇoddhṛtiḥ śrītulasīvivāho 'nanyakarma ca
kṛpayā kṛṣṇadevasya tadbhaktajanasaṅgataḥ
bhakter māhātmyam ākarṇya tām icchan sadguruṃ bhajet
atrānubhūyate nityaṃ duḥkhaśreṇī paratra ca
duḥsahā śrūyate śāstrāt titīrṣed api tāṃ sudhīḥ
tathā coktam ekādaśaskandhe labdhvā sudurlabham idaṃ bahusambhavānte mānuṣyam arthadam anityam apīha dhīraḥ
tūrṇaṃ yateta na pated anumṛtyu yāvan niḥśreyasāya viṣayaḥ khalu sarvataḥ syāt
svayaṃ śrībhagavatā ca nṛdeham ādyaṃ sulabhaṃ sudurlabhaṃ plavaṃ sukalpaṃ gurukarṇadhāram
mayānukūlena nabhasvateritaṃ pumān bhavābdhiṃ na taret sa ātmahā
tatraiva śrīprabuddhayogeśvaroktau tasmād guruṃ prapadyeta jijñāsuḥ śreya uttamam
śābde pare ca niṣṇātaṃ brahmaṇy upaśamāśrayam
svayaṃ śrībhagavaduktau madabhijñaṃ guruṃ śāntam upāsīta madātmakam
kramadīpikāyāṃ ca
vipraṃ pradhvastakāmaprabhṛtiripughaṭaṃ nirmalāṅgaṃ gariṣṭhāṃ bhaktiṃ kṛṣṇāṅghripaṅkeruhayugalarajorāgiṇīm udvahantam
vettāraṃ vedaśāstrāgamavimalapathāṃ saṃmataṃ satsu dāntaṃ vidyāṃ yaḥ saṃvivitsuḥ pravaṇatanumanā deśikaṃ saṃśrayeta
śrutāv api
tadvijñānārthaṃ sa gurum evābhigacchet samitpāṇiḥ śrotriyaṃ brahmaniṣṭham
ācāryavān puruṣo veda
śrībhāgavate daśamaskandhe śrutistutau vijitahṛṣīkavāyubhir adāntamanasturagaṃ ya iha yatanti yantum atilolam upāyakhidaḥ
vyasanaśatānvitāḥ samavahāya guroś caraṇaṃ vaṇija ivāja santy akṛtakarṇadharā jaladhau
śrutau ca
naiṣā tarkeṇa matir āpaneyā proktānyenaiva sujñānāya preṣṭha
mantramuktāvalyām
avadātānvayaḥ śuddhaḥ svocitācāratatparaḥ
āśramī krodharahito vedavit sarvaśāstravit
śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca priyavāk priyadarśanaḥ
śuciḥ suveśas taruṇaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
dhīmān anuddhatamatiḥ pūrṇo 'haṃtāvimarśakaḥ
saguṇo 'rcāsu kṛtadhīḥ kṛtajñaḥ śiṣyavatsalaḥ
nigrahānugrahe śakto homamantraparāyaṇaḥ
ūhāpohaprakārajñaḥ śuddhātmā yaḥ kṛpālayaḥ
ityādilakṣaṇair yukto guruḥ syād garimānidhiḥ
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ ca
devatopāsakaḥ śānto viṣayeṣv api niḥspṛhaḥ
adhyātmavid brahmavādī vedaśāstrārthakovidaḥ
uddhartuṃ caiva saṃhartuṃ samartho brāhmaṇottamaḥ
tattvajño yantramantrāṇāṃ marmabhettā rahasyavit
puraścaraṇakṛddhomamantrasiddhaḥ prayogavit
tapasvī satyavādī ca gṛhastho gurur ucyate
viṣṇusmṛtau
paricaryāyaśolābhalipsuḥ śiṣyād gurur nahi
kṛpāsindhuḥ susampūrṇaḥ sarvasattvopakārakaḥ
niḥspṛhaḥ sarvataḥ siddhaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ
sarvasaṃśayasaṃchettā nālaso gurur āhṛtaḥ
śrīnāradapañcarātre śrībhagavannāradasaṃvāde
brāhmaṇaḥ sarvakālajñaḥ kuryāt sarveṣv anugraham
tadabhāvād dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ śāntātmā bhagavanmayaḥ
bhāvitātmā ca sarvajñaḥ śāstrajñaḥ satkriyāparaḥ
siddhitrayam āyukta ācāryatve'bhiṣecitaḥ
kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīnāṃ kṣatriyo 'nugrahe kṣamaḥ
kṣatriyasyāpi ca guror bhāvād īdṛśo yadi
vaiśyaḥ syāt tena kāryaś ca dvaye nityam anugrahaḥ
sajātīyena śūdreṇa tādṛśena mahāmate
anugrahābhiṣekau ca kāryau śūdrasya sarvadā
kiṃca
varṇottam'tha ca gurau sati yā viśrute'pi ca
svadeśato 'that vānyatra nedaṃ kāryaṃ śubhārthinā
vidyamāne tu yaḥ kuryāt yatra tatra viparyayam
tasyehāmutra nāśaḥ syāt tasmācchāstroktam ācaret
kṣatraviṭśūdrajātīyaḥ prātilomyaṃ na dīkṣayet
pādme ca
mahābhāgavataḥ śreṣṭho brāhmaṇo vai gurur nṛṇām
sarveṣām eva lokānām asau pūjyo yathā hariḥ
mahākūlaprasūto 'pi sarvayajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ
sahasraśākhādhyāyī ca na guruḥ syād avaiṣṇavaḥ
gṛhītaviṣṇudīkṣāko viṣṇupūjāparo naraḥ
vaiṣṇavo 'bhihito 'bhijñair itaro 'smād avaiṣṇavaḥ
tattvasāgare
bahvāśī dīrghasūtrī ca viṣayādiṣu lolupaḥ
hetuvādarato duṣṭo 'vāgvādī guṇanindakaḥ
aromā bahuromā ca ninditāśramasevakaḥ
kāladanto 'sitauṣṭhaś ca durgandhiśvāsavāhakaḥ
duṣṭalakṣaṇasampanno yadyapi svayam īśvaraḥ
bahupratigrahāsakta ācāryaḥ śrīkṣayāvahaḥ
mantramuktāvalyām
śiṣyaḥ śuddhānvayaḥ śrīmān vinītaḥ priyadarśanaḥ
satyavāk puṇyacarito 'dabhradhīr dambhavarjitaḥ
kāmakrodhaparityāgī bhaktaś ca gurupādayoḥ
devatāpravaṇaḥ kāyamanovāgbhir divāniśam
nīrujo nirjitāśeṣapātakaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
dvijadevapitṝṇāṃ ca nityam arcāparāyaṇaḥ
yuvā viniyatāśeṣakaraṇaḥ karuṇālayaḥ
ityādilakṣaṇair yuktaḥ śiṣyo dīkṣādhikāravān
ekādaśaskandhe ca
amāny amatsaro dakṣo nirmamo dṛḍhasauhṛdaḥ
asatvaro 'rthajijñāsur anasūyur amoghavāk
agastyasaṃhitāyām
alasā malināḥ kliṣṭā dāmbhikāḥ kṛpaṇās tathā
daridrā rogiṇo ruṣṭā rāgiṇo bhogalālasāḥ
asūyāmatsaragrastāḥ śaṭhāḥ paruṣavādinaḥ
anyāyopārjitadhanāḥ paradāraratāś ca ye
viduṣāṃ vairiṇaś caiva ajñāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ
bhraṣṭavratāś ca ye kaṣṭavṛttayaḥ piśunāḥ khalāḥ
bahvāśinaḥ krūraceṣṭā durātmanaś ca nindita
ity evamādayo 'py anye pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ
akṛtyebhyo 'nivāryāś ca guruśikṣāsahiṣṇavaḥ
evambhūtāḥ parityājyāḥ śiṣyatve nopakalpitāḥ
yady ete hy upakalperan devatākrośabhājanāḥ
bhavantīha daridrās te putradāravivarjitāḥ
nārakāś caiva dehānte tiryañcaḥ prabhavanti te
hayaśīrṣapañcarātre
jaiminiḥ sugataś caiva nāstiko nagna eva ca
kapilaś cākṣapādaś ca ṣaḍ ete hetuvādinaḥ
etanmatānusāreṇa vartante ye narādhamāḥ
te hetuvādinaḥ proktās tebhyas tantraṃ na dāpayet
tayoḥ parīkṣā cānyo 'nyam ekābdaṃ sahavāsataḥ
vyavahārasvabhāvānubhavenaivābhijāyate
mantramuktāvalyāṃ
tayor vatsaravāsena jñātānyonyasvabhāvayoḥ
gurutā śiṣyatā ceti nānyathaiveti niścayaḥ
śrutiś ca
nāsaṃvatsaravāsine deyāt
sārasaṃgrahe'pi
sadguruḥ svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣam ekaṃ parīkṣayet
rājñi cāmātyajā doṣāḥ patnīpāpaṃ svabhartari
tathā śiṣyārjitaṃ pāpaṃ guruḥ prāpnoti niścitam
kramadīpikāyāṃ tu
saṃtoṣayed akuṭilādretarāntarātmā taṃ svair dhanaiś ca vapuṣāpy anukūlavāṇyā
abdatrayaṃ kamalanābhadhiyātidhīras tuṣṭe vivakṣatu gurāv atha mantradīkṣām
kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
udakumbhaṃ kuśān puṣpaṃ samidho 'syāharet sadā
mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ nityam aṅgānāṃ vāsasāṃ caret
nāsya nirmālyaśayanaṃ pādukopāsanahāv api
ākrāmed āsanaṃ chāyām āsandīṃ vā kadācana
sādhayed dantakāṣṭhādīn kṛtyaṃ cāsmai nivedayet
anāpṛcchya na gantavyaṃ bhavet priyahite rasaḥ
na pādau sārayed asya sannidhāne kadācana
jṛmbhāhāsyādikaṃ caiva kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇaṃ tathā
varjayet sannidhau nityam athāsphoṭanam eva ca
kiṃca
śreyas tu guruvad vṛttir nityam eva samācaret
guruputreṣu dāreṣu guroś caiva svabandhuṣu
utsādanaṃ vai gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭabhojane
na kuryād guruputrasya pādayoḥ śaucam eva ca
guruvat paripūjyāś ca savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ
asavarṇās tu saṃpūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ
abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanam eva ca
gurupatnyā ca kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam
devyāgame śrīśivoktau
guruśayyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pāduke pādapīṭhakam
snānodakaṃ tathā chāyāṃ laṅghayen na kadācana
guror agre pṛthakpūjām advaitaṃ ca parityajet
dīkṣāṃ vyākhyāṃ prabhutvaṃ ca guror agre vivarjayet
śrīnāradoktau
yatra yatra guruṃ paśyet tatra tatra kṛtāñjali
praṇamet daṇḍavad bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ
guror vākyāsanaṃ yānaṃ pādukopānahau tathā
vastraṃ chāyāṃ tathā śiṣyo laṅghayen na kadācana
śrīmanusmṛtau
nodāhared guror nāma parokṣam api kevalam
na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣaṇaceṣṭitam
guror gurau saṃnihite guruvad dhṛtim ācaret
na cāvisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivādayet
śrīnāradapañcarātre
yathā tathā yatra tatra na gṛhṇīyāc ca kevalam
abhaktyā na guror nāma gṛhṇīyāc ca yatātmavān
praṇavaḥ śrīs tato nāma viṣṇuśabdād anantaram
pādaśabdasametaṃ ca natamūrdhāñjalīyutaḥ
kiṃca
na tam ājñāpayen mohāt tasyājñāṃ na ca laṅghayet
nānivedya guroḥ kiṃcid bhoktavyaṃ vā guros tathā
anyatra ca
āyāntam agrato gacched gacchantaṃ tam anuvrajet
āsane śayane vāpi na tiṣṭhed agrato guroḥ
yat kiṃcid annapānādi priyaṃ dravyaṃ manoramam
samarpya gurave paścāt svayaṃ bhuñjīta pratyaham
śrīviṣṇusmṛtau
na guror apriyaṃ kuryāt tāḍitaḥ pīḍito 'pi vā
nāvamanyeta tadvākyaṃ nāpriyaṃ hi samācaret
ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair api
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
śrīnāradapañcarātre
yo vakti nyāyarahitam anyāyena śṛṇoti yaḥ
tāv ubhau narakaṃ ghoraṃ vrajataḥ kālam akṣayam
vaiṣṇavatantre
trāyasva bho jagannātha guro saṃsāravahninā
dagdhaṃ māṃ kāladaṣṭaṃ ca tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
tatra śrīvāsudevasya sarvadevaśiromaṇeḥ
pādāmbujaikabhāg eva dīkṣā grāhyā manīṣibhiḥ
prathamaskandhe
sattvaṃ rajas tama iti prakṛter guṇās tair yuktaḥ paramapuruṣa eka ihāsya dhatte
sthityādaye hariviriñcihareti saṃjñāḥ śreyāṃsi tatra khalu sattvatanor nṝṇāṃ syuḥ
kiṃca
athāpi yatpādanakhāvasṛṣṭaṃ jagad viriñcopahṛtārhaṇāmbhaḥ
seśaṃ punāty anyatamo mukundāt ko nāma loke bhagavatpadārthaḥ
śrīdaśamaskandhe
tan niśamyātha munayo vismitā muktasaṃśayāḥ
bhūyāṃsaṃ śraddadhur viṣṇuṃ yataḥ śāntir yato 'bhayam
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
vyāmohāya carācarasya jagatas te te purāṇāgamās tāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi
siddhānte punar eka eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samastāgamavyāpāreṣu vivecanavyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate
nārasiṃhe
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyam utkṣipya bhujam ucyate
vedācchāstraṃ paraṃ nāsti na devaḥ keśavāt paraḥ
yataḥ pādme
arir mitraṃ viṣṃ pathyam adharmo dharmatāṃ vrajet
suprasanne hṛṣīkeśe viparīte viparyayaḥ
tatraiva śrībhagavadvākyam
mannimittaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpam api dharmāya kalpate
mām anādṛtya dharmo 'pi pāpaṃ syān matprabhāvataḥ
ata evoktaṃ skānde śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo 'nyaṃ devam upāsate
svamātaraṃ parityajya śvapacīṃ vandate hi saḥ
tatraivānyatra
vāsudevaṃ parityajya yo 'nyaṃ devam upāsate
tyaktvāmṛtaṃ sa mūḍhātmā bhuṅkte halāhalaṃ viṣam
mahābhārate
yas tu viṣṇuṃ parityajya mohād anyam upāsate
sa hemarāśim utsṛjya pāṃśurāśiṃ jighṛkṣati
anādṛtya tu yo viṣṇum anyadevaṃ samāśrayet
gaṅgāmbhasaḥ sa tṛṣṇārto mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ pradhāvati
pañcarātre
yo mohād viṣṇum anyena hīnadevena durmatiḥ
sādhāraṇaṃ sakṛd brūte so 'ntyajo nāntyajo 'ntyajaḥ
vaiṣṇavatantre
na labheyuḥ punar bhaktiṃ harer aikāntikīṃ janāḥ
ekāgramanasaś cāpi viṣṇusāmānyadarśinaḥ
anyatra ca
yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahmarudrādidaivataiḥ
samatvenaiva vīkṣeta sa pāṣaṇḍī bhaved dhruvam
sahasranāmastotrādau ślokaughāḥ santi cedṛśāḥ
viśeṣataḥ sattvaniṣṭhaiḥ sevyo viṣṇur na cāparaḥ
tathā ca śrīharivaṃśe śivavākyam
harir eva sadārādhyo bhavadbhiḥ sattvasaṃsthitaiḥ
viṣṇumantraṃ sadā viprāḥ paṭhadhvaṃ dhyāta keśavam
īdṛṅmāhātmyavākyeṣu saṃgṛhīteṣu sarvataḥ
granthabāhulyadoṣaḥ syāl likhyante'pekṣitāni tat
āgame
mantrān śrīmantrarājādīn vaiṣṇavān gurvanugrahāt
sarvaiśvaryaṃ japan prāpya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam
puṇyaṃ varṣasahasrair yaiḥ kṛtaṃ suvipulaṃ tapaḥ
japanti vaiṣṇavān mantrān narās te lokapāvanāḥ
vaiṣṇave ca
prajapan vaiṣṇavān mantrān yaṃ yaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā
padā vā saṃspṛśet sadyo mucyate'sau mahābhayāt
likhyate viṣṇumantrāṇāṃ mahimātha viśeṣataḥ
tātparyataḥ śrīgopālamantramāhātmyapuṣṭaye
padmapurāṇe devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
sāṅgaṃ samudraṃ sanyāsaṃ saṛṣidaivatam
sadīkṣāvidhi sadhyānaṃ sayantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram
aṣṭākṣaraṃ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ
tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śudhyete yato viṣṇavaḥ svayam
śaṅkhinaś cakriṇo bhūtvā brahmāyur vanamālinaḥ
vasanti vaiṣṇave loke viṣṇurūpeṇa te narāḥ
tatraiva dvādaśākṣarayas caturthaskandhe
japaś ca paramo guhyaḥ śrūyatāṃ me nṛpātmaja
yaṃ saptarātraṃ prapaṭhan pumān paśyati khecarān
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe
gatvā gatvā nivartante candrasūryādayo grahāḥ
adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ
aṣṭākṣarasya yathā nāradapañcarātre
trayo vedāḥ ṣaḍaṅgāni chandāṃsi vividhāḥ surāḥ
sarvam aṣṭākṣarāntaḥsthaṃ yac cānyad api vāṅmayam
sarvavedāntasārārthaṃ saṃsārārṇavatāraṇaḥ
gatir aṣṭākṣaro nṝṇāṃ na punar bhavakāṅkṣiṇām
yatrāṣṭākṣarasaṃsiddho mahābhāgo mahīyate
na tatra saṃcariṣyanti vyādhidurbhikṣataskarāḥ
devadānavagandharvāḥ siddhavidyādharādayaḥ
praṇamanti mahātmānam aṣṭākṣaravidaṃ naram
vyaktaṃ hi bhagavān eva sākṣān nārāyaṇaḥ svayam
aṣṭākṣarasvarūpeṇa mukheṣu parivartate
pādmottarakhaṇḍe
evam aṣṭākṣaro mantro jñeyaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
sarvaduḥkhaharaḥ śrīmān sarvamantrātmakaḥ śubhaḥ
liṅgapurāṇe
kim anyair bahubhir mantraiḥ kim anyair bahubhir vrataiḥ
namo nārāyaṇeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu namo nārāyaṇeti yaḥ
japet sa yāti viprendra viṣṇulokaṃ sabāndhavaḥ
bhaviṣyapurāṇe
aṣṭākṣaro mahāmantraḥ sarvapāpaharaḥ paraḥ
sarveṣāṃ viṣṇumantrāṇāṃ rājatve parikīrtitaḥ
śrīśukavyāsasaṃvāde ca
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
bhaktānāṃ japatāṃ tāta svargamokṣaphalapradaḥ
eṣa eva paro mokṣa eṣa svarga udāhṛtaḥ
sarvavedarahasyebhyaḥ sāra eṣa samuddhṛtaḥ
viṣṇunā vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu hitāya manunā purā
kīrtitaḥ sarvapāpaghnaḥ sarvakāmapradāyakaḥ
nārāyaṇāya nama ity ayam eva satyaṃ saṃsāraghoraviṣasaṃharaṇāya mantraḥ
śṛṇvantu satyamatayo muditās tarāgā uccaistarām upadiśāmy aham ūrdhvabāhuḥ
bhūtvordhvabāhur adyāhaṃ satyapūrvaṃ bravīmi vaḥ
he putraśiṣyāḥ śṛṇuta na mantro 'ṣṭākṣarāt paraḥ
ata evoktaṃ gāruḍe
āsīno vā śayāno vā tiṣṭhāno yatra tatra vā
namo nārāyaṇeti mantraikaśaraṇo bhavet
tāpanīśrutiṣu
devā ha vai prajāpatim abruvann ānuṣṭubhasya mantrarājasya nārasiṃhasya phalaṃ no brūhi bhagava iti sa hovāca prajāpatirya etaṃ mantrarājaṃ nārasiṃham ānuṣṭubhaṃ nityam adhīte so 'gnipūto bhavati sa vāyupūto bhavati sa ādityapūto bhavati sa somapūto bhavati sa satyapūto bhavati sa brahmapūto bhavati sa viṣṇupūto bhavati sa rudrapūto bhavati sa sarvapūto bhavati sa sarvapūto bhavati
tatraivānte
anupanītaśatam ekam ekenopanītena tatsamam
upanītaśatam ekam ekena gṛhasthena tatsamam
gṛhasthaśatam ekam ekena vānaprasthena tat samaṃ
vānaprasthaśatam ekam ekena yatinā tat samaṃ
yatīnāṃ tu śataṃ pūrṇam ekam ekena rudrajāpakena tatsamam
rudrajāpakaśatam ekam ekena atharvaśiraḥśikhādhyāpakena tatsamam
tad vā etat paramaṃ dhāma mantrarājādhyāpakasya yatra na sūryas tapati yatra na vāyur vāti yatra na candramā bhāti yatra na nakṣatrāṇi bhānti yatra nāgnir dahati yatra na mṛtyuḥ praviśati yatra na duḥkhaṃ sadānandaṃ paramānandaṃ śāntaṃ śāśvataṃ sadāśivaṃ brahmādivanditaṃ yogidhyeyaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ yatra gatvā na nivartante yoginaḥ
tad etad ṛcābhyuktam
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ
divīva cakṣur ātatam
tad viprāso vipanyavo jāgṛvāṃsaḥ samindhate
viṣṇor yat paramaṃ padam
agastyasaṃhitāyām
sarveṣu mantravargeṣu śreṣṭhaṃ vaiṣṇavam ucyate
gāṇapatyeṣu śaiveṣu śāktasaureṣv abhīṣṭadam
vaiṣṇaveṣv api mantreṣu rāmamantrāḥ phalādhikāḥ
gāṇapatyādimantrebhyaḥ koṭikoṭiguṇādhikāḥ
vinaiva dīkṣāṃ viprendra puraścaryāṃ vinaiva hi
vinaiva nyāsavidhinā japamātreṇa siddhidāḥ
mantreṣv aṣṭasv anāyāsaphalado 'yaṃ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ
ṣaḍakṣaro 'yaṃ mantras tu mahāghaughanivāraṇaḥ
mantrarāja iti proktaḥ sarveṣām uttamottamaḥ
dainandinaṃ tu duritaṃ pakṣamāsartuvarṣajam
sarvaṃ dahati niḥśeṣaṃ tūlācalam ivānalaḥ
brahmahatyāsahasrāṇi jñānājñānakṛtāni ca
svarṇasteyasurāpānagurutalpayutāni ca
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi hyupapāpāni yāny api
sarvāṇy api praṇaśyanti rāmamantrānukīrtanāt
tāpanīśrutiṣu ca
ya etattārakaṃ brāhmaṇo nityam adhīte sa pāpmānaṃ tarati sa mṛtyuṃ tarati sa bhrūhatyāṃ tarati sa sarvahatyāṃ tarati sa saṃsāraṃ tarati sa sarvaṃ tarati sa vimuktāśrito bhavati so 'mṛtatvaṃ ca gacchati
mantrās tu kṛṣṇadevasya sākṣād bhagavato hareḥ
sarvāvatārabījasya sarvato vīryavattamāḥ
tathā ca bṛhadgautamīye śrīgovindavṛndāvanākhye
sarveṣāṃ mantravaryāṇāṃ śreṣṭho vaiṣṇava ucyate
viśeṣāt kṛṣṇamanavo bhogamokṣaikasādhanam
yasya yasya ca mantrasya yo yo devas tathā punaḥ
abhedāt tanmanūnāṃ ca devatā saiva bhāṣyate
kṛṣṇa eva paraṃ brahma saccidānandavigrahaḥ
smṛtimātreṇa teṣāṃ vai bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ
tatrāpi bhagavattāṃ svāṃ tanvato gopalīlayā
tasya śreṣṭhatamā mantrās teṣv apy aṣṭādaśākṣaraḥ
tāpanīśrutiṣu
oṃ munayo ha vai brahmāṇam ūcuḥ
kaḥ paramo devaḥ
kuto mṛtyur bibheti
kasya jñānenākhilaṃ jñātaṃ bhavati
kenedaṃ viśvaṃ saṃsaratīti
tān u hovāca brāhmaṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vai paramaṃ daivatam
govindān mṛtyur bibheti
gopījanavallabhajñānenākhilaṃ jñātaṃ bhavati
svāhayedaṃ saṃsaratīti
tam u hocuḥ
kaḥ kṛṣṇo govindaḥ ko 'sau gopījanavallabhaḥ kaḥ kā svāheti
tān uvāca brāhmaṇaḥ pāpakarṣaṇo gobhūmivedavidito veditā gopījanāvidyākalāprerakas tanmāyā ceti
sakalaṃ paraṃ brahmaiva tat
yo dhyāyati rasati bhajati so 'mṛto bhavati so 'mṛto bhavatīti
te hocuḥ kiṃ tadrūpaṃ kiṃ rasanaṃ kathaṃ vāho tadbhajanaṃ
tat sarvaṃ vividiṣatām ākhyāhīti
tad u hovāca hairaṇyaḥ gopaveśam abhrābhaṃ taruṇaṃ kalpadrumāśritam
kiṃca tatraivāgre
bhaktir asya bhajanam
tad ihāmutropādhinairāsyenaivāmuṣmin manaḥkalpanam
etad eva ca naiṣkarmyam
kṛṣṇaṃ taṃ viprā bahudhā yajanti govindaṃ santaṃ bahudhārādhayanti
gopījanavallabho bhuvanāni dadhre svāhāśrito jagad ejayjat svaretāḥ
vāyur yathaiko bhuvanaṃ praviṣṭo janye janye pañcarūpo babhūva
kṛṣṇas tathaiko 'pi jagaddhitārthaṃ śabdenāsau pañcapado vibhāti
kiṃca tatraivopāsanavidhikathanānantaram
eko vaśī sarvagaḥ kṛṣṇa īḍya eko 'pi san bahudhā yo vibhāti
taṃ pīṭhasthaṃ ye 'nubhajanti dhīrās teṣāṃ sukhaṃ śāśvataṃ netareṣām
nityo nityānāṃ cetanaś cetanānām eko bahūnāṃ yo vidadhāti kāmān
taṃ pīṭhagaṃ ye 'nubhajanti dhīrās teṣāṃ siddhiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām
etad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ ye nityamuktāḥ saṃyajante na kāmān
teṣām asau goparūpaḥ prayatnāt prakāśayed ātmapadaṃ tadaiva
yo brahmāṇaṃ vidadhāti pūrvaṃ yo vidyās tasmai gopāyati sma kṛṣṇaḥ
taṃ ha daivam ātmabuddhiprakāśaṃ mumukṣur vai śaraṇam anuvrajeta
oṃkāreṇāntaritaṃ ye japanti govindasya pañcapadaṃ manum
teṣām asau darśayed ātmarūpaṃ tasmān mumukṣur abhyasen nityaśāntyai
tasmād anye pañcapadād abhūvan govindasya manavo mānavānām
daśārṇādyās te'pi saṅkrandanādyair abhyasyante bhūtikāmair yathāvat
kiṃca tatraiva
tad u hovāca brāhmaṇo 'sāv anavarataṃ me dhyātaḥ stutaḥ parārdhānte so 'budhyata
gopaveśo me puruṣaḥ purastād āvirbabhūva
tataḥ praṇatena mayānukūlena hṛdā mahyam aṣṭādaśārṇaṃ svarūpaṃ sṛṣṭaye dattvāntarhitaḥ
punaḥ sisṛkṣā me prādurabhūt
teṣv akṣareṣu bhaviṣyajjagadrūpaṃ prakāśayat
tad iha kād āpaḥ
lāt pṛthivī
īto 'gniḥ
bindor induḥ
tannādād arka iti klīṃkārād asṛjam
kṛṣṇād ākāśaṃ yad vāyur ity uttarāt surabhiṃ vidyāṃ prādurakārṣam
taduttarāt taduttarāt strīpumādi cedaṃ sakalam idaṃ iti
tathā ca gautamīyatantre
klīṃkārād asṛjad viśvam iti prāha śruteḥ śiraḥ
lakārāt pṛthivī jātā kakārāj jalasambhavaḥ
īkārād vahnir utpanno nādād āyur ajāyata
bindor ākāśasambhūtir iti bhūtātmako manuḥ
svāśabdena ca kṣetrajño heti citprakṛtiḥ parā
tayor aikyasamudbhūtir mukhaveṣṭanavarṇakaḥ
ata eva hi viśvasya layaḥ svāhārṇake bhavet
punaś ca sā śrutiḥ
etasyaiva yajanena candradhvajo gatamoham ātmānaṃ vedayitvā oṃkārāntarālakaṃ manum āvartayat saṅgarahito 'bhyānayat
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ
divīva cakṣur ātatam
tasmād enaṃ nityam abhyaset
tatraivāgre
yasya pūrvapadād bhūmir dvitīyāt salilodbhavaḥ
tṛtīyāt teja udbhūtaṃ caturthād gandhavāhanaḥ
pañcamād ambarotpattis tam evaikaṃ samabhyaset
candradhvajo 'gamad viṣṇuḥ paramaṃ padam avyayam
tato viśuddhaṃ vimalaṃ viśokam aśeṣalobhādinirastasaṅgam
yat tat padaṃ pañcapadaṃ tad eva sa vāsudevo na yato 'nyad asti
tam ekaṃ govindaṃ saccidānandavigraham pañcapadaṃ vṛndāvanasurabhūruhatalāsīnaṃ satataṃ samarudgaṇo 'haṃ paramayā stutyā toṣayāmi
kiṃca stutyanantaram
amuṃ pañcapadaṃ mantram āvartayed yaḥ sa yāty anāyāsataḥ kevalaṃ tat padaṃ tat
anejad ekaṃ manaso javīyo naitad devā āpnuvan pūrvam arśāt
tasmāt kṛṣṇa eva paro devas taṃ dhyāyet taṃ raset taṃ yajed iti oṃ tat sad iti
trailokyasaṃmohanatantre ca
devīṃ prati śrīmahādevoktāṣṭādaśākṣaraprasaṅga eva
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇām īśvaro jagadīśvaraḥ
santi tasya mahābhāgā avatārāḥ sahasraśaḥ
teṣāṃ madhye'vatārāṇāṃ bālatvam atidurlabham
amānuṣāṇi karmāṇi tāni tāni kṛtāni ca
śāpānugrahakartṛtve yena sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
tasya mantraṃ pravakṣyāmi sāṅgopāṅgam anuttamam
yasya vijñānamātreṇa naraḥ sarvajñatām iyāt
putrārthī putram āpnoti dharmārthī labhate dhanam
sarvaśāstrārthapārajño bhavaty eva na saṃśayaḥ
trailokyaṃ ca vaśīkuryāt vyākulīkurute jagat
mohayet sakalaṃ so 'pi mārayet sakalān ripūn
bahunā kim ihoktena mumukṣur mokṣam āpnuyāt
yathā cintāmaṇiḥ śreṣṭho yathā gauś ca yathā satī
yathā dvijo yathā gaṅgā tathāsau mantra uttamaḥ
yathāvad akhilaśreṣṭhaṃ yathā śāstraṃ tu vaiṣṇavam
yathā susaṃskṛtā vāṇī tathāsau mantra uttamaḥ
kiṃca
ato mayā sureśāni pratyahaṃ japyate manuḥ
naitena sadṛśaḥ kaścid jagaty asmin carācare
sanatkumārakalpe'pi
gopālaviṣayā mantrās trayastriṃśat prabhedataḥ
teṣu sarveṣu mantreṣu mantrarājam imaṃ śṛṇu
suprasannam imaṃ mantraṃ tantre sammohanāhvaye
gopanīyas tvayā mantro yatnena munipuṅgava
anena mantrarājena mahendratvaṃ purandaraḥ
jagāma devadeveśo viṣṇunā dattam añjasā
durvāsasaḥ purā śāpād asaubhāgyena pīḍitaḥ
sa eva subhagavatvaṃ vai tenaiva punar āptavān
bahunā kim ihoktena puraścaraṇasādhanaiḥ
vināpi japamātreṇa labhate sarvam īpsitam
prabhuṃ śrīkṛṣṇacaitanyaṃ taṃ nato 'smi gurūttamam
kathañcid āśrayād yasya prākṛto 'py uttamo bhavet
tāntrikeṣu ca mantreṣu dīkṣāyāṃ yoṣitām api
sādhvīnām adhikāro 'sti śūdrādīnāṃ ca saddhiyām
tathā ca smṛtyarthasāre pādme ca vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
āgamoktena mārgeṇa strīśūdrair api pūjanam
kartavyaṃ śraddhayā viṣṇoś cintayitvā patiṃ hṛdi
śūdrāṇāṃ caiva bhavati nāmnā vai devatārcanam
sarve 'py āgamamārgeṇa kuryur vedānukāriṇā
strīṇām apy adhikāro 'sti viṣṇor ārādhanādiṣu
patipriyaratānāṃ ca śrutir eṣā sanātanī
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ śrīrāmamantrarājam uddiśya
śucivratatamāḥ śūdrā dhārmikā dvijasevakāḥ
striyaḥ pativratāś cānye pratilomānulomajāḥ
lokāś cāṇḍālaparyantāḥ sarve'py atrādhikāriṇaḥ
guruś ca siddhasādhyādimantradāne vicārayet
svakulāny akulatvaṃ ca bālaprauḍhatvam eva ca
strīpuṃnapuṃsakatvaṃ ca rāśinakṣatramelanam
suptaprabodhakālaṃ ca tathā ṛṇadhanādikam
saradātilake
prāk pratyag agrā rekhāḥ syuḥ pañca yāmyottarāgragāḥ
tāvatyaś ca catuṣkoṣṭhacatuṣkaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhavet
indvagnirudranavanetrayugena dikṣu ṛtvaṣṭaṣaḍdaśacaturdaśabhautikeṣu
pātālapañcadaśavahnihimāṃśukoṣṭhe varṇāṃl likhel lipibhavān kramaśas tu dhīmān
caturbhiḥ koṣṭhakais tv ekam iti koṣṭhacatuṣṭaye
punaḥ koṣṭhakakoṣṭheṣu savyato janmabhākṣarāt
siddhasādhyasusiddhārikramāj jñeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ
siddhaḥ sidhyati kālena sādhyas tu japahomataḥ
susiddho grahamātreṇa arir mūlanikṛntanaḥ
siddhasiddho yathoktena dviguṇāt siddhasādhakaḥ
siddhasusiddho 'rdhajapāt siddhārir hanti bāndhavān
sādhyasiddho dviguṇikaḥ sādhyasādhyo hy anarthakaḥ
tatsusiddhas triguṇitāt sādhyārir hanti gotrajān
susiddhasiddho 'rdhajapāt tatsādhyas tu guṇādhikāt
tatsusiddho grahād eva susiddhāriḥ svagotrahā
arisiddhaḥ sutān hanyād arisādhyas tu kanyakāḥ
tatsusiddhas tu patnīghnas tadarir hanti sādhakam
tathā ca tantre asya ca mantraviśeṣe'pavādaḥ
nṛsiṃhārkavarāhāṇāṃ prāsādapraṇavasya ca
vaidikasya ca mantrasya siddhādīn naiva śodhayet
svapnalabdhe striyā datte mālāmantre ca tryakṣare
ekākṣare tathā mantre siddhādīn naiva śodhayet
svakulāny akulatvādi vijñeyaṃ cāgamāntarāt
na vistarabhayād atra vyarthatvād api likhyate
śrīmadgopāladevasya sarvaiśvaryapradarśinaḥ
tādṛkśaktiṣu mantreṣu nahi kiṃcid vicāryate
tathā ca kramadīpikāyām
sarveṣu varṇeṣu tathāśrameṣu nārīṣu nānāhvayajanmabheṣu dātā phalānām abhivāñchitānāṃ drāg eva gopālakamantra eṣaḥ
trailokyasaṃmohanatantre ca
aṣṭādaśākṣaramantram adhikṛtya śrīśivenoktam
na cātra śātravā doṣā narṇasvādivicāraṇā
ṛkṣarāśivicāro vā na kartavyo manau priye
kecic chinnāś ca ruddhāś ca kecin madasamuddhatāḥ
malināḥ stambhitāḥ kecit kīlitā dūṣitā api
etair doṣair yuto nāyaṃ yatas tribhunottamaḥ
sāmānyataś ca yathā bṛhadgautamīye
atha kṛṣṇamanūn vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalapradān
yān vai vijñāya munayo lebhire muktim añjasā
gṛhasthā vanagāś caiva yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ
striyaḥ śūdrādayaś caiva sarve yatrādhikāriṇaḥ
nātra cintyo 'riśuddhyādir nārimitrādilakṣaṇam
na vā prayāsabāhulyaṃ sādhane na pariśramaḥ
ajñānatūlarāśeś ca analaḥ kṣaṇamātrataḥ
siddhasādhyasusiddhārirūpā nātra vicāraṇā
sarveṣāṃ siddhamantrāṇāṃ yato brahmākṣaro manuḥ
prajāpatir avāpāgryaṃ devarājyaṃ śacīpatiḥ
avāpus tridaśāḥ svargaṃ vāgīśatvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ
tatraivāntare
viṣṇubhaktyā viśeṣeṇa kiṃ na sidhyati bhūtale
kīṭādibrahmaparyantaṃ govindānugrahān mune
sarvasampattinilayāḥ sarvatrāpy akutobhayāḥ
ityādi kathitaṃ kiṃcin māhātmyaṃ vo munīśvarāḥ
ākāśe tārakā yadvat sindhoḥ saikatasṛṣṭivat
etadvijñānamātreṇa labhen muktiṃ caturvidhām
etadanyeṣu mantreṣu doṣāḥ santi pare ca ye
tadarthaṃ mantrasaṃskārā lipyante tantrato daśa
saradātilake
jananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti tāḍanaṃ rodhanaṃ tathā
athābhiṣeko vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥ
tarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ guptir daśaitā mantrasaṃskriyāḥ
mantrāṇāṃ mātṛkāmadhyād uddhāro jananaṃ smṛtam
praṇavāntaritān kṛtvā mantravarṇān japet sudhīḥ
etaj jīvanam ity āhur mantratantraviśāradāḥ
manor varṇān samālikhya tāḍayec candanāmbhasā
pratyekaṃ vāyunā mantrī tāḍanaṃ tad udāhṛtam
vilikhya mantraṃ taṃ mantrī prasūnaiḥ karavīrajaiḥ
tanmantrākṣarasaṃkhyātair hanyād yat tena rodhanam
svatantroktavidhānena mantrī mantrārṇasaṅkhyayā
aśvatthapallavair mantram abhiṣiñced viśuddhaye
saṃcintya manasā mantraṃ yotir mantreṇa nirdahet
mantre mūlatrayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ tv idam
tāravyomāgnimanuyugadaṇḍī jyotir manur mataḥ
kuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ
tena mantreṇa vidhivad etad āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam
mantreṇa vāriṇā yantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtam
tāramāyāramāyogo manor dīpanam ucyate
japyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tv aprakāśanam
balitvāt kṛṣṇamantrāṇāṃ saṃskārāpekṣaṇaṃ nahi
sāmānyoddeśamātreṇa tathāpy etad udīritam
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse gauravo nāma prathamo vilāsaḥ
taṃ śrīmatkṛṣṇacaitanyaṃ vande jagadgurum
yasyānukampayā śvāpi mahābdhiṃ saṃtaret sukham
atha dīkṣāvidhiḥ
dīkṣāvidhir likhyate'trānusṛtya kramadīpikām
vinā dīkṣāṃ hi pūjāyāṃ nādhikāro 'sti karhicit
āgame
dvijānām anupetānāṃ svakarmādhyayanādiṣu
yathādhikāro nāstīha syāc copanayanād anu
tathātrādīkṣitānāṃ tu mantradevārcanādiṣu
nādhikāro 'sty ataḥ kuryād ātmānaṃ śivasaṃstutam
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
te narāḥ paśavo loke kiṃ teṣāṃ jīvane phalam
yair na labdhā harer dīkṣā nārcito vā janārdanaḥ
tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvāde viṣṇuyāmale ca
adīkṣitasya vāmoru kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam
paśuyonim avāpnoti dīkṣāvirahito janaḥ
viśeṣato viṣṇuyāmale
snehād vā lobhato vāpi yo gṛhṇīyād adīkṣayā
tasmin gurau saśiṣye tu devatāśāpa āpatet
viṣṇurahasye ca
avijñāya vidhānoktaṃ haripūjāvidhikriyām
kurvan bhaktyā samāpnoti śatabhāgaṃ vidhānataḥ
divyaṃ jñānaṃ yato dadyāt kuryāt pāpasya saṅkṣayam
tasmād dīkṣeti sā proktā deśikais tattvakovidaiḥ
ato guruṃ praṇamyaivaṃ sarvasvaṃ vinivedya ca
gṛhṇīyād vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣāpūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ
skānde tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
tapasvinaḥ karmaniṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhās te vai narā bhuvi
prāptā yais tu harer dīkṣā sarvaduḥkhavimocinī
tantrasāgare ca
yathā kāñcanatāṃ yāti kāṃsyaṃ rasavidhānataḥ
tathā dīkṣāvidhānena dvijatvaṃ jāyate nṛṇām
āgame
mantrasvīkaraṇaṃ caitre bahuduḥkhaphalapradam
vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam
āṣāḍhe bandhunāśāya śrāvaṇe tu bhayāvaham
prajāhānir bhādrapade sarvatra śubham āśvine
kārttike dhanavṛddhiḥ syān mārgaśīrṣe śubhapradam
pauṣe tu jñānahāniḥ syān māghe medhāvivardhanam
phālgune sarvavaśyatvam ācāryaiḥ parikīrtitam
kvacicca
samṛddhiḥ śrāvaṇe nūnaṃ jñānaṃ syāt kārttike tathā
phālgune'pi samṛddhiḥ syān malamāsaṃ parityajet
gautamīye
mantrārambhas tu caitre syāt samastapuruṣārthadaḥ
vaiśākhe ratnalābhaḥ syāt jyaiṣṭhe tu maraṇaṃ dhruvam
āṣāḍhe bandhunāśaḥ syāt pūrṇāyuḥ śrāvaṇe bhavet
prajānāśo bhaved bhādre āśvine ratnasañcayaḥ
kārttike mantrasiddhiḥ syāt mārgaśīrṣe tathā bhavet
pauṣe tu śatrupīḍā syāt māghe medhāvivardhanam
phālgune sarvakāmāḥ syur malamāsaṃ parityajet
skānde tatraiva śrīrukmāṅgadamohinīsaṃvāde
kārttike tu kṛtā dīkṣā nṝṇāṃ janmanikṛntanī
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dīkṣāṃ kurvīta kārttike
śrīmadgopālamantrāṇāṃ dīkṣāyāṃ tu na duṣyati
caitramāse yad uktā tad dīkṣā tatraiva deśikaiḥ
ravau gurau tathā some kartavyaṃ budhaśukrayoḥ
nāradatantre
rohiṇī śravaṇārdrā ca dhaniṣṭhā cottarātrayaḥ
puṣyaṃ śatabhiṣaś caiva dīkṣānakṣatram ucyate
kvacicca
aśvinīrohiṇīsvātiviśākhāhastabheṣu ca
jyeṣṭhottarātrayeṣv eva kuryān mantrābhiṣecanam
sārasaṅgrahe
dvitīyā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhī caiva viśeṣataḥ
dvādaśyām api kartavyaṃ trayodaśyām athāpi ca
kvacic ca
pūrṇimā pañcamī caiva dvitīyā saptamī tathā
trayodaśī ca daśamī praśastā sarvakāmadā
evaṃ śuddhe dine śuklapakṣe śukragurūdaye
sallagne candratārānukūle dīkṣā praśasyate
rudrayāmale
sattīrthe'rkavidhugrāse tantudāmanaparvaṇoḥ
mantradīkṣāṃ prakurvīta māsarkṣādi na śodhayet
sulagnacandratārādibalam atra sadaiva hi
labdho 'tra mantro dīrghāyuḥsampatsantativardhanaḥ
sūryagrahaṇakālena samāno nāsti kaścana
yatra yad yat kṛtaṃ sarvam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet
na māsatithivārādiśodhanaṃ sūryaparvaṇi
tattvasāgare ca
durlabhe sadgurūṇāṃ ca sakṛt saṅga upasthite
tadanujñā yadā labdhā sa dīkṣāvasaro mahān
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye kṣetre vā divase niśi
āgacchati gurur daivād yadā dīkṣā tadājñayā
yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā guror ājñānurūpataḥ
na tīrthaṃ na vrataṃ homo na snānaṃ na japakriyā
dīkṣāyāḥ karaṇaṃ kintu svecchāprāpte tu sadgurau
kriyāvatyādibhedena bhaved dīkṣā caturvidhā
tatra kriyāvatī dīkṣā saṅkṣepeṇaiva likhyate
bhūmiṃ saṃskṛtya tasyāṃ cārcayitvā vāstudevatāḥ
saptahastamitaṃ kuryān maṇḍapaṃ ramyavedikam
aṣṭadhvajaṃ caturdhāraṃ kṣīrapādapatoraṇam
triguṇīkṛtasūtrāḍhyaṃ kuśamālābhiveṣṭitam
tasmiṃś ca diśi kauveryāṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ trimekhalam
kuṇḍe kuryāc caturviṃśatyaṅgulipramitaṃ budhaḥ
khātaṃ trimekhalocchrāyasahitaṃ tāvad ācaret
tasmāt khātād bahiḥ kuryāt kaṇṭham ekāṅgulaṃ dhruvam
tatrādymekhalocchrāyavistārau caturaṅgulau
tryaṅgulau tau dvitīyāyās tṛtīyāyā yugāṅgulau
yoniṃ ca paścime bhāge mekhalātritayopari
ṣaḍaṅgulāṃ ca vistāre dairghye ca dvādaśāṅgulām
ekāṅgulāṃ tathocchrāye madhye chidrasamanvitām
gadādharākṛtiṃ kuryād vidhivan mekhalānvitām
śatārdhahome kuṇḍaṃ syād ūrdhvamuṣṭikaronmitam
śatahome'ratnimātram sahasre pāṇinā mitam
lakṣe caturbhir hastaiś ca koṭau tair aṣṭabhir mitam
caturasraṃ kuṇḍakhātaṃ kurvītādhaś ca tādṛśam
homas tv adhikasaṅkhyākaḥ kuṇḍe vai nyūnasaṅkhyayā
kṛte kāryo na c anyūnasaṅkhyākaḥ saṅkhyādhike
yathāvidhy eva kartavyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatnena dhīmatā
anyathā bahavo doṣā bhaveyur bahuduḥkhadāḥ
tad uktaṃ tāntrikaiḥ
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kuṇḍam iṣṭaphalapradam
anekadoṣadaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatra nyūnādhikām bhavet
tasmāt samyak parīkṣyaiva kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā
hastamātraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā saṃkṣipte homakarmaṇi
hārītenāpi
vistārādhikyahīnatve alpāyur jāyate dhruvam
khātādhikye bhaved yogī hīne tu dhanasaṃkṣayaḥ
kuṇḍe vakre ca santāpo maraṇaṃ chinnamekhale
śokas tu mekhalonatve tadādhikye paśukṣayaḥ
bhāryānāśo yonihīne kaṇṭhahīne śubhakṣayaḥ
aṅguliparimāṇaṃ coktam
tiryagyavodarāṇyaṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā vrīhayas trayaḥ
jñeyam aṅgulimānaṃ tu madhyamā madhyaparvaṇā
viśeṣo 'pekṣito 'nyatra sraksruvaprakriyādikaḥ
jñeyo granthāntarāt so 'trādhikyabhītyā na likhyate
athokṣite pañcagavyair gandhāmbhobhiś ca maṇḍape
yathāvidhi likhed dīkṣāmaṇḍalaṃ vedikopari
tanmadhye cāṣṭapatrābjaṃ bahir vṛttatrayaṃ tataḥ
tato rāśīṃs tataḥ pīṭhaṃ catuṣpādasamanvitam
tasmād bahiś caturdikṣu likhed vīthīcatuṣṭayam
śobhāpaśobhākoṇāḍhyaṃ tato dvāracatuṣṭayam
prātaḥkṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā yathāsthānaṃ nyaset tataḥ
śaṅkhaṃ pūjopacārāṃś ca purolekhyaprakārataḥ
gurūn gaṇeśaṃ cābhyarcya pīṭhapūjāṃ vidhāya ca
padmamadhye nyaset śālīṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca kuśāṃs tathā
vahner daśakalā yādivarṇādyāś ca kuśopari
nyasyābhyarcya japaṃs tāraṃ nyaset kumbhaṃ yathoditam
tāś coktāḥ
dhūmrārcir uṣmā jvalanī jvālinī visphuliṅginī
suśrīḥ surūpā kapilā havyakavyavahe api
kādyaṣṭhāntair yutā bhādyair ḍāntaiś cārṇair vilomagaiḥ
sūryasya ca kalāḥ kumbhe dvādaśa nyasya pūjayet
adhunā tasmin kuṇḍe sūryakalānāṃ nyāsādikaṃ likhati kādyair iti
kakārādyaiṣ ṭhakārāntair arṇair varṇair yutā dvādaśāpi kalāḥ
cakāraḥ samuccaye
bhakārādyair ḍakārāntair varṇair api yutāḥ
nanu bhakārādīnāṃ dvādaśavarṇānāṃ ḍakārāntatā kathaṃ syāt krameṇa kṣakārāntatāprāptes tatrāhavilomagaiḥ vyutkramaprāptaiḥ
ayam arthaḥ anulomapaṭhitakakārādyaikaikam akṣaraṃ pratilomapaṭhitabhakārādyekaikākṣareṇa sahitam ādau sūryakalāsu saṃyojya nyāsādikaṃ kuryād iti
prayogaś ca kaṃ bhaṃ tapanyai nama ityādi
tāś coktāḥ
tapanī tāpanī dhūmrā bhrāmarī jvālinī ruciḥ
suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvā bodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamā
kumbhāntar nikṣipen mūlamantreṇa kusumaṃ sitam
sākṣataṃ sasitaṃ svarṇaṃ saratnaṃ ca kuśāṃs tathā
tataś coktaprakāreṇādhārarūpam agniṃ kumbharūpaṃ sūryaṃ ca vicintya kumbhasya tasya antar madhye śuklakusumādikaṃ kṣipet
sasitaṃ saśarkaram
tad uktam
prottolayitvā tanmadhye śuklapuṣpaṃ sitāyutam
svarṇaṃ ratnaṃ ca kūrcaṃ ca mūlenaiva vinikṣipet
yac ca mūlagranthārthād adhikaṃ kiṃcil likhate tat pūrvagatasya yathoditam ity asyānuvartanād iti jñeyam
kumbhaṃ ca vidhinā tīrthāmbunā śuddhena pūrayet
jale cendukulā nyasya sasvarāḥ ṣoḍaśārcayet
tāś coktāḥ
amṛtā mānadā pūṣā tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭī ratir dhṛtiḥ
śaśinī candrikā kāntir jyotsnā śrīḥ prītir aṅgadā
pūrṇā pūrṇāmṛtā ca
śuddhāmbupūrite śaṅkhe kṣiptvā gandhāṣṭakaṃ kalāḥ
āvāhya sarvās tāḥ prāṇapratiṣṭhām ācaret kramāt
gandhāṣṭakaṃ coktam
uśīraṃ kuṅkumaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bālakaṃ cāgurur murā
jaṭāmāṃsī candanaṃ cetīṣṭaṃ gandhāṣṭakaṃ hareḥ
kaiścic candanakarpūrāgurukuṅkumarocanāḥ
kakkolakapimāṃsyaś ca gandhāṣṭakam idaṃ matam
tathaivākārajā varṇaiḥ kādibhir daśabhir daśa
ukārajāṣṭakārādyaiḥ pakārādyair makārajāḥ
catasro bindujāḥ ṣādyaiś caturbhir nādajāḥ kalāḥ
svaraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhir yuktā nyasecchaṅkhe ca ṣoḍaśa
tāś coktāḥ
sṛṣṭir ṛddhiḥ smṛtir medhā kāntir lakṣmīr dhṛtiḥ sthirā
sthitiḥ siddhir akārotthāḥ kalā daśa samīritaḥ
jarā ca pālinī śāntir aiśvarī ratikāmike
varadā hlādinī prītir dīrghā cokārajāḥ kalāḥ
tīkṣṇā raudrā bhayā nidrā tantīḥ kṣut krodhanī kriyā
utkārī caiva mṛtyuś ca makārākṣarajāḥ kalāḥ
nivṛttiś ca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntis tathaiva ca
indhikā dīpikā caiva recikā mocikā parā
sūkṣmā sūkṣmāmṛtā jñānājñānā cāpy āyanī tathā
vyāpinī vyomarūpā ca anantā nādasambhavāḥ
nyāsaṃ kalānāṃ sarvāsāṃ kuryād ekaikaśaḥ kramāt
nāmoccārya caturthāntaṃ tattadvarṇair namo'ntakam
pūrvaṃ prāṇapratiṣṭhāyās tāsām āvāhanāt param
ṛcaḥ pañca yathāsthānaṃ paṭhet tāś cārcayet kalāḥ
haṃśaḥ śuciṣad ityādau pratad viṣṇus tataḥ param
tryambakaṃ tat savitur viṣṇur yonim iti kramāt
tac ca śaṅkhodakaṃ kumbhe mūlamantreṇa nikṣipet
pidadhyāt tanmukhaṃ śakravallīcūtādipallavaiḥ
śarāvenātha puṣpādiyuktenācchādya tat punaḥ
saṃveṣṭya vastrayugmena tataḥ kumbhaṃ ca maṇḍayet
tasminn āvāhya kalase paraṃ tejo yathāvidhi
sakalīkṛtya cācāryaḥ pūjayed āsanādibhiḥ
sakalīkaraṇaṃ coktam
devatāṅge ṣaḍaṅgānāṃ nyāsaḥ syāt sakalīkṛtiḥ
kecic cāhuḥ karanyāsau vinākhilaiḥ
nyāsais tattejasaḥ sāṅgīkaraṇaṃ sakalīkṛtaḥ
evaṃ ca kumbhe taṃ sāṅgopāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ prabhum
agrato lekhyavidhinārcayed bhojyārpaṇāvadhi
naivedyārpaṇataḥ paścān maṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ
sadīpān paiṣṭikān nyasyet sabījāṅkurabhājanāt
tato dīkṣāṅgahomārthaṃ kuṇḍalasya ca sarvataḥ
saṃmārjya darbhamārjanyā yathāvidhy upalepayet
vikīrya sarṣapāṃs tatra gavyaiḥ samprokṣya pañcabhiḥ
madhye sampūjayed vāstupuruṣaṃ dikṣu tatpatīn
śoṣaṇādīni kuṇḍasya kṛtvā prokṣya kuśāmbubhiḥ
ullikhya cāsmin yonyādisahitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ likhet
śrībījaṃ madhyayonau ca vilikhyābhyukṣya pūjayet
nidhāya tatra puṣpādiviṣṭaraṃ sādhu kalpayet
tatra lakṣmīmṛtyusnānāṃ viṣṇuṃ cāvāhya pūjayet
tāmrādipātreṇānīyāgrato 'gniṃ sthāpayecchubhram
gandhādināgnim abhyarcya viṣṇoḥ sakrīḍataḥ śriyā
retorūpaṃ vicintyāmuṃ kuṇḍaṃ tāreṇa cārcayet
vaiśvānareti mantreṇācchādyāgniṃ taṃ sadindhanaiḥ
citpiṅgaleti prajvālyopatiṣṭhed agnim ity amum
jihvā nyasyet sapta tasminn apy aṅgeṣv aṅgadevatāḥ
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭ nyasya mūrtīś ca nyasyāṣṭābhyarcayec ca tāḥ
saptajihvāś coktāḥ
hiraṇyā gaganā raktā tathā kṛṣṇā ca suprabhā
bahurūpātirūpā ca sapta jihvā vasor imāḥ
sahasrārciḥ svastipūrṇa uttiṣṭhapuruṣas tathā
dhūmavyāpī saptajihvo dhanurdhara iti smṛtaḥ
jātavedāḥ saptajihvo havyavāhana eva ca
aśvodarajasaṃjñaś ca tathā vaiśvānaro 'paraḥ
kaumāratejāś ca tathā viśvadevamukhāhvayau
tato vahniṃ paristīrya saṃskṛtājyaṃ yathāvidhi
hutvā ca vyāhṛtīḥ paścāt trīn vārān juhuyāt punaḥ
tato 'sya garbhadhānādīn vivhāntān yathākramam
saṃskārān ācared uktamantreṇāṣṭāhutais tathā
itthaṃ hi saṃskṛte vahnau pīṭham abhyarcya tatra ca
devam āvāhya gandhādidīpāntavidhinārcayet
taṃ cāgniṃ devarasanāṃ saṃkalpyāṣṭottaraṃ budhaḥ
sahasraṃ juhuyāt sarpiḥśarkarāpāyasair yutaiḥ
hutvājyenātha mahatīvyāhṛtīr vidhinā kṛtī
graharkṣakaraṇādibhyo baliṃ dadyād yathoditam
karṣamātraṃ ghṛtaṃ home śuktimātraṃ payaḥ smṛtam
uktāni pañcagavyāni tatsamāni manīṣibhiḥ
tatsamaṃ madhudugdhānnam akṣamātram udāhṛtam
dadhi prasṛtimātraṃ syāt lājāḥ syuḥ muṣṭisaṃmitāḥ
atha natvāmbupānārthaṃ pradāyācamanāni ca
ātmārpaṇāntam abhyarcya lekhyena vidhinācaret
vratasthaṃ vāgyataṃ śiṣyaṃ praveśyātha yathāvidhi
taddehe mātṛkāṃ sāṅgāṃ nyasyāthopadiśec ca tām
devaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ kumbhagataṃ cānusmaran guruḥ
japtvāṣṭottarasāhasraṃ śayīta prāśya kiṃcana
darbhoparyajine tvaiṇe niviṣṭo mātṛkāṃ smaran
guruṃ ca śiṣyo nidrāṇaṃ tāṃ śayīta japan vratī
prātaḥkṛtyaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā kumbhaṃ cābhyarcya pūrvavat
hutvā dattvā baliṃ karmānyat kuryāt svārpaṇāvadhi
saṃhāramudrayā kṛṣṇe saṃyojyāvṛttidevatāḥ
tam cāmṛtamayaṃ dhyātvā svasmiṃś cāgniṃ vilāpayet
dhvajatoraṇadikkumbhamaṇḍapādyadhidevatāḥ
sarvā vibhāvya cidrūpāḥ kumbhe saṃyojya pūjayet
ato guruṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca viṣvaksenaṃ ca pūjayet
udvāsya kalasaṃ spṛṣṭvā śatam aṣṭottaraṃ japet
kṛtopavāsaḥ śiṣyo 'that prātaḥkṛtyaṃ vidhāya saḥ
śuklavastraḥ suveśaḥ san viprān dravyeṇa toṣayet
guruṃ ca bhagavaddṛṣṭyā parikramya praṇamya ca
dattvoktāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ tasmai svaśarīraṃ samarpayet
tathā ca daśamaskandhe
iyad eva hi sacchiṣyaiḥ kartavyaṃ guruniṣkṛtam
yad vai viśuddhabhāvena sarvārthātmārpaṇaṃ gurau
yāgālayād uttarasyām āśāyāṃ snānamaṇḍape
pīṭhe niveśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ kārayecchoṣaṇādikam
pīṭhanyāsāntam akhilaṃ mātṛkānyāsapūrvakam
nyāsaṃ śiṣyatanau kṛtvā pīṭhamantreṇa pūjayet
sadūrvākṣatapuṣpāṃ ca mūrdhni śiṣyasya rocanām
nidhāya kalasaṃ tasyāntike vādyādinā nayet
śrīkṛṣṇam atha saṃprārthya guruḥ kumbhasya vāsasā
nīrājya śiṣyaṃ tanmūrdhni nyaset tatpallavādikam
tad uktam
vidhivat kumbham uddhṛtya tanmukhasthān suradrumān
śiśoḥ śirasi vinyasya mātṛkāṃ manasā japet
tataḥ kumbhāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya trir mūlamantrataḥ
viprāśīr maṅgalodghoṣair abhiṣiñcen manūn paṭhan
vaśiṣṭhasaṃhitāyām
surās tvām abhiṣiñcyaṃ tu brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
vāsudevo jagannāthas tathā saṅkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ
pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca bhavantu vibhavāya te
ākhaṇḍalo 'gnir bhagavān yamo vai nirṛtis tathā
varuṇaḥ pavanaś caiva dhanādhyakṣas tathā śivaḥ
brahmaṇā sahitā hy ete dikpālāḥ pāntu vaḥ sadā
kīrtir lakṣmīr dhṛtir medhā puṣṭiḥ śraddhā kriyā gatiḥ
buddhir lajjā vapuḥ śāntir māyā nidrā ca bhāvanā
etās tvām abhiṣiñcantu rāhuḥ ketuś ca pūjitāḥ
devadānavagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ
ṛṣayo munayo gāvo devamātara eva ca
devapatnyo dhruvā nāgā daityā apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
astrāṇi sarvaśastrāṇi rājāno vāhanāni ca
auṣadhāni ca ratnāni kālasyāvayavāś ca ye
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailās tīrthāni jaladā nadāḥ
ete tvām abhiṣiñcantu dharmakāmārthasiddhaye
paridhāyāṃśuke śiṣya ācānto yāgamaṇḍape
gatvā bhaktyā guruṃ natvā guror āsīta dakṣiṇe
guruḥ samarpya gandhādīn puruṣāhārasaṃmitam
nivedya pāyasaṃ kṛṣṇe kuryāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ
sāmpradāyikamudrādibhūṣitaṃ taṃ kṛtāñjalim
pañcāṅgapramukhair nyāsaiḥ kuryāt śrīkṛṣṇasācchiśum
nyasya pāṇitalaṃ mūrdhni tasya karṇe ca dakṣiṇe
ṛṣyādiyuktaṃ vidhivan mantraṃ vāratrayaṃ vadet
dīrghamantraṃ ca śiṣyasya yāvad āgrahaṇaṃ paṭhet
gurudaivatamantraikyaṃ śiṣyas taṃ bhāvayan paṭhet
sākṣataṃ gurur ādāya vāri śiṣyasya dakṣiṇe
kare'rpayed vadan mantro 'yaṃ samo 'stv āvayor iti
svasmāj jyotirmayīṃ vidyāṃ gacchantīṃ bhāvayed guruḥ
āgatāṃ bhāvayecchiṣyo dhanyo 'smīti viśeṣataḥ
mahāprasādaṃ śiṣyāya dattvā tatpāyasaṃ guruḥ
nidadhyād akṣatān mūrdhni tasya yacchan śubhāśiṣam
guruṇā kṛpayā dattaṃ śiṣyaś cāvāpya taṃ manum
aṣṭottaraśataṃ japtvā samayān śṛṇuyāt tataḥ
śrīnāradapañcarātre
svamantro nopadeṣṭavyo vaktavyaś ca na saṃsadi
gopanīyaṃ tathā śāstraṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ śarīravat
vaiṣṇavānāṃ parā bhaktir ācāryāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ
pūjanaṃ ca yathāśakti tān āpannāṃś ca pālayet
prāptam āyatanād viṣṇoḥ śirasāṃ praṇato vahet
nikṣiped ambhasi tato na pated avanau yathā
somasūryāntarasthaṃ ca gavāśvatthāgnimadhyagam
bhāvayed daivataṃ viṣṇuṃ guruvipraśarīragam
yatra yatra parivādo mātsaryācchrūyate guroḥ
tatra tatra na vastavyaṃ niryāyāt saṃsmaran harim
yaiḥ kṛtā ca guror nindā vibhoḥ śāstrasya nārada
nāpi taiḥ saha vastavyaṃ vaktavyaṃ vā kathañcana
pradakṣiṇe prayāṇe ca pradāne ca viśeṣataḥ
prabhāte ca pravāse ca svamantraṃ bahuśaḥ smaret
svapne vākṣisamakṣaṃ vā āścaryam atiharṣadam
akasmād yadi jāyeta na khyātavyaṃ guror vinā
pañcarātrāntare
samayāṃś ca pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepāt pañcarātrakāt
na bhakṣayen matsyamāṃsaṃ kūrmaśūkarakāṃs tathā
kāṃsyapātre na bhuñjīta na plakṣavaṭapatrayoḥ
devāgāre na niṣṭhīvet kṣutaṃ cātra vivarjayet
na sopānatkacaraṇaḥ praviśed antaraṃ kvacit
ekādaśyāṃ na cāśnīyāt pakṣayor ubhayor api
jāgaraṃ niśi kurvīta viśeṣāc cārcayed vibhum
sammohanatantre ca
gopayed devatām iṣṭāṃ gopayed gurum ātmanaḥ
gopayec ca nijaṃ mantraṃ gopayen nijamālikām
caturyukśatasaṅkhyeṣu prāg guroḥ samayeṣu ca
śiṣyeṇāṅgīkṛteṣv eva dīkṣā kaiścana manyate
tathā ca viṣṇuyāmale
guruḥ parīkṣayecchiṣyaṃ saṃvatsaram atandritaḥ
niyamān vihitān varjyān śrāvayec ca catuḥśatam
brāhme muhūrta utthānaṃ mahāviṣṇoḥ prabodhanam
nīrājanaṃ ca vādyena prātaḥsnānaṃ vidhānataḥ
viśuddhāhatayugvastradhāraṇaṃ devatārcanam
gopīcandanamṛtsnāyāḥ sarvadā corddhvapuṇḍrakam
pañcāyudhānāṃ vidhṛtiś caraṇāmṛtasevanam
tulasīmaṇimālādibhūṣādhāraṇam anvaham
śālagrāmaśilāpūjā pratimāsu ca bhaktitaḥ
nirmālyatulasībhakṣas tulasyavacayo vidheḥ
vidhinā tāntrikī sandhyā śikhābandho hi karmaṇi
viṣṇupādodakenaiva pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇakriyā
mahārājopacāraiś ca śaktyāṃ sampūjanaṃ hareḥ
viṣṇubhaktyavirodhena nityanaimittikī kriyā
bhūtaśuddhyādikaraṇaṃ nyāsāḥ sarve yathāvidhi
navīnaphalapuṣpāder bhaktitaḥ saṃnivedanam
tulasīpūjanaṃ nityaṃ śrībhāgavatapūjanam
trikālaṃ viṣṇupūjā ca purāṇaśrutir anvaham
viṣṇor niveditānāṃ vai vastrādīnāṃ ca dhāraṇam
sarveṣāṃ puṇyakāryāṇāṃ svāmidṛṣṭyā pravartanam
gurvājñāgrahaṇaṃ tatra viśvāso guruṇodite
yathāsvamudrāracanaṃ gītanṛtyādi bhaktitaḥ
śaṅkhādidhvanimāṅgalyalīlādyabhinayo hareḥ
nityahomavidhānaṃ ca balidānaṃ yathāvidhi
sādhūnāṃ svāgataṃ pūjā śeṣanaivedyabhojanam
tāmbūlaśeṣagrahaṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaiḥ saha saṅgamaḥ
viśiṣṭadharmajijñāsā daśamyādidinatraye
vrate niyamataḥ svāsthyaṃ santoṣo yena kena vai
parvayātrādikaraṇaṃ vāsarāṣṭakasadvidhiḥ
viṣṇoḥ sarvartucaryā ca mahārājopacārataḥ
sarveṣāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vratānāṃ paripālanam
gurāv īśvarabhāvaś ca tulasīsaṅgrahaḥ sadā
śayanādyupacāraś ca rāmādīnāṃ ca cintanam
sandhyayoḥ śayanaṃ naiva na śaucaṃ mṛttikāṃ vinā
tiṣṭhatācamanaṃ naiva tathā gurvāsanāsanam
gurvagre pādavistāracchāyāyā laṅghanaṃ guroḥ
śaktau snānakriyāhānir devatārcanalopanam
devatānāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca pratyutthānādyabhāvanam
guroḥ purastāt pāṇḍityaṃ prauḍhapādakriyā tathā
amantratilakācāmo nīlīvastravidhāraṇam
abhaktaiḥ saha maitryādi asacchāstraparigrahaḥ
tucchasaṅgasukhāsaktir madyamāṃsaniṣevaṇam
mādakauṣadhasevā ca masurādyannabhojanam
śākaṃ tumbī kalañjādi tathābhaktānnasaṅgrahaḥ
avaiṣṇavavratārambhas tathā japyam avaiṣṇavam
abhicārādikaraṇaṃ śaktyā gauṇopacārakam
śokādipāravaśyaṃ ca digviddhaikādaśīvratam
śuklākṛṣṇāvibhedaś cāsadvyāpāro vrate tathā
śaktau phalādibhuktiś ca śrāddhaṃ caikādaśīdine
dvādaśyāṃ ca divāsvāpas tulasyāvacayas tathā
tatra viṣṇor divāsnānaṃ śrāddhaṃ haryaniveditaiḥ
vṛddhāv atulasīśrāddhaṃ tathā śrāddham avaiṣṇavam
caraṇāmṛtapāne'pi śuddhyarthācamanakriyā
kāṣṭhāsanopaviṣṭena vāsudevasya pūjanam
pūjākāle'sadālāpaḥ karavīrādipūjanam
āyasaṃ dhūpapātrādi tiryakpuṇḍraṃ pramādataḥ
pūjā cāsaṃskṛtair dravyais tathā cañcalacittataḥ
ekahastapraṇāmādi akāle svāmidarśanam
paryuṣitādiduṣṭānām annādīnāṃ nivedanam
saṅkhyāṃ vinā mantrajapas tathā mantraprakāśanam
sadā śaktyāṃ mukhyalopo gauṇakālaparigrahaḥ
prasādāgrahaṇaṃ viṣṇor varjayed vaiṣṇavaḥ sadā
catuḥśataṃ vidhīn etān niṣedhān śrāvayed guruḥ
aṅgīkāre kṛte bāḍhaṃ tannīrājanapūrvakam
devapūjāṃ kārayitvā dakṣakarṇe mantraṃ japet
tataś cotthāya pūrṇātmā daṇḍavat praṇamed gurum
tatpādapaṅkajaṃ śiṣyaḥ pratiṣṭhāpya svamūrdhani
atha nyāsān guruḥ svasmin kṛtvāntaryajanaṃ tathā
sāṣṭaṃ sahasraṃ tanmantraṃ svaśaktyakṣataye japet
śiṣyaḥ kumbhādi tat sarvaṃ dravam anyac ca śaktitaḥ
dattvābhyarcya guruṃ natvā viprān sampūjya bhojayet
śrīguror brāhmaṇānāṃ ca śubhāśīrbhiḥ samedhitaḥ
tān anujñāpya gurvādīn bhuñjīta saha bandhubhiḥ
iti dīkṣāvidhānena yo mantraṃ labhate guroḥ
sa bhāgyavān cirañjīvī kṛtakṛtyaś ca jāyate
tathā ca saṃmohanatantre śrīśivomāsaṃvāde
evaṃ yaḥ kurute martyaḥ kare tasya vibhūtayaḥ
ataḥ paraṃ mahābhāge nānyat karmāsti bhūtale
yasyācaraṇamātreṇa sākṣāt kṛṣṇaḥ prasīdati
prāyaḥ prapañcasārādāv ukto 'yaṃ tāntriko vidhiḥ
dīkṣāyā likhyate divyo vidhiḥ paurāṇiko 'dhunā
idānīṃ śṛṇu me devi pañcapātakanāśanam
yajanaṃ devadevasya viṣṇoḥ putravasupradam
iha janmani dāridryavyādhikuṣṭhādipīḍitaḥ
alakṣmīvān aputras tu yo bhavet puruṣo bhuvi
tasya sadyo bhavel lakṣmīr āyur vittaṃ sutāḥ sukham
dṛṣṭvā tu maṇḍale devi devaṃ devyā samanvitam
nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ devaṃ yaḥ paśyati vidhānataḥ
pūjitaṃ navanābhe tu ṣoḍaśābjadale tathā
ācāryadarśitaṃ devaṃ mantramūrtim ayonijam
kārttike māsi śuddhāyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ
sarvāsu ca yajed devaṃ dvādaśīṣu vidhānataḥ
saṅkrāntau ca mahābhāge candrasūryagrahe'pi vā
yaḥ paśyati hariṃ devaṃ pūjitaṃ guruṇā śubhe
tasya sadyo bhavet tuṣṭiḥ pāpadhvaṃso 'py aśeṣataḥ
sa sāmānyo hi devānāṃ bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca parīkṣaṇam
saṃvatsaraṃ guruḥ kuryāj jātiśaucakriyādibhiḥ
upasannāṃs tato jñātvā hṛdayenāvadhārayet
te'pi bhaktimato jñātvā ātmanaḥ parameśvaram
saṃvatsaraṃ guror bhaktiṃ kuryur viṣṇāv ivācalām
saṃvatsaraṃ tataḥ pūrṇe guruṃ caiva prasādayet
bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam
icchāmas tv aihikīṃ lakṣmīṃ viśeṣeṇa tapodhana
evam abhyarthya medhāvī guruṃ viṣṇum ivāgrataḥ
abhyarcya tadanujñāto daśamyāṃ kārttikasya tu
kṣīravṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mantritaṃ parameṣṭhinā
bhakṣayitvā śayītorvyāṃ devadevasya sannidhau
svapnān dṛṣṭvā guror agre śrāvayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ
tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ tadvad ālapet paramo guruḥ
ekādaśyām upoṣyātha snātvā devālayaṃ vrajet
guruś ca maṇḍalaṃ bhūmau kalpitāyāṃ tu vartayet
lakṣaṇair vividhair bhūmiṃ lakṣayitvā vidhānataḥ
ṣoḍaśāraṃ likhec cakraṃ navanābham athāpi vā
aṣṭapatram atho vāpi likhitvā darśayed budhaḥ
netrabandhaṃ prakurvīta sitavastreṇa yatnataḥ
varṇānukramataḥ śiṣyān puṣpahastān praveśayet
navanābhaṃ yadā kuryān maṇḍalaṃ varṇakair budhaḥ
tadānīṃ pūrvato devam indram aindryāṃ tu pūjayet
lokapālam athāgneyyām agniṃ sampūjayed dvijaḥ
yamaṃ tad anu yāmyāyāṃ nairṛtyāṃ nirṛtiṃ nyaset
vāruṇyāṃ varuṇaṃ caiva vāyavyāṃ pavanaṃ yajet
dhanadaṃ cottare nyasya rudram aiśānagocare
sampūjyaivaṃ vidhānena dikpatreṣu viśeṣataḥ
adhaḥpatre tathā viṣṇum arcayet parameśvaram
pūrvapatre balaṃ pūjya pradyumnaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā
aniruddhaṃ tathā pūjya paścime cottare tathā
pūjayed vāsudevaṃ tu sarvapātakaśāntidam
aiśānyāṃ vinyasecchaṅkham āgneyyāṃ cakram eva ca
saumyāyāṃ tu gadā pūjyā vāyavyāṃ padmam eva ca
nairṛtyāṃ muṣalaṃ pūjyaṃ dakṣiṇe garuḍaṃ tathā
vāmato vinyasel lakṣmīṃ devadevasya buddhimān
dhanuś caiva ca khaḍgaṃ ca devasya purato nyaset
śrīvatsaṃ kaustubhaṃ caiva devasya purato 'rcayet
evaṃ pūjya yathānyāyaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam
diṅmaṇḍale ca vinyasya cāṣṭau kumbhān vidhānataḥ
vaiṣṇavaṃ kalasaṃ caiva navamaṃ tatra kalpayet
snāpayen muktikāmāṃs tu vaiṣṇavena ghaṭena tu
śrīkāmān snāpayet tadvad aindreṇātha ghaṭena tu
jayapratāpakāmāṃs tu āgneyenābhiṣecayet
mṛtyuñjayavidhānena yāmyena snāpanaṃ tathā
duṣṭapradhvaṃsāyālaṃ nairṛtena vidhīyate
śāntaye vāruṇyenātha pāpanāśāya vāyavam
dravyasampattikāmasya kaubereṇa vidhīyate
raudreṇa jñānahetus tu lokapālaghaṭās tv ime
ekaikena naraḥ snātaḥ sarvapāpavarjitaḥ
bhaved avyāhatajñānaḥ śrīmāṃś ca puruṣaḥ sadā
kiṃ punar navabhiḥ snāto naraḥ pātakavarjitaḥ
jāyate viṣṇusadṛśaḥ sadyo rājāthavā punaḥ
athavā dikṣu sarvāsu yathāsaṅkhyena lokapān
pūjayet svasvanāmnā tu ṣaḍbhinnena vidhānataḥ
evaṃ sampūjya devāṃs tu lokapālān prasannadhīḥ
paścāt parīkṣitān śiṣyān baddhanetrān praveśayet
āgneyadhāraṇādagdhān vāyunā vidhūtāṃs tataḥ
somenāpy āyitān paścācchrāvayen niyamān budhaḥ
na ninded abrāhmaṇān devān viṣṇuṃ brāhmaṇam eva ca
rudram ādiyam agniṃ ca lokapālān grahāṃs tathā
vandeta vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi puruṣaṃ pūrvadīkṣitam
evaṃ tu samayān śrāvya paścāddhomaṃ tu kārayet
tattvāni śiṣyadeheṣu vinyasya ca viśodhayet
oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvarūpiṇe huṃ svāhā
ṣoḍaśākṣaramantreṇa homayej jvalitānalaḥ
garbhādhānādikāś caiva kriyāḥ sarvāś ca kārayet
tribhis tribhir āhutibhir devadevasya sannidhau
tato 'panīya dṛgbandhaṃ puraḥ śiṣyaṃ niveśya ca
prāyaḥ pūrvoktavidhinā mantraṃ tasmai gurur diśet
homānte dīkṣitaḥ paścād dāpayed gurudakṣiṇām
hastyaśvaratnakaṭakaṃ hemagrāmādikaṃ nṛpaḥ
dāpayed gurave prājño madhyamo madhyamāṃ tathā
dāpayed itaro yugmaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi
evaṃ kṛte tu yat puṇyaṃ māhātmyaṃ jāyate dhare
tad aśakyaṃ tu gaditum api varṣaśatair api
dīkṣitātmā guror bhūtvā vārāhaṃ śṛṇuyād yadi
tena vedāḥ purāṇāni sarve mantrāḥ susaṅgrahāḥ
japtāḥ syuḥ puṣkare tīrthe prayāge sindhusāgare
devahūte kurukṣetre vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
graheṇa viṣuve caiva yat phalaṃ japatāṃ bhavet
tat phalaṃ dviguṇaṃ tasya dīkṣito yaḥ śṛṇoti ca
devā api tapaḥ kṛtvā dhyāyanti ca vadanti ca
kadā me bhārate varṣe janma syād bhūtadhāriṇi
dīkṣitāś ca bhaviṣyāmo vārāhaṃ śṛṇumaḥ kadā
vārāhaṃ ṣoḍaśātmānaṃ yuktā dehe kadācana
paśyāmaḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ yad gatvā na punar bhavet
evaṃ jalpanti vibudhā manasā cintayanti ca
vārāhayāgaṃ kārttikyāṃ kadā drakṣyāmahe dhare
eṣa te vidhir uddiṣṭo mayā te bhūtadhāriṇi
devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ sarvathā durlabho hy asau
evaṃ yo vetti tattvena yaś ca paśyati maṇḍalam
yaś cemaṃ śṛṇuyād devi sarve muktā iti śrutiḥ
saṃkṣiptaś cātha dīkṣāyā vidhir eṣa vilikhyate
mukhyakalpe hy aśaktasya janasya syāddhitāya ca
sumuhūrte'tha samprāpte sarvatobhadramaṇḍale
nūtanaṃ gandhapuṣpādimaṇḍitaṃ kalasaṃ nyaset
vastrāvṛtaṃ payaḥpūrṇaṃ pañcapallavasaṃyutam
sarvauṣadhipañcaratnamṛtsnāsaptakagarbhitam
mṛttikāś ca saptoktāḥ
aśvasthānād gajasthānād valmīkāc ca catuṣpathāt
rājadvārāc ca goṣṭhāc ca nadyāḥ kūlān mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ
kṛṣṇam abhyarcya taṃ kumbhaṃ kuśakūrcena deśikaḥ
deyamantreṇa sāṣṭaṃ tu sahasram abhimantrayet
tadadbhiḥ pūrvavacchiṣyam abhiṣicya diśen manum
śiṣyo 'rcayed guruṃ bhaktyā yathāśakti dvijān api
athopadeśas tattvasāgare
atrāpy aśaktaḥ kaścic ced abjam abhyarcya sākṣatam
tadambhasābhiṣicyāṣṭa vārān mūlena ke karam
nidhāyāmuṃ japet karṇe upadeśeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ
candrasūryagrahe tīrthe siddhakṣetre śivālaye
mantramātraprakathanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate
tatra tatraiva viśeṣaḥ śrīnāradapañcarātre
vittalobhād vimuktasya svalpavittasya dehinaḥ
saṃsārabhayabhītasya viṣṇubhaktasya tattvataḥ
agnāv ājyānvite bījaiḥ salilaiḥ kevalaiś ca vā
dravyahīnasya kurvīta vacasānugrahaṃ guruḥ
yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhūteṣu virāgo vītamatsaraḥ
jitendriyaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ sarvāṅgāvayavānvitaḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā bhīte cābhayadaḥ sadā
samabuddhipadaṃ prāptas tatrāpi bhagavanmayaḥ
pañcakālaparaś caiva pañcarātrārthavit tathā
viṣṇutattvaṃ parijñāya ekaṃ cānekabhedagam
vīkṣayen medinīṃ sarvāṃ kiṃ punaś copasannatān
skānde brahmanāradasaṃvāde
iha kīrtiṃ vadānyatvaṃ prajāvṛddhiṃ dhanaṃ sukham
vidyādānena labhate sāttviko nātra saṃśayaḥ
yathā surāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ paramaḥ parameśvaraḥ
tathaiva sarvadānānāṃ vidyādānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
yāvac ca pātakaṃ tena kṛtaṃ janmaśatair api
tat sarvaṃ nāśam āpnoti vidyādānena dehinām
vidyādānāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
yena dattena cāpnoti śivaṃ paramakāraṇam
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse daikṣiko nāma dvitīyo vilāsaḥ
vande'nantādbhutaiśvaryaṃ śrīcaitanyaṃ mahāprabhum
nīco 'pi yatprasādāt syāt sadācārapravartakaḥ
puṃso gṛhītadīkṣasya śrīkṛṣṇaṃ pūjayiṣyataḥ
ācāro likhyate kṛtyaṃ śrutismṛtyanusārataḥ
labdhvā mantraṃ tu yo nityaṃ nārcayen mantradevatām
sarvakarmaphalaṃ tasyāniṣṭaṃ yacchati devatā
na kiṃcit kasyacit sidhyet sadācāraṃ vinā yataḥ
tasmād avaśyaṃ sarvatra sadācāro hy apekṣyate
viṣṇupurāṇe
varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān
viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyat tattoṣakāraṇam
mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe śrīmadālasālarkasaṃvāde
gṛhasthena sadā kāryam ācāraparipālanam
na hy ācāravihīnasya sukham atra paratra ca
yajñadānatapāṃsīha puruṣasya na bhūtaye
bhavanti yaḥ sadācāraṃ samullaṅghya pravartate
bhaviṣyottare ca śrīkṛṣṇayudhiṣṭhirasaṃvāde
ācārahīnaṃ na punanti vedāḥ yadyapy adhītāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ
chandāṃsy enaṃ mṛtyukāle tyajanti nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāḥ
kapālasthaṃ yathā toyaṃ śvadṛtau vā yathā payaḥ
duṣṭaṃ syāt sthānadoṣeṇa vṛttahīne tathāśubham
ācārarahito rājan neha nāmutra nindati
lekhyena smaraṇādīnāṃ nityatvenaiva setsyati
smaraṇādyātmakasyāpi sadācārasya nityatā
viṣṇupurāṇe tatraiva gṛhidharmaprasaṅge
sadācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāv ubhāv api
sādhavaḥ kṣīṇadoṣās tu sacchabdaḥ sādhuvācakaḥ
teṣām ācaraṇaṃ yat tu sadācāraḥ sa ucyate
kāśīkhaṇḍe skandāgastyasaṃvāde
anadhyayanaśīlaṃ ca sadācāravilaṅghinam
sālasyaṃ ca durannādaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bādhate'ntakaḥ
tato 'bhyaset prayatnena sadācāraṃ sadā dvijaḥ
tīrthāny apy abhilaṣyanti sadācārasamāgamam
bhaviṣyottare ca tatraiva
ācāraprabhavo dharmaḥ santaś cācāralakṣaṇāḥ
sādhūnāṃ ca yathā vṛttaṃ sa sadācāra iṣyate
tasmāt kuryāt sadācāraṃ ya icched gatim ātmanaḥ
sarvalakṣaṇahīno 'pi samucācāravān nṛpa
śraddadhāno 'nasūyaś ca sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt
kiṃca
ācāra eva dharmasya mūlaṃ rājan kulasya ca
ācārād vicyuto jantur na kulīno na dhārmikaḥ
kiṃca
ācāro bhūtijanana ācāraḥ kīrtivardhanaḥ
ācārād vardhate hy āyur ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam
ācāra eva nṛpapuṅgava sevyamāno dharmārthakāmaphalado bhaviteha puṃsām
tasmāt sadaiva viduṣāvahitena rājan śāstrodito hy anudinaṃ paripālanīyaḥ
brāhme muhūrta utthāya kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kīrtayan
prakṣālya pāṇipādau ca dantadhāvanam ācaret
ācamya vasanaṃ rātres tyaktvānyat paridhāya ca
punar ācamane kuryāl lekhyena vidhināgrataḥ
athecchan paramāṃ śuddhiṃ mūrdhni dhyātvā guroḥ padau
stutvā ca kīrtayan kṛṣṇaṃ smaraṃś caitad udīrayet
jayati jananivāso devakījanmavādo yaduvarapariṣat svair dorbhir asyann adharmam
sthiracaravṛjinaghnaḥ susmita śrīmukhena vrajapuravanitānāṃ vardhayan kāmadevam
smṛte sakalakalyāṇabhājanaṃ yatra jāyate
puruṣas tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim
vidagdhagopālavilāsinīnāṃ sambhogacihnāṅkitasarvagātram
pavitram āmnāyagirām agamyaṃ brahma prapadye navanītacauram
daśamaskandhe
udgāyatīnām aravindalocanaṃ vrajāṅganānāṃ divam aspṛśad dhvaniḥ
dadhnaś ca nirmanthanaśabdamiśrito nirasyate yena diśām amaṅgalam
paṭhet punaś ca sādhūnāṃ sampradāyānusārataḥ
catuḥślokīm imāṃ sarvadoṣaśāntyai śubhāptaye
prātaḥ smarāmi bhavabhītimahārtiśāntyai nārāyaṇaṃ garuḍavāhanam abjanābham
grāhābhibhūtavaravārivāraṇamuktihetuṃ cakrāyudhaṃ taruṇavārijapatranetram
prātar namāmi manasā vacasā ca mūrdhnā pādāravindayugalaṃ paramasya puṃsaḥ
nārāyaṇasya narakārṇavatāraṇasya pārāyaṇapravaṇavipraparāyaṇasya
prātar bhajāmi bhajatām abhayaṅkaraṃ taṃ prāk sarvajanmakṛtapāpabhayāvahatyai
yo grāhavaktrapatitāṅghrigajendraghoraśokapraṇāśam akaroddhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ
ślokatrayam idaṃ puṇyaṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ paṭhet tu yaḥ
lokatrayagurus tasmai dadyād ātmapadaṃ hariḥ
tad etal likhitaṃ kutra kutracid vyavahārataḥ
kintu svābhīṣṭarūpādi śrīkṛṣṇasya vicintayet
itthaṃ vidadhyād bhagavatkīrtanasmaraṇādikam
sarvatīrthābhiṣekaṃ vai bahir antarviśodhanam
tathā ca skānde skandaṃ prati śrīśivoktau
sakṛn nārāyaṇety uktvā pumān kalpaśatatrayam
gaṅgādisarvatīrtheṣu snāto bhavati putraka
anyatra ca
śayanād utthito yas tu kīrtayen madhusūdanam
kīrtanāt tasya pāpasya nāśam āyāty aśeṣataḥ
māhātmyaṃ kīrtanasyāgre lekhyaṃ mukhyaprasaṅgataḥ
smaraṇasya tu māhātmyam adhunā likhyate kiyat
pādme bṛhatsahasranāmni stotre
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit
sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīmadagastyoktau
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃ sa mohaḥ sa ca vibhramaḥ
yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi vāsudevo na cintyate
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīdhruvacarite
iyam eva parā hānir upasargo 'yam eva ca
abhāgyaṃ paramaṃ caitad vāsudevaṃ na yat smaret
ye muhūrtāḥ kṣaṇā ye ca yāḥ kāṣṭhā ye nimeṣakāḥ
ṛte viṣṇusmṛter yātās teṣu muṣṭo yamena saḥ
nityatve'py asya māhātmyaṃ vicitraphaladānataḥ
jñeyaṃ śāstroditaṃ darśapūrṇamāsādivad budhaiḥ
uktaṃ ca smārtair api
māntraṃ pārthivam āgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca
vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ ceti snānaṃ saptavidhaṃ smṛtam
śaṃ na āpas tu vai māntraṃ mṛdālambhaṃ tu pārthivam
bhasmanā snānam āgneyaṃ snānaṃ gorajasānilam
ātape sati yā vṛṣṭir divyaṃ snānaṃ tad ucyate
bahir nadyādiṣu snānaṃ vāruṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ
dhyānaṃ yan manasā viṣṇor mānasaṃ tat prakīrtanam
kiṃca
asāmarthyena kāyasya kāladeśādyapekṣayā
tulyaphalāni sarvāṇi syur ity āha parāśaraḥ
snānānāṃ mānasaṃ snānaṃ manvādyaiḥ paramaṃ smṛtam
kṛtena yena mucyante gṛhasthā api vai dvijāḥ
gāruḍe śrīnāradoktau viṣṇudharme ca pulastyoktau
apavitraḥ pavitro vā sarvāvasthāṃ gato 'pi vā
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ
yadyapy upahataḥ pāpair manasāyantadustaraiḥ
tathāpi saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe
prāyaścittāny aśeṣāṇi tapaḥ karmātmakāni vai
yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param
kṛte pāpe'nutāpo vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate
prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param
kiṃca
kalikalmaṣam atyugraṃ narakārtipradaṃ nṝṇām
prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṃsmṛte
bṛhannāradīye śukrabalisaṃvāde
harir harati pāpāni duṣṭacittair api smṛtaḥ
anicchayāpi saṃspṛṣṭo dahaty eva hi pāvakaḥ
tatraiva prāyaścittaprasaṅgānte
mahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ
sa vai vimucyate sadyo yasya viṣṇuparaṃ manaḥ
brahmavaivarte
karmaṇā manasā vācā yaḥ kṛtaḥ pāpasañcayaḥ
so 'py aśeṣaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti smṛtvā kṛṣṇāṅghripaṅkajam
ata evoktaṃ skānde kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśareṇa
yamamārgaṃ mahāghoraṃ narakāṃś ca yamaṃ tathā
svapne'pi na naraḥ paśyed yaḥ smared garuḍadhvajam
ṣaṣṭhaskandhe śrīśukena
sakṛn manaḥ kṛṣṇapadāravindayor niveśitaṃ tadguṇarāgi yair iha
na te yamaṃ pāśabhṛtaś ca tadbhaṭān svapne 'pi paśyanti hi cīrṇaniṣkṛtāḥ
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe śrīprahlādoktau
dantā gajānāṃ kulśāgraniṣṭhurāḥ śīrṇā yad ete na balaṃ mamaitat
mahāvipatpātavināśano 'yaṃ janārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ
vāmanapurāṇe ca
viṣṭayo vyatipātāś ca ye'nye durnītisambhavāḥ
te sarve smaraṇād viṣṇor nāśam āyānty upadravāḥ
pādme māghamāhātmye devadyutistutau
yasya smaraṇamātreṇa na moho na ca durgatiḥ
na rogo na ca duḥkhāni tam anantaṃ namāmy aham
dvādaśaskandhe
yathā hemni sthito vahnir durvarṇaṃ hanti dhātujam
evam ātmagato viṣṇur yoginām aśubhāśayam
pāṇḍavagītāyām
lābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ
yeṣām indīvaraśyāmo hṛdayasthajanārdanaḥ
sarvasatkarmaphaladatvam skānde kārttikaprasaṅge 'gastyoktau
deveṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caiva dāneṣu tīrtheṣu vrateṣu caiva
iṣṭeṣu pūrteṣu ca yat pradiṣṭaṃ nṝṇāṃ smṛte tatphalam acyute ca
bṛhannāradīye
nyūnātiriktatā siddhā kalau vedoktakarmaṇām
harisaṃsmaraṇam evātra sampūrṇaphaladāyakam
smṛtau ca
pramādāt kurvatāṃ karma pracyavetādhvareṣu yat
smaraṇād eva tad viṣṇoḥ sampūrṇaṃ syād iti śrutiḥ
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge
tulāpuruṣadānānāṃ rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ
phalaṃ viṣṇoḥ smṛtisamaṃ na jātu dvijasattama
dvādaśaskandhe
vidyātapaḥprāṇanirodhamaitrī tīrthābhiṣekavratadānajapyaiḥ
nātyantaśuddhiṃ labhate 'ntarātmā yathā hṛdisthe bhagavaty anante
viṣṇupurāṇe hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati śrīprahlādoktau
bhayaṃ bhayānām apahāriṇi sthite manasy anante mama kutra tiṣṭhati
yasmin smṛte janmajarodbhavāni bhayāni sarvāṇy apayānti tāta
tatraivānyatra
viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇāt kṣīṇasamastakleśasaṃcayaḥ
muktiṃ prayāti svargāptis tasya vighno 'numīyate
bṛhannāradīye
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ purāṇaṃ nijaprabhābhāvitasarvalokam
saṃkalpitārthapradam ādidevaṃ smṛtvā vrajen muktipadaṃ manuṣyaḥ
skānde
yasya smaraṇamātreṇa janmasaṃsārabandhanāt
vimucyate namas tasmai viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge śrīparāśaroktau
tadaiva puruṣo mukto janmaduḥkhajarādibhiḥ
bhaktyā tu parayā nūnaṃ yadaiva smarate harim
bṛhannāradīye
yena kenāpy upāyena smṛto nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ
api pātakayuktasya prasannaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ
vāmanapurāṇe
anādyanantam ajarāmaraṃ hariṃ ye saṃsmaranty aharahar niyataṃ narā bhuvi
tat sarvagaṃ brahma paraṃ purāṇaṃ te yānti vaiṣṇavapadaṃ dhruvam avyayaṃ ca
pādme devadūtavikuṇḍalasaṃvāde yamasya dūtānuśāsane
smaranti ye sakṛd bhūtāḥ prasaṅgenāpi keśavam
te vidhvastākhilāghaughā yanti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam
brahmapurāṇe viṣṇurahasye
śāṭhyenāpi narā nityaṃ ye smaranti janārdanam
te 'pi yānti tanuṃ tyaktvā viṣṇulokam anāmayam
viṣṇudharmottare
nirāśīr nirmamo yas tu viṣṇor dhyānaparo bhavet
tatpadaṃ samavāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati
kāśīkhaṇḍe śrībindumādhavaprasaṅge agnibindustutau
ye tvāṃ trivikrama sadā hṛdi śīlayanti kādambinīrucir arociṣam ambujākṣa
saudāminīvilasitāṃśukavītamūrte te'pi spṛśanti tava kāntim acintyarūpām
śrībhagavadgītāsu
antakāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaram
yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ
daśamaskandhe pṛthukopākhyāne
smarataḥ pādakamalam ātmānam api yacchati
kiṃnv arthakāmān bhajato nātyabhīṣṭān jagadguruḥ
vaiṣṇave
vāsudeve mano yasya japahomārcanādiṣu
tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādi satphalam
gāruḍe
mahatas tapaso mūlaṃ prasavaḥ puṇyasantateḥ
jīvitasya phalaṃ svādu niyataṃ smaraṇaṃ hareḥ
dvitīyaskandhe
etāvān sāṅkhyayogābhyāṃ svadharmapariniṣṭhayā
janmalābhaḥ paraḥ puṃsām ante nārāyaṇasmṛtiḥ
ata eva jarāsandhaniruddhanṛpavargaiḥ prārthitaṃ daśamaskandhe
taṃ naḥ samādiśopāyaṃ yena te caraṇābjayoḥ
smṛtir yathā na viramed api saṃsaratām iha
śrīnāradenāpi
dṛṣṭaṃ tavāṅghriyugalaṃ janatāpavargaṃ brahmādibhir hṛdi vicintyam agādhabodhaiḥ
saṃsārakūpapatitottaraṇāvalambaṃ dhyāyaṃś carāmy anugṛhāṇa yathā smṛtiḥ syāt
kṛṣṇasmaraṇamāhātmyamahābdhir dustaro dhiyā
yo yiyāsati tatpāraṃ sa hi caitanyavañcitaḥ
tataḥ pādodakaṃ kiṃcit prāk pītvā tulasīdalaiḥ
gṛhītenācaret tena svamūrdhany abhiṣecanam
athādau śrīguruṃ natvā śrīkṛṣṇasya padābjayoḥ
kiṃcid vijñāpayan sarvasvakṛtyāny arpayen namet
vāmanapurāṇe
sarvamaṅgalamaṅgalyaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ śivam
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
viṣṇudharmottare
yadutsavādikaṃ karma tat tvayā prerito hare
kariṣyāmi tvayā jñeyam iti vijñāpanaṃ mama
prātaḥ prabodhito viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśena yat tvayā
yad yat kārayasīśāna tat karomi tavājñayā
trailokyacaitanyamayādideva śrīnātha viṣṇo bhavadājñayaiva
prātaḥ samutthāya tava priyārthaṃ saṃsārayātrām anuvartayiṣye
saṃsārayātrām anuvartamānaṃ tvadājñayā śrīnṛhare'ntarātman
spardhātiraskārakalipramādabhayāni mā mābhibhavantu bhūman
jānāmi dharmaṃ na ca me pravṛttir jānāmy adharmaṃ na ca me nivṛttiḥ
tvayā hṛṣīkeśa hṛdi sthitena yathā niyukto 'smi tathā karomi
mahābhārate
namo brahmaṇyadevāya gobrāhmaṇahitāya ca
jagaddhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ
garuḍapurāṇe
asuravibudhasiddhair jñāyate yasya nāntaḥ sakalamunibhir antaś cintyate yo viśuddhaḥ
nikhilahṛdi niviṣṭo vetti yaḥ sarvasākṣī tam ajam amṛtam īśaṃ vāsudevaṃ nato 'smi
viṣṇupurāṇe
yajñibhir yajñapuruṣo vāsudevaś ca sātvataḥ
vedāntavedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato 'smi tam
evaṃ vijñāpayan dhyāyan kīrtayaṃś ca yathāvidhi
praṇāmānācarecchaktyā catuḥsaṅkhyāvarān budhaḥ
śrīgopīcandanenordhvapuṇḍraṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi
āsīta prāṅmukho bhūtvā śuddhasthāne śubhāsane
tathā ca nāradīyapañcarātre
nirgatyācamya vidhivat praviśya ca punaḥ sudhīḥ
āsane prāṅmukho bhūtvā vihite copaviśya vai
sampradāyānusāreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca
prāṇāyāmāṃś ca vidhivat kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyet yathoditam
tathā coktam
upapātakeṣu sarveṣu pātakeṣu mahatsu ca
praviśya rajanīpādaṃ viṣṇudhyānaṃ samācaret
vaihāyasapañcarātre ca
tathaiva rātriśeṣaṃ tu kālaṃ sūryodayāvadhi
kartavyaṃ sajapaṃ dhyānaṃ nityam ārādhakena vai
vibhajya pañcadhā rātriṃ śeṣe devārcanādikam
japaṃ homaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ nityaṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ
ata eva viṣṇusmṛtau
rātres tu paścime yāme muhūrto brāhmya ucyate
pādodapānādīnāṃ ca sa vidhir mahimāgrataḥ
lekhyo 'dhunā tu dhyānasya sa saṅkṣepeṇa likhyate
tāpanīyaśrutiṣu
satpuṇḍarīkanayanaṃ meghābhaṃ vaidyutāmbaram
dvibhujaṃ jñānamudrāḍhyaṃ vanamālinam īśvaram
gopagopīgavāvītaṃ suradrumatalāśritam
dviyālaṃkaraṇopetaṃ ratnapaṅkajamadhyagam
kālindījalakallolasaṅgimārutasevitam
cintayaṃś cetasā kṛṣṇaṃ mukto bhavati saṃsṛteḥ
mṛtyuñjayasaṃhitānusāroditasāradātilake ca
smared vṛndāvane ramye mohayantam anāratam
govindaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ gopakanyāḥ sahasraśaḥ
ātmano vadanāmbhojapreritākṣimadhuvratāḥ
kāmabāṇena vivaśāś ciram āśleṣeṇotsukāḥ
muktāhāralasatpīnottuṅgastanabharānatāḥ
srastadhammillavasanā madaskhalitabhāṣaṇāḥ
dantapaṅktiprabhodbhāsispandamānādharāñcitāḥ
vilobhayantīr vividhair vibhramair bhāvagarbhitaiḥ
phullendīvarakāntim induvadanaṃ barhāvataṃsapriyaṃ śrīvatsāṅkam udārakaustubhadharaṃ pītāmbaraṃ sundaram
gopīnāṃ nayanotpalārcitatanuṃ gogopasaṅghāvṛtaṃ govindaṃ kalaveṇuvādanaparaṃ divyāṅgabhūṣaṃ bhaje
śrīgautamīyatantrādau taddhyānaṃ prathitaṃ param
agrato 'trāpi saṃlekhyaṃ yad iṣṭaṃ tatra tad bhajet
bṛhatśātātāpasmṛtau
pakṣopavāsād yat pāpaṃ puruṣasya praṇaśyati
prāṇāyāmaśatenaiva yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām
prāṇāyāmasahasreṇa yat pāpaṃ naśyate nṝṇām
kṣaṇamātreṇa tat pāpaṃ harer dhyānāt praṇaśyati
viṣṇudharme
sarvapāpaprasakto 'pi dhyāyan nimiṣam acyutam
bhūtas tapasvī bhavati paṅktipāvanapāvanaḥ
viṣṇupurāṇe ca
dhyāyen nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānādiṣu ca karmasu
prāyaścittaṃ hi sarvasya duṣkṛtasyeti niścitam
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge
samastajagadādhāraṃ paramārthasvarūpiṇam
ghore kaliyuge prāpte viṣṇuṃ dhyāyan na sīdati
skānde kārttikamāhātmye agastyoktau
kintv asya bahubhis tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir vrataiḥ
yo nityaṃ dhyāyate devaṃ nārāyaṇam ananyadhīḥ
bṛhannāradīye kaliprasaṅge
ye mānavā vigatarāgaparāvarajñā nārāyaṇaṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ smaranti
dhyānena tena hata kilbiṣacetanās te mātuḥ payodhararasaṃ na punaḥ pibanti
skānde śrībrahmoktau
muhūrtam api yo dhyāyen nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ
so 'pi sadgatim āpnoti kiṃ punas tatparāyaṇaḥ
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye yamabrāhmaṇasaṃvāde
dhyāyanti puruṣaṃ divyam acyutaṃ ye smaranti ca
labhante te'cyutasthānaṃ śrutir eṣā purātanī
ekādaśaskandhe
vaireṇa yaṃ nṛpatayaḥ śiśupālapauṇḍraśālvādayo gativilāsavilokanādyaiḥ
dhyāyanta ākṛtadhiyaḥ śayanāsanādau tatsāmyam āpur anuraktadhiyāṃ punaḥ kim
caturthaskandhe śrīpṛthūktau
bhajanty atha tvām ata eva sādhavo vyudastamāyāguṇavibhramodayam
bhavatpadānusmaraṇād ṛte satāṃ nimittam anyad bhagavan na vidmahe
skandapurāṇe brahmoktau ca
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ
idam eva suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā
ata evoktaṃ hayaśīrṣapañcarātre nārāyaṇavyūhastave
ye tyaktalokadharmārthā viṣṇubhaktivaśaṃ gatāḥ
dhyāyanti paramātmānaṃ tebhyo 'pīha namo namaḥ
smaraṇe yat tan māhātmyaṃ taddhyāne'py akhilaṃ viduḥ
bhedaḥ kalpyeta sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ tayoḥ kiyān
tato devālaye gatvā ghaṇṭādyudghoṣapūrvakam
prabodhya stutibhiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ nīrājyaṃ prārthayed idam
tṛtīyaskandhe
so 'sāv adabhrakaruṇo bhagavān vivṛddhapremasmitena nayanāmburuhaṃ vijṛmbhan
utthāya viśvavijayāya ca no viṣādaṃ mādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ
devaprapannārtihara prasādaṃ kuru keśava
avalokanadānena bhūyo māṃ pārayācyuta
devālayaṃ praviśyātha stotrāṇīṣṭāni kīrtayan
kṛṣṇasya tulasīvarjaṃ nirmālyam apasārayet
atrismṛtau
prātaḥkāle sadā kuryān nirmālyottāraṇaṃ budhaḥ
tṛṣitāḥ paśavo baddhāḥ kanyakā ca rajasvalā
devatā ca sanirmālyā hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam
nārasiṃhe śrīyamoktau
devamālyāpanayanaṃ devāgāre samūhanam
snāpanaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopradānasamaṃ smṛtam
nāradapañcarātre
yaḥ prātar utthāya vidhāya nityaṃ nirmālyam īśasya nirākaroti
na tasya duḥkhaṃ na daridratā ca nākālamṛtyur na ca rogamātram
aruṇodayavelāyāṃ nirmālyaṃ śalyatāṃ vrajet
prātas tu syān mahāśalyaṃ ghaṭikāmātrayogataḥ
atiśalyaṃ vijānīyāt tato vajraprahāravat
aruṇodayavelāyāṃ śalyaṃ tat kṣamate hariḥ
ghaṭikāyām atikrāntau kṣudraṃ pātakam āvahet
muhūrte samatikrānte pūrṇaṃ pātakam ucyate
atipātakam eva syāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye
muhūrtatritaye pūrṇe mahāpātakam ucyate
tataḥ paraṃ brahmavadho mahāpātakapañcakam
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte prāyaścittaṃ tato na hi
nirmālyasya vilambe tu prāyaścittam athocyate
atikrānte muhūrtārdhe sahasraṃ japam ācaret
pūrṇe muhūrte saṃjāte sahasraṃ sārdham ucyate
sahasradvitīyaṃ kuryāt ghaṭikānāṃ catuṣṭaye
muhūrtatritaye'tīte ayutaṃ japam ācaret
prahare pūrṇatāṃ yāte puraścaraṇam ucyate
prahare samatikrānte prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate
śrīhastāṅghrimukhāmbhojakṣālanāya ca tadgṛhe
gaṇḍūṣāṇi jalair dattvā dantakāṣṭhaṃ samarpayet
jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā pāduke śuddhamṛttikām
salilaṃ ca punar dadyād vāso 'pi mukhamārjanam
tataḥ śrītulasīṃ puṇyām arpayet bhagavatpriyām
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca tanmukhyaprasaṅge lekhyam agrataḥ
viṣṇudharmottare
dantakāṣṭhapradānena dantasaubhāgyam ṛcchati
jihvollekhanikāṃ dattvā virogas tv abhijāyate
pādukāyāḥ pradānena gatim iṣṭām avāpnuyāt
mṛdbhāgadānād devasya bhūmim āpnoty anuttamām
paṭhitvātha priyān ślokān mahāvāditranisvanaiḥ
prabhor nīrājanaṃ kuryān maṅgalākhyaṃ jagaddhitam
nīrājanaṃ tv idaṃ sarvaiḥ kartavyaṃ śucivigrahaiḥ
paramaśraddhayotthāya draṣṭavyaṃ ca sadā naraiḥ
strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca sarveṣām etat sarveṣṭapūrakam
samastadainyadāridryaduritādyupaśāntikṛt
tato 'ruṇodayasyānte snānārthaṃ niḥsared bahiḥ
kīrtayan kṛṣṇanāmāni tīrthaṃ gacched anantaram
tathā ca śukrasmṛtau
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ
svastikādyāsanaṃ baddhvā dhyātvā kṛṣṇapādāmbujam
tato nirgatya nilayānnāmānīmāni kīrtayet
śrīvāsudevāniruddhapradyumnādhokṣajācyuta
śrīkṛṣṇānanta govinda saṅkarṣaṇa namo 'stu te
gatvā tīrthādikaṃ tatra nikṣipya snānasādhanam
vidhinācarya maitryādikṛtyaṃ śaucaṃ vidhāya ca
ācamya khāni saṃmārjya snānaṃ kuryāt yathocitam
śrīviṣṇupurāṇe aurvasagarasaṃvāde gṛhidharmakathane
tataḥ kalye samutthāya kuryān mūtraṃ nareśvara
nairṛtyām iṣuvikṣepam atītyādhikaṃ gṛhāt
dūrādāvasathān mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca samutsṛjet
pādāv asecanocchiṣṭe prakṣipen na gṛhāṅgaṇe
ātmacchāyāṃ taroś chāyāṃ gosūryāgnyanilāṃs tathā
guruṃ dvijādīṃś ca budho na meheta kadācana
na kṛṣṭe śasyamadhye vā govraje janasaṃsadi
na vartmani na nadyāditīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha
nāpsu naivāmbhasas tīre na śmaśāne samācaret
utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam
udaṅmukho divotsargaṃ viparītamukho niśi
kurvītānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva
tṛṇair ācchādya vasudhāṃ vastraprāvṛtamastakaḥ
tiṣṭhen nāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiṃcid udīrayet
tathā kaurme vyāsagītāyām
nidhāya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahmasūtram udaṅmukhaḥ
antardhāpya mahīṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ patrair loṣṭrais tṛṇena vā
prāvṛtya tu śiraḥ kuryād viṇmūtrasya visarjanam
na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayor gavām
na devadevālayor nāpām api kadācana
nadīṃ jyotīṃṣi vīkṣitvā na vāyvagnimukho 'pi vā
pratyādityaṃ pratyanalaṃ pratisomaṃ tathaiva ca
kāśīkāṇḍe śrīskandāgastyasaṃvāde
tataś cāvaśyakaṃ kartuṃ nairṛtīṃ diśam āśrayet
grāmād dhanuḥśataṃ gacchen nagarāc ca caturguṇam
karṇopavītyudagvaktro divase sandhyayor api
viṇmūtre visṛjen maunī niśāyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
nālokayed diśo bhāgān jyotiś cakraṃ nabho 'malam
vāmena pāṇinā śiśnaṃ dhṛtvottiṣṭhet prayatnavān
tatraivāgre
na mūtraṃ govraje kuryān na valmīke na bhasmani
na garteṣu sasattveṣu na tiṣṭhan na vrajann api
yathāsukhamukho rātrau divā chāyāndhakārayoḥ
bhītiṣu prāṇabādhāyāṃ kuryān malavisarjanam
viṣṇupurāṇe tatraiva
valmīkamūṣikotkhātāṃ mṛdaṃ nāntarjalāt tathā
śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca na dadyāl lepasambhavām
antaḥprāṇyavapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ ca pārthiva
parityajen mṛdaś caitāḥ sakalāḥ śaucasādhane
ekā liṅge gude tisro daśa vāmakare nṛpa
hastadvaye saptānyā mṛdaḥ śaucopapādikāḥ
yamasmṛtau
tisras tu pādayor deyāḥ śuddhikāmena nityaśaḥ
kiṃca
tisras tu mṛttikā deyāḥ kṛtvā tu nakhaśodhanam
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tatraiva
guhye dadyān mṛdaṃ caikāṃ pāyau pañcāmbusāntarāḥ
daśa vāmakare cāpi sapta pāṇidvaye mṛdaḥ
ekaikāṃ pādayor dadyāt tisraḥ pāṇyor mṛdaḥ smṛtāḥ
itthaṃ śaucaṃ gṛhī kuryād gandhalepakṣayāvadhi
kramād dviguṇam etat tu brahmacaryādiṣu triṣu
divā vihitaśaucāc ca rātrāv ardhaṃ samācaret
rujārdhaṃ ca tadardhaṃ ca pathi caurādipīḍite
tadardhayoṣitāṃ cāpi svāsthye nyūnaṃ na kārayet
ārdradhātrīphalonmānā mṛdaḥ śauce prakīrtitāḥ
śaṅkhasmṛtau
mṛttikā tu samuddiṣṭā triparvī pūryate yayā
dakṣasmṛtau
ardhaprasṛtimātrā tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā
dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tadardhaṃ parikīrtitā
dakṣaḥ
ekā liṅge tu savye trir ubhayor mṛddvayaṃ smṛtam
brāhme
pādayor dve gṛhītvā ca suprakṣālitapāṇinā
ācamya tu tataḥ śuddhaḥ smṛtvā viṣṇuṃ sanātanam
viṣṇupurāṇe tatraiva
acchenāgandhaphenena jalenābudbudena ca
ācāmeta mṛdaṃ bhūyas tathā dadyāt samāhitaḥ
niṣpāditāṅghriśaucas tu pāpāv abhyukṣya vai punaḥ
triḥ pibet salilaṃ tena tathā dviḥ parimārjayet
śīrṣaṇyāni tataḥ khāni mūrdhānaṃ ca mṛdā labhet
bāhū nābhiṃ ca toyena hṛdayaṃ cāpi saṃspṛśet
atra ca viśeṣo dakṣeṇoktaḥ
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca triḥ pibed ambu vīkṣitam
saṃvṛttāṅguṣṭhamūlena dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham
saṃhatya tisṛbhiḥ pūrvam āsyam evam upaspṛśet
aṅguṣṭhena pradeśinyā ghrāṇaṃ paścād anantaram
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu cakṣuḥśrotre punaḥ punaḥ
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayor nābhiṃ hṛdayaṃ tu talena vai
sarvābhis tu śiraḥ paścād bāhū cāgreṇa saṃspṛśet
tathā kāśīkhaṇḍe tatraiva
prāgāsya udagāsyo vā sūpaviṣṭaḥ śucau bhuvi
upaspṛśed vihīnāyāṃ tuṣāṅgārāsthibhasmabhiḥ
anuṣṇābhir aphenābhir adbhir hṛdgābhir atvaraḥ
brāhmaṇo brahmatīrthena dṛṣṭipūtanābhir ācamet
kaṇṭhagābhir nṛpaḥ śudhyet tālugābhis tathorujaḥ
strīśūdrāvāsyasaṃsparśamātreṇāpi viśudhyataḥ
yājñavalkyasmṛtau
pādakṣālanaśeṣeṇa nācāmet vāriṇā dvijaḥ
yady ācamet srāvayitvā bhūmau baudhāyano 'bravīt
bharadvājasmṛtau
pāṇinā dakṣiṇenaiva saṃhatāṅgulinācamet
muktāṅguṣṭhakaniṣṭhena nakaspṛṣṭā apas tyajet
kaurme ca vyāsagītāyām
bhuktvā pītvā ca suptvā ca snātvā rathyopasarpaṇe
auṣṭhau vilomakau spṛṣṭvā vāso viparidhāya ca
retomūtrapurīṣāṇām utsarge'nṛtabhāṣaṇe
ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanārambhe kāśaśvāsāgame tathā
catvaraṃ vā śmaśānaṃ vā samabhyasya dvijottamaḥ
sandhyor ubhayos tadvad ācānto 'py ācamet punaḥ
kiṃca
śiraḥ prāvṛtya kaṇṭhaṃ vā muktakacchaśikho 'pi vā
akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucam ācānto 'py aśucir bhavet
sopānatkau jalastho vā noṣṇīṣī cācamed budhaḥ
na caiva varṣadhārābhir hastocchiṣṭe tathā budhaḥ
naikahastārpiuttajalair vinā sūtreṇa vā punaḥ
na pādukāsanastho vā bahir jānur athāpi vā
triḥpāne keśavaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ mādhavam apy atha
prakṣālane dvayoḥ pāṇyor govindaṃ viṣṇum apy ubhau
madhusūdanam ekaṃ ca mārjane'nyaṃ trivikramam
unmārjane'py adharayor vāmanaśrīdharāv ubhau
prakṣālane punaḥ pāṇyor hṛṣīkeśaṃ ca pādayoḥ
padmanābhaṃ prokṣaṇe tu mūrdhno dāmodaraṃ tataḥ
vāsudevaṃ mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ pradyumnam ity ubhau
nāsayor netrayugale'niruddhaṃ puruṣottamam
adhokṣajaṃ nṛsiṃhaṃ ca karṇayor nābhito 'cyutam
janārdanaṃ ca hṛdaye upendraṃ mastake tataḥ
dakṣiṇe tu hariṃ bāhau vāme kṛṣṇaṃ yathāvidhi
namo 'nantaṃ ca caturthyantam ācāmet kramato japan
aśaktaḥ kevalam dakṣaṃ spṛśet karṇaṃ tathā ca vāk
kurvītālabhanaṃ vāpi dakṣiṇaśravaṇasya vai
tatra kātyāyanaḥ
utthāya netraṃ prakṣālya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ
parijapya ca mantreṇa bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam
mantraś cāyam
āyur balaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajā paśuvasūni ca
brahma prajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tvaṃ no dhehi vanaspate
kāśīkhaṇḍe
atho mukhaviśuddhyarthaṃ gṛhṇīyād dantadhāvanam
ācānto 'py aśucir yasmād akṛtvā dantadhāvanam
vārāhe ca
dantakāṣṭham akhāditvā yas tu mām upasarpati
sarvakālakṛtaṃ karma tena caikena naśyati
manuḥ
caturdaśyaṣṭamīdarśapaurṇamāsyarkasaṅkramaḥ
eṣu strītailamāṃsāni dantakāṣṭhāni varjayet
saṃvartakaḥ
ādye tithau navamyāṃ ca kṣaye candramasas tathā
ādityavāre śaure ca varjayed dantadhāvanam
kātyāyanaḥ
pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo dahaty ā saptamaṃ kulam
vṛddhavaśiṣṭhaḥ
upavāse tathā śrāddhena khāded dantadhāvanam
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti saptakulāni vai
anyatra ca
pratipaddaraṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyekādaśīravau
dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam
dineṣv eteṣu kāṣṭhair hi dantānāṃ dhāvanasya tu
niṣiddhatvāt tṛṇaiḥ kuryāt tathā kāṣṭhetaraiś ca tat
tathā ca vyāsaḥ
pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ dantadhāvanam
parṇair anyatra kāṣṭhaiś ca jīvollekhaḥ sadaiva hi
paiṭhīnasiḥ
alābhe ca niṣedhe vā kāṣṭhānāṃ dantadhāvanam
parṇādinā viśuddhena jihvollekhaḥ sadaiva hi
kāṣṭhaiḥ pratipadādau yan niṣiddhaṃ dantadhāvanam
tṛṇaparṇais tu tat kuryād amām ekādaśīṃ vinā
ata eva vyāsasya vacanāntaram
alābhe dantakāṣṭhānāṃ niṣiddhāyāṃ tathā tithau
apāṃ dvādaśagaṇḍūṣair vidadhyād dantadhāvanam
kāśīkhaṇḍe tatraiva
mukhe paryuṣite yasmād bhaved aśucibhāg naraḥ
tataḥ kuryāt prayatnena śuddhyarthaṃ dantadhāvanam
upavāse'pi no duṣyed dantadhāvanam añjanam
gandhālaṅkārasadvastrapuṣpamālānulepanam
smṛtau
sarvakaṇṭakinaḥ puṇyāḥ āyurdāḥ kṣīriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ
kaṭutiktakaṣāyāś ca balārogyasukhapradāḥ
kiṃca
palāśānāṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ pāduke caiva varjayet
varjayec ca prayatnena vaṭaṃ vāśvattham eva ca
kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
madhyāṅgulisamasthaulyaṃ dvādaśāṅgulasaṃmitam
satvacaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ yat tadagre na tu dhārayet
kṣīrivṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mālatīsambhavaṃ śubham
apāmārgaṃ ca bilvaṃ vā karavīraṃ viśeṣataḥ
varjayitvā ninitāni gṛhītvaikaṃ yathoditam
parihṛtya dinaṃ pāpaṃ bhakṣayed vai vidhānavit
na pāṭayet dantakāṣṭhaṃ nāṅgulyagreṇa dhārayet
prakṣālya bhuktvā taj jahyāt śucau deśe samāhitaḥ
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tatraiva
kaniṣṭhāgraparīṇāhaṃ satvacaṃ nirvraṇaṃ ṛjum
dvādaśāṅgulamānaṃ ca sārdraṃ syād dantadhāvanam
jihvollekhanikām vāpi kuryāc cāpākṛtiṃ śubhām
rāmārcanacandrikāyām ca
dantollekho vitastyā bhavati parimitād annam ity ādimantrāt prātaḥ kṣīryādikāṣṭhād vaṭakhadirapalāśair vinārkāmrabilvaiḥ
bhuktvā gaṇḍūṣaṣaṭkaṃ dvir api kuśam ṛte deśinīm aṅgulībhir nandābhūtāṣṭaparvaṇy api na khalu navamyarkasaṅkrāntipāte
tataś cācamya vidhivat kṛtvā keśaprasādhanam
smṛtvā praṇavagāyatryau nibadhnīyācchikhāṃ dvijaḥ
tathā coktaṃ
na dakṣiṇāmukho nordhvaṃ kuryāt keśaprasādhanam
smṛtvoṅkāraṃ ca gāyatrīṃ nibadhnīyācchikhāntataḥ
viṣṇupurāṇe tatraiva
nadīnadataḍāgeṣu devakhātajaleṣu ca
nityakriyārthaṃ snāyīta giriprasravaṇeṣu ca
kūpeṣūddhṛtatoyena snānaṃ kurvīta vā bhuvi
snāyītoddhṛtatoyena athavā bhuvy asambhave
tatra kātyāyanaḥ
yathāhani tathā prātar nityaṃ snāyād anāturaḥ
atyantamalinaḥ kāyo navacchidrasamanvitaḥ
sravat eva divārātrau prātaḥsnānaṃ viśodhanam
dakṣaḥ
prātar madhyāhnayoḥ snānaṃ vānaprasthagṛhasthayoḥ
yates trisavanaṃ snānaṃ sakṛt tu brahmacāriṇaḥ
sarve cāpi sakṛt kuryur aśaktau codakaṃ vinā
kiṃca
aśiraskaṃ bhavet snānam aśaktau karmiṇāṃ sadā
ārdreṇa vāsasā vāpi pāṇinā vāpi mārjanam
śaṅkhaś ca
asnātas tu pumān nārho japādihavanādiṣu
kaurme vyāsagītāyām
prātaḥsnānaṃ vinā puṃsāṃ pāpitvaṃ karmasu smṛtam
home jape viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānaṃ samācaret
kāśīkhaṇḍe
prasvedalālasādyāklinno nidrādhīno yato naraḥ
prātaḥsnānāt tato 'rhaḥ syān mantrastotrajapādiṣu
pādme ca devahūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
snānaṃ vinā tu yo bhuṅkte malāśī sa sadā naraḥ
asnāyino 'śuces tasya vimukhāḥ pitṛdevatāḥ
snānahīno naraḥ pāpaḥ snānahīno naro 'śuciḥ
asnāyī narakaṃ bhuṅkte puṃskīṭādiṣu jāyate
mahābhārate udyogaparvaṇi śrīviduroktau
guṇā daśa snānaśīlaṃ bhajante balaṃ rūpaṃ svaravarṇapraśuddhiḥ
sparśaś ca gandhaś ca viśuddhatā ca śrīḥ saukumāryaṃ pravarāś ca nāryaḥ
pādme ca tatraiva
yāmyaṃ hi yātanāduḥkhaṃ nityasnāyī na paśyati
nityasnānena pūyante api pāpakṛto narāḥ
prātaḥsnānaṃ hared vaiśya bāhyābhyantarajaṃ malam
prātaḥsnānena niṣpāpo naro na nirayaṃ vrajet
ye punaḥ srotasi snānam ācarantīha parvaṇi
tenaiva narakaṃ yānti na jāyante kuyoniṣu
duḥsvapnā duṣṭacintāś ca bandhyā bhavanti sarvadā
prātaḥsnānena śuddhānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viśāṃ vara
atrismṛtau
snāne manaḥprasādaḥ syād devā abhimukhāḥ sadā
