saubhāgyaṃ śrīḥ sukhaṃ puṣṭiḥ puṇyaṃ vidyā yaśo dhṛtiḥ
mahāpāpāny alakṣmīṃ ca duritaṃ durvicintitam
śokaduḥkhādi harate prātaḥsnānaṃ viśeṣataḥ
kaurme tatraiva
prātaḥsnānaṃ praśaṃsanti dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakaraṃ hi tat
prātaḥsnānena pāpāni pūyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca
prātaḥsnānāt yataḥ śudhyet kāyo 'yaṃ malinaḥ sadā
chidrito navabhiś chidraiḥ sravaty eva divāniśam
utsāhamedhāsaubhāgyarūpasampatpravartakam
manaḥprasannatāhetuḥ prātaḥsnānaṃ praśasyate
prātaḥ prātas tu yat snānaṃ saṃjāte cāruṇodaye
prājāpatyasamaṃ prāhus tan mahāghavighātakṛt
prātaḥsnānaṃ haret pāpam alakṣmīṃ glānim eva ca
aśucitvaṃ ca duḥsvapnaṃ tuṣṭiṃ puṣṭiṃ prayacchati
nopasarpanti vai duṣṭāḥ prātaḥsnāyijanaṃ kvacit
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalaṃ tasmāt prātaḥsnānaṃ samācaret
snānamātraṃ tathā prātaḥsnānaṃ cātra niyojitam
yadyapy anyo 'nyamilite pṛthag jñeye tathāpy amū
atha tīrthagatas tatra dhautavastraṃ kuśāṃs tathā
mṛttikāṃ ca taṭe nyasya snāyāt svasvavidhānataḥ
adhautena tu vastreṇa nityanaimittikīṃ kriyām
kurvan na phalam āpnoti kṛtā cen niṣphalā bhavet
dhautāṅghripāṇir ācāntaḥ kṛtvā saṅkalpam ādarāt
gaṅgādismaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tīrthāyārghyaṃ samarpayet
sāgarasvananirghoṣadaṇḍahastāsurāntaka
jagatsraṣṭar jaganmardin namāmi tvāṃ sureśvara
imaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya tīrthasnānaṃ samācaret
anyathā tatphalasyārdhaṃ tīrtheśo harati svayam
natvātha tīrthaṃ snānārtham anujñāṃ prārthayed imām
devadeva jagannātha śaṅkhacakragadādhara
dehi viṣṇo mamānujñāṃ tava tīrthaniṣevaṇe
vidhivan mṛdam ādāya tīrthatoye praviśya ca
pravāhābhimukho nadyāṃ syād anyatrārkasammukhaḥ
digbandhaṃ vidhinācarya tīrthāni parikalpya ca
āvāhayed bhagavatīṃ gaṅgām ādityamaṇḍalāt
darbhapāṇiḥ kṛtaprāṇāyāmaḥ kṛṣṇapadāmbujam
dhyātvā tannāma saṃkīrtya nimajjet puṇyavāriṇi
ācamya mūlamantraṃ ca saprāṇāyāmakaṃ japan
kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyan jale bhūyo nimajjya snānam ācaret
kṛtvāghamarṣaṇāntaṃ ca nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ
tatra dvādaśadhā toye nimajjya snānam ācaret
śrīnāradapañcarātre
prasiddheṣu ca tīrtheṣu yady anyasyābhidhāṃ smaret
snātakaṃ taṃ tu tat tīrtham abhiśapya kṣaṇād vrajet
pādme vaiśākhyamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
evam uccārya tattīrthe pādau prakṣālya vāgyataḥ
smaran nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānaṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ
tīrthaṃ prakalpayed dhīmān mūlamantram imaṃ paṭhan
auṃ namo nārāyaṇāya mūlamantra udāhṛtaḥ
darbhapāṇis tu vidhivad ācāntaḥ praṇato bhuvi
caturhastasamāyuktaṃ caturasraṃ samantataḥ
prakalpyāvāhayed gaṅgāṃ mantreṇānena mānavaḥ
viṣṇupādaprasūtāsi vaiṣṇavī viṣṇudevatā
trāhi nas tvenasas tasmād ā janmamaraṇāntikāt
saptavārābhijaptena karasampuṭayojite
mūrdhni kṛtvā jalaṃ bhūpaś catur vā pañca sapta vā
snānaṃ kṛtvā mṛdā tadvad āmantrya tu vidhānataḥ
aśvakrānte rathakrānte viṣṇukrānte vasundhare
mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam
uddhṛtāsi varāheṇa viṣṇunā śatabāhunā
namas te sarvalokānāṃ prabhavāraṇi suvrate
guroḥ saṃnihitasyātha pitroś ca caraṇodakaiḥ
viprāṇāṃ ca padāmbhodhiḥ kuryān mūrdhany abhiṣecanam
tathā ca pādme
guroḥ pādodakaṃ putra tīrthakoṭiphalapradam
kiṃca
viprapādodakaklinnaṃ yasya tiṣṭhati vai śiraḥ
tasya bhāgīrathīsnānam ahany ahani jāyate
tathā gautamīyatantre
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni tāni tīrthāni sāgare
sasāgarāṇi tīrthāni pāde viprasya dakṣiṇe
śaṅkhe vasanti sarvāṇi tīrthāni ca viśeṣataḥ
śaṅkhena mūlamantreṇābhiṣekaṃ punar ācaret
tathaiva tulasīmiśraśālagrāmaśilāmbhasā
abhiṣekaṃ vidadhyāc ca pītvā tat kiṃcid agrataḥ
tad uktaṃ gautamīyatantre
śālagrāmaśilātoyaṃ tulasīgandhamiśritam
kṛtvā śaṅkhe bhrāmayaṃs triḥ prakṣipen nijamūrdhani
śālagrāmaśilātoyam apītvā yas tu mastake
prakṣepaṇaṃ prakurvīta brahmahā sa nigadyate
viṣṇupādodakān pūrvaṃ viprapādodakaṃ pibet
viruddham ācaran mohād brahmahā sa nigadyate
akālamṛtyuharaṇaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam
viṣṇoḥ pādodakaṃ pītvā śirasā dhārayāmy aham
lekhyo 'grye kṛṣṇapādābjatīrthadhāraṇapānayoḥ
mahimātra tu tattīrthenābhiṣekasya likhyate
padmapurāṇe
sa snātaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ
śālagrāmaśilātoyair yo 'bhiṣekaṃ samācaret
gaṅgā godāvarī revā nadyo muktipradās tu yāḥ
nivasanti satīrthās tāḥ śālagrāmaśilājale
koṭitīrthasahasrais tu sevitaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam
tīrthaṃ yadi bhavet puṇyaṃ śālagrāmaśilodbhavam
tatraiva śrīgautamāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
yeṣāṃ dhautāni gātrāṇi hareḥ pādodakena vai
ambarīṣa kule teṣāṃ dāso 'smi vaśagaḥ sadā
rājante tāni tāvac ca tīrthāni bhuvanatraye
yāvan na prāpyate toyaṃ śālagrāmābhiṣekajam
skānde kārttikamāhātmye
gṛhe'pi vasatas tasya gaṅgāsnānaṃ dine dine
śālagrāmaśilātoyair yo 'bhiṣiñcati mānavaḥ
tatraivānyatra ca
yāni kāni ca tīrthāni brahmādyā devatās tathā
viṣṇupādodakasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
śālagrāmodbhavo devo devo dvāravatībhavaḥ
ubhayoḥ snānatoyena brahmahatyā nivartate
kiṃca
sa vai cāvabhṛtasnātaḥ sa ca gaṅgājalāplutaḥ
viṣṇupādodakaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkheyaḥ snāti mānavaḥ
śrīnṛsiṃhapurāṇe
gaṅgāprayāgagayanaimiṣapuṣkarāṇi puṇyāni yāni kurujāṅgalayāmunāni
kālena tīrthasalilāni punanti pāpaṃ pādodakaṃ bhagavataḥ prapunāti sadyaḥ
smṛtau ca
trirātriphaladā nadyo yāḥ kāścid asamudragāḥ
samudragāś ca pakṣasya māsasya saritāṃ patiḥ
ṣaṇmāsaphaladā godā vatsarasya tu jāhnavī
pādodakaṃ bhagavato dvādaśābdaphalapradam
garuḍapurāṇe
jalaṃ ca yeṣāṃ tulasīvimiśritaṃ pādodakaṃ cakraśilāsamudbhavam
nityaṃ trisandhyaṃ plavate na gātraṃ khagendra te dharmabahiṣkṛtā narāḥ
tato jalāñjalīn kṣiptvā mūrdhni trīn kumbhamudrayā
mūlenāthāviśeṣeṇa kuryād devāditarpaṇam
tac ca vaidikeṣu prasiddham eva
brahmādayo ye devās tān devān tarpayāmi
bhūrdevāṃs tarpayāmi
bhuvar devāṃs tarpayāmi
svardevāṃs tarpayāmi
bhūr bhuvaḥ svar devāṃs tarpayāmi
ācāmyāṅgāni saṃmārjya snānavastrāṇyavāsasā
paridhāyāṃśuke śukle niviśyācamanaṃ caret
vidhivat tilakaṃ kṛtvā punaś cācamya vaiṣṇavaḥ
vidhāya vaidikīṃ sandhyām athopāsīta tāntrikīm
kaurme tatraiva
prākkuleṣu tataḥ sthitvā darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet sandhyām iti śrutiḥ
manusmṛtau
brāhmaṇāḥ śāktikāḥ sarve na śaivā na ca vaiṣṇavāḥ
yata upāsate devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
yā ca sandhyā jagatsūtir māyātītā hi niṣkalā
aiśvarī kevalā śaktis tattvatrayasamudbhavā
dhyātvārkamaṇḍalagatāṃ sāvitrīṃ tāṃ japed budhaḥ
prāṅmukhaḥ satataṃ vipraḥ sandhyopāsanam ācaret
kiṃca
sahasraparamāṃ nityaṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām
sāvitrīṃ vai japed vidvān prāṅmukhaḥ prayataḥ sthitaḥ
kiṃca
sandhyāhīno 'śucir nityam anarhaḥ sarvakarmasu
yad anyat kurute kiṃcin na tasya phalam āpnuyāt
yo 'nyatra kurute yatnaṃ dharmakārye dvijottamaḥ
vihāya sandhyāpraṇatiṃ sa yāti narakāyutam
ananyacetasaḥ śāntā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
upāsya vidhivat sandhyāṃ prāptāḥ pūrve parāṃ gatim
tataḥ sampūjya salile nijāṃ śrīmantradevatām
tarpayed vidhinā tasya tathaivāvaraṇāni ca
tathā ca bodhāyanasmṛtau
haviṣāgnau jale puṣpair dhyānena hṛdaye harim
arcanti sūrayo nityaṃ japena ravimaṇḍale
pādme ca tatraiva
sūrye cābhyarhaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ salile salilādibhiḥ
mūlamantram athoccārya dhyāyan kṛṣṇāṅghripaṅkaje
śrīkṛṣṇaṃ tarpayāmīti triḥ samyak tarpayet kṛtī
dhyānoddiṣṭasvarūpāya sūryamaṇḍalavartine
kṛṣṇāya kāmagāyatryā dadyād arghyam anantaram
śrīsanatkumārakalpe
ādau manmatham uddhṛtya kāmadevapadaṃ vadet
āyānte vidmahe puṣpabāṇāyeti padaṃ vadet
dhīmahīti tathoktvātha tan no 'naṅgaḥ pracodayāt
athārkamaṇḍale kṛṣṇaṃ dhyātvaitāṃ daśadhā japet
kṣamasveti tam udvāsya dadyād arghyaṃ vivasvate
vidhis tāntrikasandhyāyā jale'rcāyāś ca kaścana
yo 'nyo manyeta so 'py atra tadviśeṣāya likhyate
ādau dakṣiṇahastena gṛhṇīyād vāri vaiṣṇavaḥ
tato hṛdayamantreṇa vāmapāṇitale'rpayet
tadaṅgulīviniryātāmbhaḥkaṇair dakṣapāṇinā
mastake netramantreṇa kuryāt samprokṣaṇaṃ tataḥ
śiṣṭaṃ tac cāstramantreṇādāyāmbho dakṣapāṇinā
adhaḥ kṣipet punaś caivam iti vāracatuṣṭayam
punar hṛdayamantreṇādāyāmbho dakṣapāṇinā
nāsāpuṭena vāmenāghrāyānyena visarjayet
athāmbho 'ñjalim ādāya sūryamaṇḍalavartine
arghyaṃ gopālagāyatryā kṛṣṇāya trir nivedayet
brūyād gopījanaṃ ṅe'ntaṃ vidmahe ity ataḥ param
punar gopījanaṃ tadvad dhīmahīti tataḥ param
tan naḥ kṛṣṇa iti prānte prapūrvaṃ codayād iti
mūrdhni nyaset tadaṅgāni lalāṭe netrayor dvayoḥ
bhujayoḥ pādayoś caiva sarvāṅgeṣu tathā kramāt
tāni coktāni
pañcabhiś ca tribhiś caiva pañcabhiś ca tribhiḥ punaḥ
caturbhiś ca caturbhiś ca kuryād aṅgāni varṇakiḥ
rāsakrīḍārataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhyātvā cādityamaṇḍale
tatsammukhotkṣiptabhujo gāyatrīṃ tāṃ japet kṣaṇam
aṅganyāsaṃ svamantreṇa kṛtvāthābjaṃ jalāntare
saṃcintya pīṭhamantreṇa tarpayec ca sakṛt sakṛt
tasmiṃś ca kṛṣṇam āvāhya sakalīkṛtya mānasān
pañcopacārāt dattvāpsu dhenumudrāṃ pradarśayet
tajjalaṃ cāmṛtaṃ dhyātvā svamantreṇābhimantrya ca
aṣṭottaraśataṃ kṛṣṇottamāṅge tarpayet kṛtī
tataś ca mūlamantreṇa vārān vai pañcaviṃśatim
abhijaptenodakenācamanaṃ vidhinā caret
pādme
brahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatīn
devā yakṣās tathā nāgā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
krūrāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāś ca taravo jambhakādayaḥ
vidyādharā jaladharās tathaivākāśagāminaḥ
nirādhārāś ca ye jīvāḥ pāpadharmaratāś ca ye
teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā
kṛtopavīto devebhyo nivītī ca bhavet tataḥ
manuṣyāṃs tarpayed bhaktyā ṛṣiputrān ṛṣīṃs tathā
sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ
kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhuḥ pañcaśikhas tathā
sarve te tṛptim āyāntu maddattenāmbunā sadā
marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum
pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca
devabrahmaṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayet sākṣatodakaiḥ
apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvāsavyaṃ jānu ca bhūtale
agniṣvāttās tathā saumyā barhiṣmantas tathoṣmapāḥ
kavyānalau barhiṣadas tathā caivājyapāḥ punaḥ
tarpayet pitṛbhaktyā ca satilodakacandanaiḥ
yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca
vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtākṣayāya ca
auḍumbarāya dadhnāya nīlāya parameṣṭhine
vṛkodarāya citrāya citraguptāya vai namaḥ
darbhapāṇiḥ suprayataḥ pitṝn svān tarpayet tataḥ
pitrādīn nāmagotreṇa tathā mātāmahān api
saṃtarpya vidhinā sarvān imaṃ mantram udīrayet
ye'bāndhavā bāndhavā vā ye'nyajanmani bāndhavāḥ
te tṛptim akhilāṃ yāntu ye cāsmattoyakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
sandhyopāsanataḥ pūrvaṃ kecid devāditarpaṇam
manyante sakṛd evedaṃ purāṇoktānusārataḥ
tathā ca pādme snāne mṛdgrahaṇānantaram
evaṃ snātvā tataḥ paścād ācamya suvidhānataḥ
utthāya vāsasī śukle śuddhe tu paridhāya vai
tatas tu tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt trailokyāpyāyanāya vai
ata eva śrīrāmārcanacandrikāyām
niṣpīḍayitvā vastraṃ tu paścāt sandhyāṃ samācaret
anyathā kurute yas tu snānaṃ tasyāphalaṃ bhavet
kiṃca
vastraṃ triguṇitaṃ yas tu niṣpīḍayati mūḍhadhīḥ
vṛthā snānaṃ bhavet tasya niṣpīḍayati cāmbuni
kāśīkāṇḍe
api sarvanadītoyair mṛtkūṭaiś cātha gorasaiḥ
āpātam ācarecchaucaṃ bhāvaduṣṭo na śuddhibhāk
naktaṃ dinaṃ nimajjyāpsu kaivartāḥ kimu pāvanāḥ
śataśo 'pi tathā snātā na śuddhā bhāvadūṣitāḥ
pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye śrīnāradāmbarīṣasaṃvāde
puṇyena gāṅgena jalena kāle deśe'pi yaḥ snānaparo 'pi bhūpa
ā janmato bhāvahato 'pi dātā na śudhyatīty eva mataṃ mamaitat
prajvālya vahniṃ ghṛtatailasiktaṃ pradakṣiṇāvartaśikhaṃ svakāle
praviśya dagdhaḥ kila bhāvaduṣṭo na svargam āpnoti phalaṃ na cānyat
ata eva bhaviṣyottare
yasya hastau ca pādau ca vāṅ manaś ca susaṃyatam
vidyātapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam āpnuyāt
aśraddadhānaḥ pāpātmā nāstiko 'cchinnasaṃśayaḥ
hetuniṣṭhaś ca pañcaite na tīrthaphalabhāginaḥ
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse śaucīyo nāma tṛtīyo vilāsaḥ
snātvā śrīkṛṣṇacaitanyanāmatīrthottame sakṛt
nityāśuciḥ śucīndraḥ san svadharmaṃ vaktum arhati
atha svagṛham āgacched ādau natveṣṭadevatām
gurūn jyeṣṭhāṃś ca puṣpaidhaḥkuśāmbhodhāraketarān
tathā ca śrīnṛsiṃhapurāṇe
jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gacched gṛhaṃ pumān
pauruṣeṇa tu sūktena tato viṣṇuṃ samarcayet
mandiraṃ mārjayed viṣṇor vidhāyācamanādikam
kṛṣṇaṃ paśyan kīrtayaṃś ca dāsyenātmānam arpayet
śuddhaṃ gomayam ādāya tato mṛtsnāṃ jalaṃ tathā
bhaktyā tat parito limped abhyukṣec ca tadaṅganam
tathā ca navamaskandhe śrīmadambarīṣopākhyāne
sa vai manaḥ kṛṣṇapadāravindayor vacāṃsi vaikuṇṭhaguṇānuvarṇane karau harer mandiramārjanādiṣu śrutiṃ cakārācyutasatkathodaye
ekādaśaskandhe śrībhagavaduddhavasaṃvāde bhagavaddharmakathane
sammārjanopalepābhyāṃ sekamaṇḍalavartanaiḥ
gṛhaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ mahyaṃ dāsavad yad amāyayā
śrīnṛsiṃhapurāṇe
narasiṃhagṛhe nityaṃ yaṃ sammārjanam ācaret
samastapāpanirmukto viṣṇuloke sa modate
śrīviṣṇudharmottare
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt puruṣaḥ keśavālaye
rajastamobhyāṃ nirmuktaḥ sa bhaven nātra saṃśayaḥ
pāṃśūnāṃ yāvatāṃ rājan kuryāt saṃmārjanaṃ naraḥ
tāvanty abdāni sa sukhī nākam āsādya modate
śrīvārāhe
yāvatkāni prahārāṇi bhūmisaṃmārjane daduḥ
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi śākadvīpe mahīyate
jāyate mama bhaktaś ca sarvadharmasamanvitaḥ
śucir bhāgavataḥ śuddho hy aparādhavivarjitaḥ
tato bhuktvā sarvabhogān tīrtvā saṃsārasāgaram
śākadvīpāt paribhraṣṭaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati
nandanaṃ vanam āśritya modate cāpsaraiḥ saha
nandanāc ca paribhraṣṭo mama karmavyavasthitaḥ
sarvasaṅgāt parityajya mama lokaṃ tu gacchati
tatraiva
gomayaṃ gṛhya vai bhūmiṃ mama veśmopalepayet
yāvatas tu padāṃs tatra samantād upalepayet
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi madbhakto jāyate tathā
samīpe yadi vā dūre yaś cālayati gomayam
yāvat tasya padāgrāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate
śālmalau tatparibhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ
madbhaktaś caiva jāyate sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
yaś cālepayate bhūmiṃ gomayena dṛḍhavrataḥ
tasya dṛṣṭvānulepaṃ tu mama tuṣṭiḥ prajāyate
goś ca yasyāḥ purīṣeṇa kriyate bhūmilepanam
ekenaiva tu lepena goyonyā vipramucyate
sthānopalepane bhūme salilaṃ yo dadāti me
tasya puṇyaṃ mahābhāge śṛṇu tattvena niṣkalam
yāvanti jalabindūni lipyamānasya sundari
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate
yāvanto bindavaḥ kecit pānīyasya vasundhare
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi krauñcadvīpe mahīyate
krauñcadvīpāt paribhraṣṭaḥ sarvadharmaparāyaṇaḥ
sarvasaṅgān parityajya mama lokaṃ ca gacchati
śrīviṣṇudharmottare
kṛtvopalepanaṃ viṣṇor naras tv āyatane sadā
gomayena śubhān lokān ayatnād eva gacchati
hastapramāṇaṃ bhūbhāgam upalipya narādhipa
devarāmāśataṃ nāke labhate satataṃ naraḥ
nārasiṃhe
gomayena mṛdā toyair yaḥ kuryād upalepanam
cāndrāyaṇaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tatraiva śrīdharmarājasya dūtānuśāsane
saṃmārjanaṃ yaḥ kurute gomayenopalepanam
karoti bhavane viṣṇos tyājyaṃ teṣāṃ kulatrayam
śrīviṣṇudharmottare
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pānīyena surālaye
sa śāntatāpo bhavati nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
abhyukṣaṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryād devadevājire naraḥ
sarvapāpavinirmukto vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute
sarvatobhadrapadmādīn abhijñaḥ svastikāni ca
viracayya vicitrāṇi maṇḍayeddharimandiram
tathā ca nārasiṃhe
saṃmārjanopalepābhyāṃ raṅgapadmādiśobhanam
kuryāt sthānaṃ mahāviṣṇoḥ sojjvalāṅgaṃ mudānvitaḥ
skandapurāṇe kārttikaprasaṅge
agamyagamane pāpam abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe
sarvaṃ tannāśam āpnoti maṇḍayitvā harer gṛham
aṇumātraṃ tu yaḥ kuryān maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ
mṛdā dhātuvikāraiś ca divi kalpaśataṃ vaset
śālagrāmaśilāgre tu yaḥ kuryāt svastikaṃ śubham
kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa punāty ā saptamaṃ kulam
maṇḍalaṃ kurute nityaṃ yā nārī keśavāgrataḥ
saptajanmāni vaidhavyaṃ na prāpnoti kadācana
gṛhītvā gomayaṃ yā tu maṇḍalaṃ keśavāgrataḥ
bhartur viyogaṃ nāpnoti santateś ca dhanasya ca
prāṅgaṇaṃ varṇakopetaṃ svastikaiś ca samanvitam
devasya kurute yas tu krīḍate bhuvanatraye
nāradīye
mṛdā dhātuvikārair vā varṇakair gomayena vā
viṣṇuloke'tha tatra rathaiḥ saspṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī
haribhaktisudhodaye
upalipyālayaṃ viṣṇoś citrayitvātha varṇakaiḥ
viṣṇuloke'tha tatrasthaiḥ saspṛhaṃ vīkṣyate sukhī
āgame
vidiggatacatuṣkāṇi bhittvā ṣoḍaśadhā sudhīḥ
mārjayet svastikākāraṃ śvetapītāruṇāsitaiḥ
tatra ca pañcarātravacanam
rajāṃsi pañcavarṇāni maṇḍalārthaṃ hi kārayet
śālitaṇḍulacūrṇena śuklaṃ vā yavasambhavam
raktakuṅkumasindūragairikādisamudbhavam
haritālodbhavaṃ pītaṃ rajanīsambhavaṃ kvacit
kṛṣṇaṃ dagdhair haridyavair haritpītair vimiśritam
tato dhvajapatākādi vinyasya harimandire
vicitraṃ bhūṣayet tac ca bhagavadbhaktimān naraḥ
dhvajam āropayed yas tu prāsādopari bhaktitaḥ
tasya brahmapade vāsaḥ krīḍate brahmaṇā saha
bṛhannāradīye
yaḥ kuryād viṣṇubhavane dhvajāropaṇam uttamam
sampūjyate viriñcyādyaiḥ kim anyair bahubhāṣitaiḥ
tatraivāgre ca
paṭo dhvajasya viprendra yāvac calati vāyunā
tāvanti pāpajālāni naśyanty eva na saṃśayaḥ
mahāpātakayukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ
dhvajaṃ viṣṇugṛhe kṛtvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
āropitaṃ dhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā ye'bhinandanti dhārmikāḥ
te'pi sarve pramucyante mahāpātakakoṭibhiḥ
evaṃ bṛhannāradīye khyātaṃ yac cānyad adbhutam
dhvajāropaṇamāhātmyaṃ tad draṣṭavyam ihākhilam
dvārakāmāhātmye
kṛṣṇālayaṃ yaḥ kurute patākābhiś ca śobhitam
sadaiva tasya loke tu vāsas tasya na cānyataḥ
viṣṇudharmottare
patākāṃ ca śubhāṃ dattvā tathā keśavaveśmani
vāyulokam avāpnoti bahūn abdagaṇān dvijaḥ
dodhūyate yathā sā tu vāyunā keśavālaye
tathā tasyāpi sakalaṃ dehāt pāpaṃ vidhūyate
dvārakāmāhātmye tatraiva
bhūpa vandanamālāṃ tu kurute kṛṣṇaveśmani
devakanyāvṛtair lakṣaiḥ sevyate suranāyakaiḥ
yaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇabhavanaṃ kadalīstambhaśobhitam
nandate cāpsaroyuktaḥ svāgataṃ tasya devarāṭ
tatra tāmrādipātraṃ yat prabhor vastrādikaṃ ca yat
pīṭhādikaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ yathoktaṃ ca viśodhayet
nārasiṃhe
pādapīṭhaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya bilvapatreṇa dharṣayet
uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe
uḍumbarāṇām amlena kṣāreṇa trapusīsayoḥ
bhasmāmbubhiś ca kāṃsyānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya ca
vāyupurāṇe ca
maṇivajrapravālānāṃ muktāśaṅkhopalasya ca
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tilakalkena vā punaḥ
brāhme
suvarṇarūpyaśaṅkhāśmaśuktiratnamayāni ca
kāṃsyāyastāmraraityāni trapusīsamayāni ca
nirlepāni tu śudhyanti kevalenodakena tu
śūdrocchiṣṭāni śodhyāni tridhā kṣārāmlavāribhiḥ
atiduṣṭaṃ tu pātrādi viśodhyātithyakarmaṇe
yuñjyāt tatparivartāya prabhukarmāntarāya vā
etasya parivartena prabhave'nyat samarpayet
ity ayaṃ sarvato loke sadācāro virājate
manuḥ
tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyaraityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca
śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ
śaṅkhaḥ
amlodakena tāmrasya sīsasya trapuṇas tathā
kṣāreṇa śuddhiṃ kāṃsyasya lauhasya ca vinirdiśet
kiṃca
sūtikocchiṣṭabhāṇḍasya surādyupahatasya ca
triḥsaptamārjanācchuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam
anyatra ca
tāmram amlena śudhyena na cedāmiṣalepanam
āmiṣeṇa tu yal liptaṃ punar dāhena śudhyanti
brāhme
sūtikāśavaviṇmūtrarajasvalahatāni ca
prakṣeptavyāni tāny agnau yac ca yāvat sahed api
ata eva devalaḥ
lohānāṃ dahanācchuddhir bhasmanā gomayena vā
dahanāt khananād vāpi śailānām ambhasāpi vā
kāṣṭhānāṃ takṣaṇācchuddhir mṛdgomayajalair api
mṛṇmayānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ dahanācchuddhir iṣyate
manuḥ
madyair mūtraiḥ purīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaiḥ pūyaśoṇitaiḥ
saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śudhyeta punaḥpākena mṛnmayam
vṛddhaśātātapaḥ
saṃhatānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ yad ekam upahanyate
tasyaivaṃ śodhanaṃ proktaṃ sāmānyadravyaśuddhikṛt
tatra śaṅkhaḥ
tāntavaṃ malinaṃ pūrvam adbhiḥ kṣāraiś ca śodhayet
aṃśubhiḥ śoṣayitvā vā vāyunā vā samāharet
ūrṇāpaṭṭāṃśukakṣaumadukūlāvikacarmaṇām
alpāśauce bhavecchuddhiḥ śoṣaṇaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ
tāny evāmedhyaliptāni nenijyād gaurasarṣapaiḥ
dhānyakalkaiḥ parṇakalkaiḥ rasaiś ca phalavalkalaiḥ
tulikādyupadhānāni puṣparatnāmbarāṇi ca
śodhayitvātape kiṃcit karair unmārjayen muhuḥ
paścāc ca vāriṇā prokṣya śucīty evam udāharet
tāny apy atimalāktāni yathāvat pariśodhayet
śātātapaḥ
kusumbhakuṅkumāraktās tathā lākṣārasena ca
prakṣālanena śudhyanti caṇḍālasparśane tathā
yamaḥ
kṛṣṇājinānāṃ vātaiś ca bālānāṃ mṛdbhir ambhasā
gomūtreṇāsthidantānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ
śaṅkhaḥ
siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena dantaśṛṅgamayasya ca
govālaiḥ phalapātrāṇām asthnāṃ syācchṛṅgavat tathā
kiṃca
niryāsānāṃ guḍānāṃ ca lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca
kusumbhakusumānāṃ ca ūrṇākārpāsayos tathā
prokṣaṇāt kathitā śuddhir ity āha bhagavān yamaḥ
manuḥ
adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām
prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate
cailavatcarmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathaiva ca
śākamūlaphalānāṃ ca dhānyavatśuddhir iṣyate
prokṣaṇāt tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati
mārjanopāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam
kiṃca
yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ
tāvan mṛdvāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu
bṛhaspatiḥ
vastravaidalacarmādeḥ śuddhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ smṛtam
atiduṣṭasya tanmātraṃ tyajecchittvā tu śuddhaye
viṣṇuḥ
mṛtparṇatṛṇakāṣṭhānāṃ śvāsthicāṇḍālavāyasaiḥ
sparśane vihitaṃ śaucaṃ somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ
baudhāyanaḥ
āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ nāvaḥ panthās tṛṇāni ca
mārutārkeṇa śudhyanti pakveṣṭaracitāni ca
tatra baudhāyanaḥ
vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇād adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca
tanmātrasyāpahārād vā nistuṣīkaraṇena ca
śaṅkhaḥ
śrapaṇaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca
bhāṇḍāni plāvayed adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca
brāhme
dravadravyāṇi bhūrīṇi pariplāvyāni cāmbhasā
śasyāni vrīhayaś caiva śākamūlaphalāni ca
tyaktvā tu dūṣitaṃ bhāgaṃ plāvyāny atha jalena tu
bṛhaspatiḥ
tāpanaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya ca
tanmātram uddhṛtaṃ śudhyet kaṭhinaṃ tu payodadhi
avilīnaṃ tathā sarpir vilīnaṃ śrapaṇena tu
ādhāradoṣe tu nayet pātrāt pātrāntaraṃ dravam
ghṛtaṃ ca pāyasaṃ kṣīraṃ tathaikṣavaraso guḍaḥ
śūdrabhāṇḍasthitaṃ takraṃ tathā madhu na duṣyati
kiṃca manuḥ
ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃcana
anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt
anye'pi śuddhividhayo dravyāṇāṃ smṛtiśāstrataḥ
apekṣyā vaiṣṇavair jñeyās tattadvistāraṇair alam
praṇamyātha mahāviṣṇuṃ prārthyānujñāṃ tu vaiṣṇavaḥ
samāharet śrītulasīṃ puṣpādi ca yathoditam
yac ca hārītavacanam
snānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye kecit puṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vai dvijāḥ
devatās tan na gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat
tac ca madhyāhnasnānaviṣayaṃ yata uktaṃ pādme vaiśākhamāhātmye
asnātvā tulasīṃ chittvā devārthaṃ pitṛkarmaṇi
tat sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ yāti pañcagavyena śudhyati
svagṛhe vācaran snānaṃ prakṣālyāṅghrī karau tathā
ācamyāyamya ca prāṇān kṛtanyāso hariṃ smaret
tato gaṇādikaṃ smṛtvā tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ
pūrṇe pātre samastāni tīrthāny āvāhayet kṛtī
āvāhanamantraś cāyam
gaṅge ca yamune caiva godāvari sarasvati
narmade sindhukāveri jale'smin sannidhiṃ kuru
athavā jāhnavīm eva sarvatīrthamayīṃ budhaḥ
āvāhayed dvādaśabhir nāmabhir jalabhājane
dvādaśanāmāni
nalinī nandinī sītā mālinī ca mahāpagā
viṣṇupādārghyasambhūtā gaṅgā tripathagāminī
bhāgīrathī bhogavatī jāhnavī tridaśeśvarī
padmapurāṇe ca vaiśākhamāhātmye
nandinīty eva te nāma vedeṣu nalinīti ca
dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā viśvagāthā śivapriyā
vidyādharī mahādevī tathā lokaprasādinī
kṣemaṃkarī jāhnavī ca śāntā śāntipradāyinī
athācamya guruṃ smṛtānujñāṃ prārthya ca pūrvavat
kṛṣṇapādābjato gaṅgāṃ patantīṃ mūrdhni cintayet
tathā coktaṃ śrīnāradapañcarātre
svasthitaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mantramūrtiṃ prabhuṃ smaret
anantādityasaṅkāśaṃ vāsudevaṃ caturbhujam
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ pītāmbarāvṛtam
śyāmalaṃ śāntavadanaṃ prasannaṃ varadekṣaṇam
divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ cārahāsamukhāmbujam
anekaratnasaṃchannajvalanmakarakuṇḍalam
vanamālāparivṛtaṃ nāradādibhir arcitam
keyūravalayopetaṃ suvarṇamukuṭojjvalam
sarvāṅgasundaraṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
tatpādapaṅkajād dhārāṃ nipatantīṃ svamūrdhani
cintayed brahmarandhreṇa praviśantīṃ svakāṃ tanum
tayā saṃkṣālayet sarvam antardehagataṃ malam
tatkṣaṇād virajā mantrī jāyate sphaṭikopamaḥ
idaṃ snānāntaraṃ māntrāt sahasram adhikaṃ smṛtam
sakṛn nārāyaṇetyādi vacanaṃ tatra kīrtayet
snānakāle tu tannāma saṃsmarec ca mahāprabhum
tathā ca kūrmapurāṇe
āpo nārāyaṇodbhūtās tā evāsyāyanaṃ yathaḥ
tasmān nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānakāle smared budhaḥ
snāyād uṣṇodakenāpi śakto 'py āmalakais tathā
tilais tailaiś ca saṃvarjya pratiṣiddhadināni tu
ṣaṭtriṃśanmate
āpaḥ svabhāvato medhyā viśeṣād agniyogataḥ
tena santaḥ praśaṃsanti snānam uṣṇena vāriṇā
yamaś ca
āpaḥ svayaṃ sadā pūtā vahnitaptā viśeṣataḥ
tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu uṣṇāmbhaḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam
yac coktaṃ śaṅkhena
snātasya vahnitaptena tathaivātapavāriṇā
śarīraśuddhir vijñeyā na tu snānaphalaṃ bhavet
tat tu kāmyanaimittikaviṣayam
kuryān naimittikaṃ snānaṃ śītādbhiḥ kāmyam eva ca
nityaṃ yādṛcchikaṃ caiva yathāruci samācaret
tatra yamaḥ
putrajanmani saṅkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ
aspṛśyasparśane caiva na snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā
vṛddhamanuḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ tathā darśe yaḥ snāyād uṣṇavāriṇā
sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ
tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ
tuṣyaty āmalakair viṣṇur ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
śrīkāmaḥ sarvadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ
saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlīvastraṃ na dhārayet
na cāpy āmalakaṃ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ
bhṛguḥ
amāṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ saptamīṃ ca navamīṃ ca trayodaśīm
saṅkrāntau ravivāre ca snānamālakais tyajet
yājñavalkyaḥ
dhātrīphalair amāvasyāsaptamīnavamīṣu ca
yaḥ snāyāt tasya hīyante tejaś cāyurdhanaṃ sutāḥ
tatra bṛhaspatiḥ
sarvakālaṃ tilaiḥ snānaṃ punar vyāso 'bravīn muniḥ
ṣaṭtriṃśanmate
tathā saptamyamāvasyāsaṅkrāntigrahaṇeṣu ca
dhanaputrakalatrārthī tilaspṛṣṭaṃ na saṃspṛśet
tatraiva
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyaṃ caturthīṣv api ca parvasu
yogī yājñavalkyaḥ
daśamyāṃ tailam apṛṣṭvā yaḥ snāyād avicakṣaṇaḥ
catvāri tasya naśyanti āyuḥ prajñā yaśodhanam
mohāt pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ kuhūṃ riktātithiṃ tathā
tailenābhyañjayed yas tu caturbhiḥ parihīyate
pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ ravisaṅkrame
dvādaśyāṃ saptamīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ tailasparśaṃ vivarjayet
anyac ca
saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ navamyāṃ pratipady api
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyām amāvasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
kiṃca
snāne vā yadi vāsnāne pakkatailaṃ na duṣyati
kiṃca atrismṛtau
tailābhyakto ghṛtābhyakto viṇmūtre kurute dvijaḥ
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā pañcagavyena śudhyati
athāṅgamalam uttārya snātvā vidhivad ācaret
nāsālagnena culukodakenaivāghamarṣaṇam
tato gurvādipādodaiḥ prāgvat kṛtvābhiṣecanam
kāryo 'bhiṣekaḥ śaṅkhena tulasīmiśritair jalaiḥ
gāruḍe
mārjayaty abhiṣeke tu tulasyā vaiṣṇavo naraḥ
sarvatīrthamayaṃ dehaṃ tatkṣaṇāt dvija jāyate
tulasīdalajasnāne ekādaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo yadyapi brahmahā bhavet
tanmūlamṛttikābhyaṅgaṃ kṛtvā snāti dine dine
daśāśvamedhāvabhṛtaṃ labhate snānajaṃ phalam
tulasīdalasaṃmiśraṃ toyaṃ gaṅgāsamaṃ viduḥ
yo vahecchirasā nityaṃ dhṛtā bhavati jāhnavī
pādodakaṃ tāmrapātre kṛtvā satulasīdalam
śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvābhiṣiñceta mūlenaiva svamūrdhani
tanmāhātmye coktaṃ pādme kārttikamāhātmye
dvārakācakrasaṃyuktaśālagrāmaśilājalam
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu nikṣiptaṃ snānārthaṃ tāmrabhājane
tulasīdalasaṃyuktaṃ brahmahatyāvināśanam
snānaśāṭītareṇaiva vāsasāmbhāṃsi gātrataḥ
saṃmārjya vāsasī dadhyāt paridhānottarīyake
tatrātriḥ
adhautaṃ kārudhautaṃ vā paredyudhautam eva vā
kāṣāyaṃ malinaṃ vastraṃ kaupīnaṃ ca parityajet
na cārdram eva vasanaṃ paridadhyāt kadācana
nagno malinavastraḥ syāt nagnaś cārdhapaṭas tathā
nagno dviguṇavastraḥ syān nagno raktapaṭas tathā
nagnaś ca syūtavastraḥ syān nagnaḥ snigdhapaṭas tathā
dvikaccho 'nuttarīyaś ca nagnaś cāvastra eva ca
śrautaṃ smārtaṃ tathā karma na nagnaś cintayed api
mohāt kurvann adho gacchet tad bhaved āsuraṃ smṛtam
japahomopavāseṣu dhautavastradharo bhavet
alaṃkṛtaḥ śucir maunī śrāddhādau ca jitendriyaḥ
gobhilaḥ
ekavastro na bhuñjīta na kuryād devanārcanam
trailokyasammohanapañcarātre
śuklavāso bhaven nityaṃ raktaṃ caiva vivarjayet
aṅgirāḥ
śaucaṃ sahasraromāṇāṃ vāyvagnyarkenduraśmibhiḥ
retaḥspṛṣṭaṃ śavaspṛṣṭam āvikaṃ naiva duṣyati
anyatra ca
chinnaṃ vā saṃdhitaṃ dagdham āvikaṃ na praduṣyati
āvikena tu vastreṇa mānavaḥ śrāddham ācaret
gayāśrāddhasamaṃ proktaṃ pitṛbhyo dattam akṣayam
na kuryāt saṃdhitaṃ vastraṃ devakarmaṇi bhūmipa
na dagdhaṃ na ca vai chinnaṃ pārakyaṃ na tu dhārayet
kākaviṣṭhāsamaṃ hy uktam avidhautaṃ ca yad bhavet
rajakād āhṛtaṃ yac ca na tad vastraṃ bhavecchuci
kīṭaspṛṣṭaṃ tu yad vastraṃ purīṣaṃ yena kāritam
mūtraṃ vā maithunaṃ vāpi tad vastraṃ parivarjayet
āvikaṃ tu sadā vastraṃ pavitraṃ rājasattama
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kriyāyāṃ ca praśasyate
dhautādhautaṃ tathā dagdhaṃ saṃdhitaṃ rajakāhṛtam
śukramūtraraktaliptaṃ tathāpi paramaṃ śuci
agnir āvikavastraṃ ca brāhmaṇāś ca tathā kuśāḥ
caturṇāṃ na kṛto doṣo brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
kiṃcānyatra
dhārayed vāsasī śuddhe paridhānottarīyake
acchinnasudaśe śukle ācāmet pīṭhasaṃsthitaḥ
bahvṛcapariśiṣṭe
yatīnām āsanaṃ śuklaṃ kūrmākāraṃ tu kārayet
anyeṣāṃ tu catuṣpādaṃ caturasraṃ tu kārayet
gośakṛnmayaṃ bhinnaṃ tathā palāśapaippalam
lohabaddhaṃ sadaivārkaṃ varjayed āsanaṃ budhaḥ
tatraiva
dānam ācamanaṃ homaṃ bhojanaṃ devatārcanam
prauḍhapādo na kurvīta svādhyāyaṃ caiva tarpaṇam
āsanārūḍhapādas tu jānunor vātha jaṅghayoḥ
kṛtāvasakthiko yas tu prauḍhapādaḥ sa ucyate
tato bhūmigatāṅghriḥ san niviśyācamya darbhabhṛt
ūrdhvapuṇḍrādikaṃ kuryāt śrīgopīcandanādinā
tatrādāv anulepena bhagavaccaraṇābjayoḥ
nirmālyena prasādena sarvāṇy aṅgāni mārjayet
tad uktaṃ brāhme śrībhagavatā
śālagrāmaśilālagnaṃ candanaṃ dhārayet sadā
sarvāṅgeṣu mahāśuddhisiddhaye kamalāsana
tato dvādaśabhiḥ kuryān nāmabhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ
dvādaśāṅgeṣu vidhivad ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇi vaiṣṇavaḥ
padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe
lalāṭe keśavaṃ dhyāyen nārāyaṇam athodare
vakṣaḥsthale mādhavaṃ tu govindaṃ kaṇṭhakūpake
viṣṇuṃ ca dakṣiṇe kukṣau bāhau ca madhusūdanam
trivikramaṃ kandhare tu vāmanaṃ vāmapārśvake
śrīdharaṃ vāmabāhau tu hṛṣīkeśaṃ tu kandhare
pṛṣṭhe tu padmanābhaṃ ca kaṭyāṃ dāmodaraṃ nyaset
tatprakṣālanatoyaṃ tu vāsudeveti mūrdhani
kiṃca
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe tu sarveṣāṃ prathamaṃ smṛtam
lalāṭādikrameṇaiva dhāraṇaṃ tu vidhīyate
evaṃ nyāsaṃ samācarya sampradāyānusārataḥ
nyaset kirīṭamantraṃ ca mūrdhni sarvārthasiddhaye
oṃ śrīkirīṭakeyūrahāramakarakuṇḍalacakraśaṅkhagadāpadmahastapītāmbaradhara śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣaḥsthala śrībhūmisahitasvātmajyotir dīptikarāya sahasrādityatejase namo namaḥ
pādme śrībhagavaduktau
matpriyārthaṃ śubhārthaṃ vā rakṣārthe caturānana
matpūjāhomakāle ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaḥ
madbhakto dhārayen nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ bhayāpaham
tatraiva śrīnāradoktau
yajño dānaṃ tapo homaḥ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam
vyarthaṃ bhavati tat sarvam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe
ūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu kiṃcit karma karoti yaḥ
iṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ sarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ
ūrdhvapuṇḍrair vihīnas tu sandhyākarmādikaṃ caret
tat sarvaṃ rākṣasaṃ nityaṃ narakaṃ cādhigacchati
anyac ca
ūrdhvapuṇḍre tripuṇḍraṃ yaḥ kurute narādhamaḥ
bhaṅktvā viṣṇugṛhaṃ puṇḍraṃ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam
ata eva pādme śrīnāradoktau
yaccharīraṃ manuṣyāṇām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vinā kṛtam
draṣṭavyaṃ naiva tat tāvat śmaśānasadṛśaṃ bhavet
padmapurāṇe
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mṛdā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate
sa cāṇḍālo 'pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ
skānde
tiryakpuṇḍraṃ na kurvīta samprāpte maraṇe'pi ca
naivānyan nāma ca brūyāt pumān nārāyaṇād ṛte
dhārayed viṣṇunirmālyaṃ dhūpaśeṣaṃ vilepanam
vaiṣṇavaṃ kārayet puṇḍraṃ gopīcandanasambhavam
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
yasyordhvapuṇḍraṃ dṛśyeta lalāṭe no narasya hi
taddarśanaṃ na kartavyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūryaṃ nirīkṣayet
anyatrāpi
vaiṣṇavānāṃ brāhmaṇānām ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ vidhīyate
anyeṣāṃ tu tripuṇḍraṃ syād iti brahmavido viduḥ
tripuṇḍraṃ yasya viprasya ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ na dṛśyate
taṃ spṛṣṭvāpy athavā dṛṣṭvā sacelaṃ snānam ācaret
ūrdhvapuṇḍre na kurvīta vaiṣṇavānāṃ tripuṇḍrakam
kṛtatripuṇḍramartyasya kriyā na prītaye hareḥ
ata evottarakhaṇḍe
aśvatthapatrasaṅkāśo veṇupatrākṛtis tathā
padmakuḍmalasaṅkāśo mohanaṃ tritayaṃ smṛtam
skānde kārttikaprasaṅge
ūrdhvapuṇḍro mṛdā śubhro lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate
caṇḍālo 'pi viśuddhātmā yāti braham sanātanam
ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā lakṣmīr ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitaṃ yaśaḥ
ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthitā muktir ūrdhvapuṇḍre sthito hariḥ
padmapurāṇe
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ mudā saumyaṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate
sa cāṇḍālo 'pi śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ
tatraivottarakhaṇḍe śivomāsaṃvāde
ūrdhvapuṇḍrasya madhye tu viśāle sumanohare
lakṣmyā sārdhaṃ samāsīno devadevo janārdanaḥ
tasmād yasya śarīre tu ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dhṛto bhavet
tasya dehaṃ bhagavato vimalaṃ mandiraṃ śubham
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo vipraḥ sarvalokeṣu pūjitaḥ
vimānavaram āruhya yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
namaskṛtvāthavā bhaktyā sarvadānaphalaṃ labhet
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaṃ vipraṃ yaḥ śrāddhe bhojayiṣyati
ā kalpakoṭipitaras tasya tṛptā na saṃśayaḥ
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharo yas tu kuryācchrāddhaṃ śubhānane
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi gayāśrāddhaphalaṃ labhet
yajñadānatapaścaryājapahomādikaṃ ca yat
ūrdhvapuṇḍradharaḥ kuryāt tasya puṇyam anantakam
śrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇe
aśucir vāpyanācāro manasā pāpam ācaran
śucir eva bhaven nityam ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṅkito naraḥ
tatraiva śrībhagavadvacanam
ūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo mriyate yatra kutracit
śvapāko 'pi vimānastho mama loke mahīyate
ūrdhvapūṇḍradharo martyo gṛhe yasyānnam aśnute
tadā viṃśatkulaṃ tasya narakād uddharāmy ahaṃ
śrībrahmāṇḍapurāṇe
vīkṣyādarśe jale vāpi yo vidadhyāt prayatnataḥ
ūrdhvapūṇḍraṃ mahābhāga sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
daśāṅgulapramāṇaṃ tu uttamottamam ucyate
navāṅgulaṃ madhyamaṃ syād aṣṭāṅgulam ataḥ param
etair aṅgulibhedais tu kārayen na nakhaiḥ spṛśet
padmapurāṇe uttarakhaṇḍe tatraiva
ekāntino mahābhāgāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
sāntarālaṃ prakurvīran puṇḍraṃ haripadākṛtim
śyāmaṃ śāntikaraṃ proktaṃ raktaṃ vaśyakaraṃ tathā
śrīkaraṃ pītam ity āhuḥ śvetaṃ mokṣakaraṃ śubham
vartulaṃ tiryag acchidraṃ hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tataṃ tanum
vakraṃ virūpaṃ baddhāgraṃ chinnamūlaṃ padacyutam
aśubhaṃ rūkṣam āsaktaṃ tathā nāṅgulikalpitam
vigandham avasahyaṃ ca puṇḍram āhur anarthakam
ārabhya nāsikāmūlaṃ lalāṭāntaṃ likhen mṛdā
nāsikāyās trayo bhāgā nāsāmūlaṃ pracakṣyate
samārabhya bhruvor madhyam antarālaṃ prakalpayet
tatraiva
nirantarālaṃ yaḥ kuryād ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ dvijādhamaḥ
sa hi tatra sthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ śriyaṃ caiva vyapohati
acchidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ tu ye kurvanti dvijādhamāḥ
teṣāṃ lalāṭe satataṃ śunaḥ pādo na saṃśayaḥ
tasmācchidrānvitaṃ puṇḍraṃ daṇḍākāraṃ suśobhanam
viprāṇāṃ satataṃ kāryaṃ strīṇāṃ ca śubhadarśane
nāsādikeśaparyantam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ suśobhanam
madhye chidrasamāyuktaṃ tad vidyāddharimandiram
vāmapārśve sthito brahmā dakṣiṇe ca sadāśivaḥ
madhye viṣṇuṃ vijānīyāt tasmān madhyaṃ na lepayet
vāyupurāṇe sevāparādhe
adhṛtvā cordhvapuṇḍraṃ ca hareḥ pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ
tiryakpuṇḍradharo yas tu yajed devaṃ janārdanam
acchidreṇordhvapuṇḍreṇa bhasmanā tiryagaṅginā
adhṛtvā śaṅkhacakre ca cetyādinā doṣa uktaḥ
śrutiś ca yajurvedasya hiraṇyakeśauryaśakhāyām
hareḥ padākrāntim ātmani dhārayati yaḥ
sa parasya priyo bhavati sa puṇyavān
madhye chidram ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ yo dhārayati sa muktibhāg bhavati
smṛtiḥ
anāmikā kāmadoktā madhyam āyuṣkarī bhavet
aṅguṣṭhaḥ puṣṭidaḥ proktas tarjanī mokṣadāyinī
padmapurāṇe tatraiva
parvatāgre nadītīre bilvamūle jalāśaye
sindhutīre ca valmīke harikṣetre viśeṣataḥ
viṣṇoḥ snānodakaṃ yatra pravāhayati nityaśaḥ
puṇḍrāṇāṃ dhāraṇārthāya gṛhṇīyāt tatra mṛttikām
śrīraṅge veṅkaṭādrau ca śrīkūrme dvārake śubhe
prayāge nārasiṃhādrau vārāhe tulasīvane
gṛhītvā mṛttikāṃ bhaktyā viṣṇupādajalaiḥ saha
dhṛtvā puṇḍrāṇi cāṅgeṣu viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt
tatraiva
yat tu divyaṃ harikṣetre tasyaiva mṛdam āharet
uktaṃ ca pādme śrīnāradena
brahmaghno vātha goghno vā haitukaḥ sarvapāpakṛt
gopīcandanasamparkāt pūto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt
gopīcandanakhaṇḍaṃ tu yo dadāti hi vaiṣṇave
kulam ekottaraṃ tena sambhavet tāritaṃ śatam
skandapurāṇe
śaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanuḥ śirasā mañjarīdharaḥ
gopīcandanaliptāṅgo dṛṣṭaś cet tad aghaṃ kṛtaḥ
gopīmṛttulasī śaṅkhaḥ śālagrāmaḥ sacakrakaḥ
gṛhe'pi yasya pañcaite tasya pāpabhayaṃ kutaḥ
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamena
śrīkhaṇḍe kva sa āmodaḥ svarovarṇaḥ kva tādṛśaḥ
tat pāvitryaṃ kva vai tīrthe śrīgopīcandane yathā
uktaṃ ca garuḍapurāṇe nāradena
yo mṛttikāṃ dvāravatīsamudbhavāṃ kare samādāya lalāṭapaṭṭake
karoti nityaṃ tv atha cordhvapuṇḍraṃ kriyāphalaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ sadā bhavet
kriyāvihīnaṃ yadi mantrahīnaṃ śraddhāvihīnaṃ yadi kālavarjitam
kṛtvā lalāṭe yadi gopīcandanaṃ prāpnoti tat karmaphalaṃ sadākṣayam
gopīcandanasambhavaṃ suruciraṃ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dvijo nityaṃ dhārayate yadi dvijapate rātrau divā sarvadā
yat puṇyaṃ kurujāṅgale ravigrahe mādhyāṃ prayāge tathā tat prāpnoti khagendra viṣṇusadane saṃtiṣṭhate devavat
yasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati gopīcandanaṃ bhaktyā lalāṭe manujo bibharti
tasmin gṛhe tiṣṭhati sarvadā hariḥ śraddhānvitaḥ kaṃsahā vihaṅgama
yo dhārayet kṛṣṇapurīsamudbhavāṃ sadā pavitrāṃ kalikilbiṣāpahām
nityaṃ lalāṭe harimantrasaṃyutāṃ yamaṃ na paśyed yadi pāpasaṃvṛtaḥ
yasyāntakāle khaga gopīcandanaṃ bāhvor lalāṭe hṛdi mastake ca
prayāti lokaṃ kamalālayaṃ prabhor gobālaghātī yadi brahmahā bhavet
grahā na pīḍanti na rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ yakṣāḥ piśācoragabhūtadānavāḥ
lalāṭapaṭṭe khaga gopīcandanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate yasya hareḥ prasādataḥ
padmapurāṇe śrīgotamena
ambarīṣa mahāghasya kṣayārthe kuru vīkṣaṇam
lalāṭe yaiḥ kṛtaṃ nityaṃ gopīcandanapuṇḍrakam
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca śrīyamena
dūtāḥ śṛṇuta yadbhālaṃ gopīcandanalāñchitam
jvaladindhanavat so 'pi tyājyo dūre prayatnataḥ
atha tasyopari śrīmattulasīmūlamṛtsnayā
tatraiva vaiṣṇavaiḥ kāryam ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ manoharam
tanmṛdaṃ gṛhya yaiḥ puṇḍraṃ lalāṭe dhāritaṃ naraiḥ
pramāṇakaṃ kṛtaṃ tais tu mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati
tatraiva ca kārttikamāhātmye brahmanāradasaṃvāde
tulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate
dehaṃ na spṛśati pāpaṃ kriyamāṇas tu nārada
garuḍapurāṇe
tulasīmṛttikāpuṇḍraṃ yaḥ karoti dine dine
tasyāvalokanāt pāpaṃ yāti varṣakṛtaṃ nṛṇām
tasyopariṣṭād bhagavannirmālyam anulepanam
tathaiva dhāryam evaṃ hi trividhaṃ tilakaṃ smṛtam
tato nārāyaṇīṃ mudrāṃ dhārayet prītaye hareḥ
matsyakūrmādicihnāni cakrādīny āyudhāni ca
smṛtau
aṅkitaḥ śaṅkhacakrābhyām ubhayor bāhumūlayoḥ
samarcayeddhariṃ nityaṃ nānyathā pūjanaṃ bhavet
ādityapurāṇe
śaṅkhacakrordhvapuṇḍrādirahitaṃ brāhmaṇādhamam
gardabhaṃ tu samāropya rājā rāṣṭrāt pravāsayet
gāruḍe śrībhagavaduktau
sarvakarmādhikāraś ca śucīnām eva coditaḥ
śucitvaṃ ca vijānīyān madīyāyudhadhāraṇāt
pādme cottarakhaṇḍe
śaṅkhacakrādibhiś cihnair vipraḥ priyatamair hareḥ
rahitaḥ sarvadharmebhyaḥ pracyuto narakaṃ vrajet
śrutau ca yajuḥkaṭhaśākhāyām
dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraḥ kutacakradhārī viṣṇuṃ paraṃ dhyāyati yo mahātmā
svareṇa mantreṇa sadā hṛdi sthitaṃ parātparaṃ yan mahato mahāntam
atharvaṇi ca
ebhir vayam urukramasya cihnair aṅkitā loke subhagā bhavema
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ ye gacchanti lāñchitāḥ
ata eva brahmapurāṇe
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sammānaṃ na karoti yaḥ
dvādaśābdārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ cāphalayopagacchati
skānde śrīsanatkumāramārkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde
yo viṣṇubhakto viprendra śaṅkhacakrādicihnitaḥ
sa yāti viṣṇulokaṃ vai dāhapralayavarjitam
tatra vānyatra ca
nārāyaṇāyudhair nityaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya vigraham
pāpakoṭiyuktasya tasya kiṃ kurute yamaḥ
śaṅkhoddhāre tu yat proktaṃ vasatāṃ varṣakoṭibhiḥ
tat phalaṃ likhite śaṅkhe pratyahaṃ dakṣiṇe bhuje
yat phalaṃ puṣkare nityaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣadarśane
śaṅkhopari kṛte padme tat phalaṃ samavāpnuyāt
vāme bhuje gadā yasya likhitā dṛśyate kalau
gadādharo gayāpuṇyaṃ pratyahaṃ tasya yacchati
yac cānandapure proktaṃ cakrasvāmīsamīpataḥ
gadādhollikhite cakre tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇadarśane
śrībhagavaduktau
yaḥ punaḥ kalikāle tu matpurīsambhavāṃ mṛdam
matsyakūrmādikāṃ cihnaṃ gṛhītvā kurute naraḥ
dehe tasya praviṣṭo 'haṃ jānantu tridaśottamāḥ
tasya me nāntaraṃ kiṃcit kartavyaṃ śreya icchatā
mamāvatāracihnāni dṛśyante yasya vigrahe
martyair martyo na vijñeyaḥ sa nūnaṃ māmakī tanūḥ
pāpaṃ sukṛtarūpaṃ tu jāyate tasya dehinaḥ
mamāyudhāni tasyāṅge likhitāni kalau yuge
ubhābhyām api cihnābhyāṃ yo 'ṅkito matsyamudrayā
kūrmayāpi svakaṃ tejo nikṣiptaṃ tasya vigrahe
śaṅkhaṃ ca padmaṃ ca gadāṃ rathāṅgaṃ matsyaṃ ca kūrmaṃ racitaṃ svadehe
karoti nityaṃ sukṛtasya vṛddhiṃ pāpakṣayaṃ janmaśatārjitasya
tatraiva śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkakavacaṃ durbhedyaṃ devadānavaiḥ
adṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śatrūṇāṃ rakṣasām api
lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī durgā sāvitrī harivallabhā
nityaṃ tasya vased dehe yasya śaṅkhāṅkitā tanuḥ
gaṅgā gayā kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ puṣkarādi ca
nityaṃ tasya sadā tiṣṭhed yasya padāṅkitaṃ vapuḥ
yasya kaumodakīcihnaṃ bhuje vāme kalipriya
pratyahaṃ tatra draṣṭavyo gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamaḥ
savye kare gadādhastād rathāṅgaṃ tiṣṭhate yadi
kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ tatra trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
trayo 'gnayas trayo devā viṣṇos trīṇi padāni ca
nivasanti sadā yasya yasya dehe sudarśanam
kiṃca
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitā mudrā yasya nārāyaṇī kare
ūrdhvalokādhikārī ca sa jñeyas tridaśāṃ patiḥ
kṛṣṇamudrāprayuktas tu daivaṃ pitryaṃ karoti yaḥ
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ pratyahaṃ cākṣayaṃ bhavet
pīḍayanti na tatraiva grahā ṛkṣāṇi rāśayaḥ
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī kare
vārāhe śrīsanatkumāroktau
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkitaṃ dehaṃ gopīcandanamṛtsnayā
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu sa gatvā kiṃ kariṣyati
yadā yasya prapaśyeta dehaṃ śaṅkhādicihnitam
tadā tasya jagatsvāmī tuṣṭo harati pātakam
bhavate yasya dehe tu ahorātraṃ dine dine
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaṃ likhitaṃ so 'cyutaḥ svayam
nārāyaṇāyudhair yuktaṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ kalau yuge
kurute puṇyakarmāṇi merutulyāni tāni vai
śaṅkhādināṅkito bhaktyā śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kurute dvija
vidhihīnaṃ tu sampūrṇaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu gayāsamam
yathāgnir dahate kāṣṭhaṃ vāyunā prerito bhṛśam
tathā dahyanti pāpāni dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇāyudhāni vai
brāhmye śrībrahmanāradasaṃvāde
viṣṇunāmāṅkitāṃ mudrām aṣṭākṣarasamanvitām
śaṅkhādikāyudhādikair yuktāṃ svarṇarūpyamayīm api
dhatte bhāgavato yas tu kalikāle viśeṣataḥ
prahlādasya samokṣeyo nānyathā kalavallabha
kiṃca
śaṅkhāṅkitatanur vipro bhuṅkte yasya ca veśmani
tadannaṃ svayam aśnāti pitṛbhiḥ saha keśavaḥ
kṛṣṇāyudhāṅkito yas tu śmaśāne mriyate yadi
prayāge yā gatiḥ proktā sā gatis tasya nārada
kṛṣṇāyudhaiḥ kalau nityaṃ maṇḍitaṃ yasya vigraham
tatrāśrayaṃ prakurvanti vividhā vāsavādayaḥ
yaḥ karoti hareḥ pūjāṃ kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkito naraḥ
aparādhasahasrāṇi nityaṃ harati keśavaḥ
kṛtvā kāṣṭhamayaṃ bimbaṃ kṛṣṇaśastrais tu cihnitam
yo hy aṅkayati cātmānaṃ tatsamo nāsti vaiṣṇavaḥ
pāṣaṇḍapatitavrātyair nāstikālāpapātakaiḥ
na lipyate kalikṛtaiḥ kṛṣṇaśastrāṅkito naraḥ
kiṃca
aṣṭākṣarāṅkitā mudrā yasya dhātumayī bhavet
śaṅkhapadmādibhir yuktā pūjyate'sau surāsuraiḥ
dhṛtā nārāyaṇī mudrā prahlādena purā kṛte
vibhīṣaṇena balinā dhruveṇa ca śukena ca
māndhātṛṇāmbarīṣeṇa mārkaṇḍapramukhair dvijaiḥ
śaṅkhādicihnitaiḥ śastrair dehe kṛtvā kalipriya
ārādhya keśavāt prāptaṃ samīhitaphalaṃ mahat
kiṃca
gopīcandanamṛtsnāyā likhitaṃ yasya vigrahe
śaṅkhapadmādicakraṃ vā tasya dehe vaseddhariḥ
tatraiva śrīsanatkumāroktau
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehaṃ śaṅkhādicihnitam
dhātrīphalakṛtā mālā tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavā
dvādaśākṣaramantrais tu niyuktāni kalevare
āyudhāni ca viprasya matsamaḥ sa ca vaiṣṇavaḥ
kiṃca
yasya nārāyaṇī mudrā dehe śaṅkhādi cihnitā
sarvāṅgaṃ cihnitaṃ yasya śastrair nārāyaṇodbhavaiḥ
praveśo nāsti pāpasya kavacaṃ tasya vaiṣṇavam
anyatra ca
ebhir bhāgavataiś cihnaiḥ kalikāle dvijātayaḥ
bhavanti martyaloke te śāpānugrahakārakāḥ
gautamīye
cakraṃ ca dakṣiṇe bāhau śaṅkhaṃ vāme'pi dakṣiṇe
gadāṃ vāme gadādhastāt punaś cakraṃ ca dhārayet
śaṅkhopari tathā padmaṃ punaḥ padmaṃ ca dakṣiṇe
khaḍgaṃ vakṣasi cāpaṃ ca saśaraṃ śīrṣṇi dhārayet
iti pañcāyudhāny ādau dhārayed vaiṣṇavo janaḥ
matsyaṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste kūrmaṃ vāmakare tathā
tathā coktaṃ
dakṣiṇe tu bhuje vipro vibhṛṣād vai sudarśanam
matsyaṃ padmaṃ cāpare'tha śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ gadās tathā
sāmpradāyikaśiṣṭānām ācārāc ca yathāruci
śaṅkhacakrādicihnāni sarveṣv aṅgeṣu dhārayet
bhaktyā nijeṣṭadevasya dhārayel lakṣaṇāny api
cakraśaṅkhau ca dhāryate saṃmiśrāv eva kaiścana
śrīgopīcandanenaivaṃ cakrādīni budho 'nvaham
dhārayecchayanādau tu taptāni kila tāni hi
dvādaśāraṃ tu ṣaṭkoṇaṃ valayatrayasaṃyutam
cakraṃ syād dakṣiṇāvartaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca śrīhareḥ smṛtaḥ
gadāpadmādikaṃ lokasiddham eva mataṃ budhaiḥ
mudrā vā bhagavannāmāṅkitā vāṣṭākṣarādibhiḥ
tataḥ kṛṣṇārpitā mālā dhārayet tulasīdalaiḥ
padmākṣais tulasīkāṣṭhaiḥ phalair dhātryāś ca nirmitāḥ
dhārayet tulasīkāṣṭhabhūṣaṇāni ca vaiṣṇavaḥ
mastake karṇayor bāhvoḥ karayoś ca yathāruci
skānde
saṃnivedyaiva haraye tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavām
mālāṃ paścāt svayaṃ dhatte sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ
haraye nārpayed yas tu tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavām
mālāṃ dhatte svayaṃ mūḍhaḥ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam
kṣālitāṃ pañcagavyena mūlamantreṇa mantritām
gāyatryā cāṣṭa kṛtvā vai mantritāṃ dhūpayec ca tām
vidhivat parayā bhaktyā sadyojātena pūjayet
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūte māle kṛṣṇajanapriye
bibharmi tvām ahaṃ kaṇṭhe kuru māṃ kṛṣṇavallabham
yathā tvaṃ vallabhā viṣṇor nityaṃ viṣṇujanapriyā
tathā māṃ kuru deveśi nityaṃ viṣṇujanapriyam
dāne lādhātur uddiṣṭo lāsi māṃ harivallabhe
bhaktebhyaś ca samastebhyas tena mālā nigadyase
evaṃ samprārthya vidhivan mālāṃ kṛṣṇagale'rpitām
dhārayed vaiṣṇavo yo vai sa gacched vaiṣṇavaṃ padam
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
dhātrīphalakṛtāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ yo vahen na hi
vaiṣṇavo na sa vijñeyo viṣṇupūjārato yadi
gāruḍe
dhārayanti na ye mālāṃ haitukāḥ pāpabuddhayaḥ
narakān na nivartante dagdhāḥ kopāgninā hareḥ
ata eva skānde
na jahyāt tulasīmālāṃ dhātrīmālāṃ viśeṣataḥ
mahāpātakasaṃhantrīṃ dharmakāmārthadāyinīm
agastyasaṃhitāyām
nirmālyatulasīmālāyukto yaś cārcayeddharim
yad yat karoti tat sarvam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet
nāradīye
ye kaṇṭhalagnatulasīnalinākṣamālā ye vā lalāṭaphalke lasadūrdhvapuṇḍrāḥ
ye bāhumūlaparicihnitaśaṅkhacakrās te vaiṣṇavā bhuvanam āśu pavitrayanti
kiṃca
bhujayugam api cihnair aṅkitaṃ yasya viṣṇoḥ paramapuruṣanāmnāṃ kīrtanaṃ yasya vāci
ṛjutaram api puṇḍraṃ mastake yasya kaṇṭhe sarasijamaṇimālā yasya tasyāsmi dāsaḥ
viṣṇudharmottare śrībhagavaduktau
tulasīkāṣṭhamālāṃ ca kaṇṭhasthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ
apy aśauco 'py anācāro mām evaiti na saṃśayaḥ
skānde
dhātrīphalakṛtā mālā tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavā
dṛśyate yasya dehe tu sa vai bhāgavatottamaḥ
tulasīdalajāṃ mālāṃ kaṇṭhasthāṃ vahate tu yaḥ
viṣṇūttīrṇā viśeṣeṇa sa namasyo divaukasām
tulasīdalajā mālā dhātrīphalakṛtāpi ca
dadāti pāpināṃ muktiṃ kiṃ punar viṣṇusevinām
tatraiva kārttikaprasaṅge
yaḥ punas tulasīmālāṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhe janārdanam
pūjayet puṇyam āpnoti pratipuṣpaṃ gavāyutam
yāval luṭhati kaṇṭhasthā dhātrīmālā narasya hi
tāvat tasya śarīre tu prītyā luṭhati keśavaḥ
spṛśec ca yāni lomāni dhātrīmālā kalau nṛṇām
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi vasate keśavālaye
yāvad dināni vahate dhātrīmālāṃ kalau naraḥ
tāvadyugasahasrāṇi vaikuṇṭhe vasatir bhavet
mālāyugmaṃ vahed yas tu dhātrītulasisaṃbhavam
vahate kaṇṭhadeśe tu kalpakoṭiṃ divaṃ vaset
gāruḍe ca mārkaṇḍeyoktau
tulasīdalajāṃ mālāṃ kṛṣṇottīrṇā vahet tu yaḥ
patre patre'śvamedhānāṃ daśānāṃ labhate phalam
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ
phalaṃ yacchati daitāriḥ pratyahaṃ dvārakodbhavam
nivedya viṣṇave mālāṃ tulasīkāṣṭhasambhavam
vahate yo naro bhaktyā tasya vai nāsti pātakam
sadā prītamanās tasya kṛṣṇa devakīnandanaḥ
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ yo mālāṃ vahate naraḥ
prāyaścittaṃ na tasyāsti nāśaucaṃ tasya vigrahe
tulasīkāṣṭhasambhūtāṃ śiraso yasya bhūṣaṇam
bāhvoḥ kare ca martyasya dehe tasya sadā hariḥ
tulasīkāṣṭhamālābhir bhūṣitaḥ puṇyam ācaret
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca kṛtaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ kalau
tulasīkāṣṭhamālāṃ tu pretarājasya dūtakāḥ
dṛṣṭvā naśyanti dūreṇa vātoddhūtaṃ yathā dalam
tulasīkāṣṭhamālābhir bhūṣito bhramate yadi
duḥsvapnaṃ durnimittaṃ ca na bhayaṃ śastrajaṃ kvacit
sandhyopāstyādikaṃ karma tataḥ kuryāt yathāvidhi
kṛṣṇapādodakenaiva tatra devāditarpaṇam
śirasā viṣṇunirmālyaṃ pādodenāpi tarpaṇam
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca vaiṣṇavais tu samaṃ matam
sandhyopāstau ca vaśiṣṭhavacanam
gṛhe tv ekaguṇā sandhyā goṣṭhe daśaguṇā smṛtā
śatasāhasrikā nadyām anantā viṣṇusannidhau
pūjayiṣyaṃs tataḥ kṛṣṇam ādau saṃnihitaṃ gurum
praṇamya pūjayed bhaktyā dattvā kiṃcid upāyanam
smṛtimahārṇave
riktapāṇir na paśyeta rājānaṃ bhiṣajaṃ gurum
nopāyanakaraḥ putraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhṛtyaṃ nirīkṣayet
kiṃca śrībhagavaduktau
prathamaṃ tu guruṃ pūjya tataś caiva mamārcanam
kurvan siddhim avāpnoti hy anyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet
śrīnāradena ca
gurau saṃnihite yas tu pūjayed anyam agrataḥ
sa durgatim avāpnoti pūjanaṃ tasya niṣphalam
śrutiṣu
yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau
tasyaite kathitā hy arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ
ekādaśaskandhe śrībhagavaduktau
ācāryaṃ māṃ vijānīyān nāvamanyeta karhicit
na martyabuddhyāsūyeta sarvadevamayo guruḥ
daśamaskandhe ca
nāham ijyāprajātibhyāṃ tapasopaśamena ca
tuṣyeyaṃ sarvabhūtātmā guruśuśrūṣayā yathā
saptamaskandhe
yasya sākṣād bhagavati jñānadīpaprade gurau
martyāsaddhīḥ śrutaṃ tasya sarvaṃ kuñjaraśaucavat
anyatrāpi
sādhakasya gurau bhaktiṃ mandīkurvanti devatāḥ
yan no 'tītya vrajed viṣṇuṃ śiṣyo bhaktyā gurau dhruvan
manusmṛtau
ajño bhavati vai bālaḥ pitā bhavati mantradaḥ
ajñaṃ hi bālam ity āhuḥ pitety eva tu mantradam
kiṃca
gurur brahmā gurur viṣṇur gurur devo maheśvaraḥ
gurur eva paraṃ brahma tasmāt sampūjayet sadā
vāmanakalpe
yo mantraḥ sa guruḥ sākṣāt yo guruḥ sa hariḥ smṛtaḥ
gurur yasya bhavet tuṣṭas tasya tuṣṭo hariḥ svayam
guroḥ samāsane naiva na caivoccāsane vaset
viṣṇurahasye
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena yathāvidhi tathā gurum
abhedenārcayet yas tu sa muktiphalam āpnuyāt
viṣṇudharme śrībhāgavate ca hariścandrasya
guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ nāma sarvadharmottamottamam
tasmād dharmāt paro dharmaḥ pavitraṃ naiva vidyate
kāmakrodhādikaṃ yad yad ātmano 'niṣṭakāraṇam
etat sarvaṃ gurau bhaktyā puruṣo hy añjasā jayet
pādme
pitur ādhikyabhāvena ye'rcayanti guruṃ sadā
bhavanty atithayo loke brahmaṇas te viśāṃ vara
tatraiva devahūtistutau
bhaktir yathā harau me'sti tadvan niṣṭhā gurau yadi
mamāsti tena satyena svaṃ darśayatu me hariḥ
ādityapurāṇe
avidyo vā savidyo vā gurur eva janārdanaḥ
mārgastho vāpy amārgastho gurur eva sadā gatiḥ
anyatra ca
harau ruṣṭe gurus trātā gurau ruṣṭe na kaścana
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena gurum eva prasādayet
brahmavaivarte
api ghnantaḥ śapanto vā viruddhā api ye kruddhāḥ
guravaḥ pūjanīyās te gṛhaṃ natvā nayeta tān
tat ślāghyaṃ janma dhanyaṃ tat dinaṃ puṇyātha nāḍikā
yasyāṃ guruṃ praṇamate samupāsya tu bhaktitaḥ
upadeṣṭāram āmnāyagataṃ pariharanti ye
tān mṛtān api kravyādāḥ kṛtaghnān nopabhuñjate
bodhaḥ kaluṣitas tena daurātmyaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam
gurur yena parityaktas tena tyaktaḥ purā hariḥ
anyatra ca
pratipadya guruṃ yas tu mohād vipratipadyate
sa kalpakoṭiṃ narake pacyate puruṣādhamaḥ
pañcarātre
avaiṣṇavopadiṣṭena mantreṇa nirayaṃ vrajet
punaś ca vidhinā samyag grāhayed vaiṣṇavād guroḥ
agastyasaṃhitāyāṃ
ye gurvājñāṃ na kurvanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ
na teṣāṃ narakakleśanistāro munisattama
yaiḥ śiṣyaiḥ śaśvad ārādhyā guravo hy avamānitāḥ
putramitrakalatrādisampadbhyaḥ pracyutā hi te
adhikṣipya guruṃ mohāt paruṣaṃ pravadanti ye
śūkaratvaṃ bhavaty eva teṣāṃ janmaśateṣv api
ye gurudrohiṇo mūḍhāḥ satataṃ pāpakāriṇaḥ
teṣāṃ ca yāvat sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ syān na saṃśayaḥ
ataḥ prāg gurum abhyarcya kṛṣṇabhāvena buddhimān
tryavarān asamān kuryāt praṇāmān daṇḍapātavat
ata eva kaurme śrīvyāsagītāyām
vyatyastapāṇinā kāryam upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ
savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ
atha śrīgurupādānāṃ prāpyānujñāṃ ca sādhakaḥ
prāk saṃskṛtaṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyan pāduke tyajet
tathā cāpastambe
agnyāgāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe devabrāhmaṇasannidhau
jape bhojanakāle ca pāduke parivarjayet
tataḥ śrībhagavatpūjāmandirasyāṅganaṃ gataḥ
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca dvirācamanam ācaret
tathā ca mārkaṇḍeye
devārcanādikāryāṇi tathā gurvabhivādanam
kurvīta samyag ācamya tadvad eva bhujikriyām
iti śrīgopālabhaṭṭavilikhite śrībhagavadbhaktivilāse śrīvaiṣṇavālaṅkāro nāma caturtho vilāsaḥ
śrīcaitanyaprabhuṃ vande bālo 'pi yadanugrahāt
taren nānāmatagrāhavyāptaṃ pūjākramārṇavam
sanātanaḥ
śrīcaitanyāya namaḥ
bālo 'jñaḥ
pakṣe śiśuḥ
nānāvidhamatāny eva grāhas tair vyāptam
pūjāyāḥ kramo vidhiḥ
vidhyanukramo vā sa evārṇavas tam
śrīmadgopāladevasyāṣṭādaśākṣarayantrataḥ
likhyate'rcāvidhir gūḍhaḥ kramadīpikayekṣitaḥ
sanātanaḥ
aṣṭādaśākṣaramantreṇa yo 'rcāvidhiḥ pūjāprakāraḥ sa likhyate
yadyapi daśākṣarādināpi pūjāvidhau bhedo nāsti tathāpi nyāsādibhedāpekṣayā tathā likhitam
gūḍho 'pi kramadīpikayā śrīkeśavācāryaviracitayā īkṣitaḥ darśitaḥ san
ataḥ kramadīpikoktānusāreṇa lekhya iti bhāvaḥ
āgamoktena mārgeṇa bhagavān brāhmaṇair api
sadaiva pūjyo 'to lekhyaḥ prāya āgamiko vidhiḥ
tathā ca viṣṇuyāmale
kṛte śrutyuktamārgaḥ syāt tretāyāṃ smṛtibhāvitaḥ
dvāpare tu purāṇoktaḥ kalāv āgamasambhavaḥ
aśuddhāḥ śūdrākalpā hi brāhmaṇāḥ kalisambhavāḥ
teṣām āgamamārgeṇa śuddhir na śrautavartmanā
sanātanaḥ
teṣām āgamamārgeṇa śrautavartmanety anena tair api āgamikavidhinaiva pūjā kāryeti bhāvaḥ
tathā caikādaśaskandhe nānātantravidhānena kalāv api tathā śṛṇu iti
tatra śrīdharasvāmipādāḥ
nānātantravidhāneneti kalau tantramārgasya prādhānyaṃ darśayati iti
śrīkṛṣṇadvāradevebhyo dattvā pādyādikaṃ tataḥ
gandhapuṣpair arcayet tān yathāsthānaṃ yathākramam
sanātanaḥ
tān śrīkṛṣṇadvāradevān praṇavādicaturthyantaṃ devanāma namo'ntakam ity agre lekhyatvād atraivaṃ prayogaḥ śrīkṛṣṇadvāradevatābhyo namaḥ
anena mantreṇa pādyārghyādikaṃ dattvā gandhādibhiḥ punar viśeṣeṇa pūjayed ity arthaḥ
evam agre'pi saparivārebhyaḥ śrīkṛṣṇapārṣadebhyo namaḥ ityādi prayogo draṣṭavyaḥ
dvārāgre saparīvārān bhūpīṭhe kṛṣṇapārṣadān
tadagre garuḍaṃ dvārasyordhve dvāraśriyaṃ yajet
prāgdvārobhayapārśve tu yajec caṇḍapracaṇḍakau
dvāre ca dakṣiṇe dhātṛvidhātārau ca paścime
jayaṃ ca vijayaṃ caiva balaṃ prabalam uttare
dvandvaśastv evam abhyarcya dehalyāṃ vāstupuruṣam
sanātanaḥ
evaṃ sāmānyena sarveṣām eva pūjāvidhir likhitaḥ
idānīṃ yathāsthānaṃ yathākramam iti yal likhitaṃ tad eva vivicya likhati dvārāgra iti dvārābhyām
tatrāpy ādau dvārasyāgre yat bhūrūpaṃ pīṭhaṃ tatra samastaparivārānvitān śrīkṛṣṇapārṣadān yajet pūjayet
anantaraṃ tasya dvārasyāgre garuḍaṃ
yadyapi dvāraśriyo 'rcanaṃ prabalārcanānantaram eva kramadīpikāyām uktam tathāpi iṣṭveti kṭvāpratyayena caṇḍādipūjātaḥ pūrvakāla eveti bodhitam
tathaiva sadācārāt
kiṃca dvandva ity agre likhanāt caṇḍapracaṇḍābhyāṃ namaḥ ity evaṃ yugmatvena prayogo jñeyaḥ
dvārāntaḥpārśvayor gaṅgāṃ yamunāṃ ca tato 'rcayet
tatpārśvayoḥ śaṅkhanidhiṃ tathā padmanidhiṃ yajet
sanātanaḥ
dvārasyāntaḥ abhyantare tatpārśvadvaye tayor gaṅgāyamunayoḥ pārśvadvaye
gaṇeśaṃ mandirasyāgnikoṇe durgāṃ ca nairṛte
vāṇīṃ vāyavya aiśāne kṣetrapālaṃ tathārcayet
sanātanaḥ
āgneye koṇe gaṇeśam arcayet
tathā coktaṃ kramadīpikāyām
parivārārāḥ kṛtāḥ sarve punaḥ śrīviṣṇupārṣadāḥ
dvārāgrābalipīṭhe 'rcyāḥ pakṣīndraś ca tadagrataḥ
caṇḍapracaṇḍau prāg dhātṛvidhātārau ca dakṣiṇe
jayaḥ savijayaḥ paścād balaḥ prabala uttare
ūrdhve dvāraśriyaṃ ceṣṭvā dvāry etān yugmaśo 'rcayet
pūjyo vāstupumāṃs tatra tatra dvāḥpīṭhamadhyataḥ
dvārāntaḥpārśvayor arcyā gaṅgā ca yamunā nadī
koṇeṣu vighnaṃ durgāṃ ca vāṇīṃ kṣetre samarcayet
dvāḥśākhām āśrayan vāmāṃ saṃkocyāṅgāni dehalīm
aspṛṣṭvā praviśed veśma nyasyan prāg dakṣiṇaṃ padam
sanātanaḥ
vāmāṃ svavāmabhāgavartinīṃ dvāraśākhāṃ āśrayan īṣat spṛṣad nijāṅgāni saṃkocya dehalīm aspṛṣṭvā na laṅghayitvety arthaḥ
dakṣiṇaṃ padaṃ prāk ādau nyasyan
dakṣiṇapādanyāsakrameṇety arthaḥ
veśma śrībhagavanmandiraṃ harer gehaṃ pravekṣyann iti pūrvalikhanāt
praviśet tanmadhyaṃ śanaiḥ pūjako gacchet
tathā ca sāradātilake kiṃcit
spṛśan vāmaśākhāṃ dehalīṃ laṅghayan guruḥ
aṅgaṃ saṃkocayann antaḥ praviśed dakṣiṇāṅghriṇā
sanātanaḥ
gurur iti dīkṣāvidhānoktaḥ
tanmāhātmyaṃ ca haribhaktisudhodaye
praviśann ālayaṃ viṣṇor arcanārthaṃ subhaktimān
na bhūyaḥ praviśan mātuḥ kukṣikārāgṛhaṃ sudhīḥ
nairṛte vāstupuruṣaṃ brahmāṇam api pūjayet
āsanastho yajet tāṃs tān anyatra bhagavadgṛhāt
tatpūjāmantraś coktaḥ
praṇavādicaturthyantaṃ devanāma namo'ntakam
pūjāmantram idaṃ proktaṃ sarvatrārcanakarmaṇi
atha kṛṣṇāgratas tiṣṭhan kṛtvā digbandhanaṃ kṣipet
puṣpākṣatān samastāsu dikṣu tatroktamantrataḥ
tataś cāsanamantreṇābhimantryābhyarcya cāsanam
tasminn upaviśet padmāsanena svastikena vā
tatra kṛṣṇārcakaḥ prāyo divase prāṅmukho bhavet
udaṅmukho rajanyāṃ tu sthiramūrtiś ca sammukhaḥ
tatra ca ekādaśaskandhe
āsīnaḥ prāg udagvārcet sthirāyāṃ tv atha sammukhaḥ
āsanamantrasya merupṛṣṭha ṛṣiḥ sutalaṃ chandaḥ
kūrmo devatā āsanābhimantreṇa viniyogaḥ
pṛthvi tvayā dhṛtā lokā devi tvaṃ viṣṇunā dhṛtā
tvaṃ ca dhāraya māṃ nityaṃ pavitraṃ kuru cāsanam
nāradapañcarātre
vaṃśāśmadārudharaṇītṛṇapallavanirmitam
varjayed āsanaṃ vidvān dāridryavyādhiduḥkhadam
kṛṣṇājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā nānyad āsanam iṣyate
anyatra ca
kṛṣṇājinaṃ vyāghracarma kauśeyaṃ vetranirmitam
vastrājinaṃ kambalaṃ vā kalpayed āsanaṃ mṛdu
nāradapañcarātre
vaṃśād āhur daridratvaṃ pāṣāṇe vyādhisambhavam
dharaṇyāṃ duḥkhasambhūtiṃ daurbhāgyaṃ dāravāsane
tṛṇāsane yaśohāniṃ pallave cittavibhramam
darbhāsane vyādhināśaṃ kambalaṃ duḥkhamocanam
kiṃca śrībhagavadgītāsu
śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥ
nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājinakuśottaram
yathoktam upaviśyātha sampradāyānusārataḥ
śaṅkhādipūjāsambhārān nyaset tattatpadeṣu tān
svasya vāmāgrataḥ śaṅkhaṃ sādhāraṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ
tatraivārghyādipātrāṇi nyasyec ca dvāri bhāgaśaḥ
tulasīgandhapuṣpādibhājanāni ca dakṣiṇe
vāme ca sthāpayet pārśve kalasaṃ pūrṇam ambhasā
dakṣiṇe ghṛtadīpaṃ ca tailadīpaṃ ca vāmataḥ
sambhārānaparān nyaset svadṛṣṭiviṣaye pade
karaprakṣālanārthaṃ ca pātram ekaṃ svapṛṣṭhataḥ
devīpurāṇe
nānāvicitrarūpāṇi puṇḍarīkākṛtīni ca
śaṅkhanīlotpalābhāni pātrāṇi parikalpayet
ratnādiracitāny eva kāñcīmūlayutāni ca
yathāśobhaṃ yathālābhaṃ tathā pātrāṇi kārayet
kiṃca
haṃsapātreṇa sarvāṇi cepsitāni labhen mune
arghyaṃ dattvā tathā raupyeṇāyurājyaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet
tāmrapātreṇa saubhāgyaṃ dharmaṃ mṛṇmayasambhavam
vārāhe
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ kāṃsyaṃ yena dīyate bhājanam
tān sarvān samparityajya tāmraṃ tu mama rocate
pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ yo maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam
viśuddhānāṃ śuciṃ caiva tāmraṃ saṃsāramokṣaṇam
dīkṣitānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ mama karmaparāyaṇaḥ
sadā tāmreṇa kartavyam evaṃ bhūmi mama priyam
kecic ca tāmrapātreṣu gavyāder yogadoṣataḥ
tāmrātiriktam icchanti madhuparkasya bhājanam
tathaiva śaṅkham evārghyapātram icchanti kecana
śaṅkhe kṛtvā tu pānīyaṃ sapuṣpaṃ salilākṣatam
arghyaṃ dadāti devasyety evaṃ skānde'bhidhānataḥ
maṅgalārthaṃ ca kalasaṃ sajalaṃ karakānvitam
phalādisahitaṃ divyaṃ nyased bhagavato 'grataḥ
tathā ca skānde
kumbhaṃ sakarakaṃ divyaṃ phalakarpūrasaṃyutam
nyased arcanakāle tu kṛṣṇasyātīva vallabham
kiṃca
sanīraṃ ca sakarpūraṃ kumbhaṃ kṛṣṇāya yo nyaset
kalpaṃ tasya na pāpekṣāṃ kurvanti prapitāmahāḥ
prakṣiped arghyapātre tu gandhapuṣpākṣatān yavān
kuśāgratiladūrvāś ca siddhārthān api sādhakaḥ
kecic cātra jalādīni dravyāṇy aṣṭau vadanti hi
yata uktaṃ bhaviṣye
āpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi dadhyakṣatatilas tathā
yavāḥ siddhārthakāś caivam arghyo 'ṣṭāṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
pādyapātre ca kamalaṃ dūrvā śyāmākam eva ca
nikṣiped viṣṇupatrīṃ cety evaṃ dravyacatuṣṭayam
tathaivācamanīyārthaṃ pātre dravyatrayaṃ budhaḥ
jātīphalaṃ lavaṅgaṃ ca kakkolam api nikṣipet
madhuparkīyapātre ca gavyaṃ dadhi payo ghṛtam
madhukhaṇḍam apīty evaṃ nikṣiped dravyapañcakam
kecit trīṇy eva pātre'smin dravyāṇīcchanti sādhavaḥ
yata uktaṃ śrīviṣṇudharme
ghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā kṣaudraṃ madhuparko vidhīyate
ādivārāhe ca
dadhisarpir madhusamaṃ pātre audumbare mama
madhunas tu alābhe tu guḍena saha miśrayet
ghṛtasyālābhe suśroṇi lājaiś ca saha miśrayet
tathā dadhno 'py alābhe tu kṣīreṇa saha miśrayet
teṣām abhāve puṣpādi tattadbhāvanayā kṣipet
nāradas tv āha vimalenodakenaiva pūryate
mūlena pātreṇaikena aṣṭakṛtvo 'bhimantrayet
kuryāc ca teṣāṃ pātrāṇāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ cakramudrayā
pūjām ārabhamāṇo hi yathoktāsanam āsthitaḥ
paṭhen maṅgalaśāntiṃ tāṃ yārcane saṃmatā satām
oṃ bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devā bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhir yajatrā
sthirair aṅgais tuṣṭuvāṃsas tanubhir vyaśema devahitaṃ yad āyuḥ
svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ
svasti naḥ pūṣā viśvadevāḥ
svasti nas tārkṣo 'riṣṭanemiḥ
svasti no bṛhaspatir dadhātu
paṭhan oṃ śāntiḥ śrīkṛṣṇapādapadmārādhaneṣu śāntir bhavatu
apasarpantu te bhūtā ye bhūtā bhuvi saṃsthitāḥ
ye bhūtā vighnakartāras te naśyantu śivājñayā
ity udīryāstramantreṇa vāmapādasya pārṣṇinā
ghātais tribhir budho vighnān bhaumān sarvān nivārayet
āntarīkṣāṃś ca tenaivordhvordhvatālatrayeṇa hi
nirasyotsārayed divyān māntriko divyadṛṣṭitaḥ
tataḥ kṛtāñjalir vāme śrīguruṃ paramaṃ gurum
parameṣṭhiguruṃ ceti named guruparamparām
gaṇeśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge durgām agre'tha pṛṣṭhataḥ
kṣetrapālaṃ named bhaktyā madhye cātmeṣṭadaivatam
tataś cāstreṇa saṃśodhya karau kurvīta tena hi
tālatrayaṃ diśāṃ bandham agniprākāram eva ca
śarīrākārabhūtānāṃ bhūtānāṃ yad viśodhanam
avyayabrahmasamparkād bhūtaśuddhir iyaṃ matā
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vinā kartur japahomādikāḥ kriyāḥ
bhavanti niṣphalāḥ sarvā yathāvidhy apy aniṣṭhitāḥ
karakacchapikāṃ kṛtvātmānaṃ buddhyā hṛdabjataḥ
śiraḥsahasrapatrābje paramātmani yojayet
pṛthivyādīni tattvāni tasmin līnāni bhāvayet
vāmahastaṃ tathottānam adho dakṣiṇabandhitam
karakacchapikā mudrā bhūtaśuddhau prakīrtitā
dehaṃ saṃśoṣya dagdhvedam āplāvyāmṛtavarṣataḥ
utpādya draḍhayitvā supratiṣṭhāṃ vidhinācaret
ātmānam evaṃ saṃśodhya nītvā kṛṣṇārcanārhatām
vātsalyāddhṛdgataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yaṣṭuṃ hṛt punar ānayet
tathā ca trailokyasaṃmohanatantre
nābhisthavāyunā dehaṃ sapāpaṃ śodhayed budhaḥ
vahninā hṛdayasthena dahet tac ca kalevaram
sahasrāre mahāpadme lalāṭasthe sthitaṃ vidhum
sampūrṇamaṇḍalaṃ śuddhaṃ cintayed amṛtātmakam
tasmād galitadhārābhiḥ plāvayed bhasmasād budhaḥ
ābhir varṇamayībhiś ca pañcabhūtātmakaṃ vapuḥ
pūrvavad bhāvayed devīm
kiṃcāgre
tatas tasmāt samākṛṣya praṇavena tu mantravit
tat tejo hṛdaye nyasya cintayed viṣṇum avyayam
kiṃ vā cintanamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāya tām
prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryāt sampradāyānusarataḥ
recaḥ ṣoḍaśamātrābhiḥ pūro dvātriṃśatā bhavet
catuḥṣaṣṭyā bhavet kumbha evaṃ syāt prāṇasaṃyamaḥ
virecya pavanaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkocya gudamaṇḍalam
pūrayitvā vidhānena svaśaktyā kumbhake sthitaḥ
tatra praṇavam abhyasyan bījaṃ vā mantram ūrdhvagam
ṛṣyādismaraṇaṃ kṛtvā kuryād dhyānam atandritaḥ
tad dhyānaṃ coktam
viṣṇuṃ bhāsvatkirīṭāṅgadavalayakalākalpahārodarāṅghriśroṇībhūṣaṃ savakṣomaṇimakaramahākuṇḍalāmṛṣṭagaṇḍam
hastodyacchaṅkhacakrāmbujagadam amalaṃ pītakauśeyavāsaṃ vidyotadbhāsam udyaddinakarasadṛśaṃ padmasaṃsthaṃ namāmi
kvacic ca
rudras tu recake brahmā pūrake dhyeyadevatā
śrīviṣṇuḥ kumbhake jñeyo dhyānasthānaṃ guror mukhāt
tathā hi
nābhisthāne pūrakeṇa cintayet kamalāsanam
brahmāṇaṃ raktagaurāṅgaṃ caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham
nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ hṛdi madhye pratiṣṭhitam
caturbhujaṃ mahātmānaṃ kumbhakena tu cintayet
recakenaiśvaraṃ dhyānaṃ lalāṭe sarvapāpaham
śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśaṃ kuryād vai nirmalaṃ budhaḥ
ekāntibhiś ca bhagavān sarvadevamayaḥ prabhuḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ priyajanopetaś cintanīyo hi sarvataḥ
pādme devahūtivikuṇḍalasaṃvāde
yamalokaṃ na paśyanti prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ
api duṣkṛtakarmāṇas tair eva hatakilbiṣāḥ
divase divase vaiśya prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍaśa
api brahmahaṇaṃ sākṣāt punanty aharahaḥ kṛtāḥ
tapāṃsi yāni tapyante vratāni niyamāś ca ye
gosahasrapradānaṃ ca prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ
ambubinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māse māse naraḥ pibet
saṃvatsaraśataṃ sāgraṃ prāṇāyāmas tu tatsamaḥ
pātakaṃ tu mahad yac ca tathā kṣudropapātakam
prāṇāyāmaiḥ kṣaṇāt sarvaṃ bhasmasāt kurute naraḥ
nyāsān vinā japaṃ prāhur āsuraṃ viphalaṃ budhāḥ
ato yathāsampradāyaṃ nyāsān kuryād yathāvidhi
ṛṣicchandodevatādi smṛtvādau mātṛkāmanoḥ
śirovaktrahṛdādau ca nyasya taddhyānam ācaret
tac coktam
pañcāśallipibhir vibhaktamukhadoḥpanmadhyavakṣaḥsthalīṃ bhāvanmaulinibaddhacandraśakalām āpīnatuṅgastanīm
mudrām akṣaguṇaṃ sudhāḍhyakalasaṃ vidyāṃ ca hastāmbujair bibhrāṇāṃ viśadaprabhāṃ trinayanāṃ vāgdevatām āśraye
akārādīn kṣakārāntān varṇānādau tu kevalān
lalāṭādiṣu cāṅgeṣu nyased vidvān yathākramam
tac ca vivicyoktam
lalāṭamukhabimbākṣiśrutighrāṇeṣu gaṇḍayoḥ
oṣṭhadantottamāṅgāsye doḥpatsandhyagrakeṣu ca
pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhato nābhau jaṭhare hṛdaye'ṃsake
kakudyase ca hṛtpūrvaṃ pāṇipādayuge tataḥ
jaṭharānanayor nyasen mātṛkārṇān yathākramam
sānusvārān visargāḍhyān sānusvāravisargakān
nyased bhūyo 'pi tān vidvān evaṃ vāracatuṣṭayam
kaṇṭhahṛnnābhiguhyeṣu pāyubhrūmadhyayos tathā
sthite ṣoḍaśapatrābje krameṇa dvādaśacchade
daśapatre ca ṣaṭpatre catuṣpattre dvipatrake
nyased ekaikapatrānte sabindvekaikam akṣaram
smṛtvā ṛṣyādikāṃ varṇān mūrtibhiḥ keśavādibhiḥ
kīrtyādibhiḥ śaktibhiś ca nyaset tān pūrvavat kramāt
nyasec caturthīn atyantā mūrtīḥ śaktīś ca yādibhiḥ
saptadhātūn prāṇajīvau krodham apy ātmane'ntakān
udyatpradyotanaśataruciṃ taptahemāvadānaṃ pārśvadvandve jaladhisutayā viśvadhātryā ca juṣṭam
nānāratnollasitavividhākalpam āpītavastraṃ viṣṇuṃ vande darakamalakaumodakīcakrapāṇim
prathamaṃ keśavo nārāyaṇaḥ paścāc ca mādhavaḥ
govindaś ca tathā viṣṇur madhusūdana eva ca
trivikramo vāmano 'tha śrīdharaś ca tataḥ param
ṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhas tato dāmodaras tathā
vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumno 'thāniruddhakaḥ
cakrī gadī tathā śārṅgī khaḍgī śaṅkhī halī tathā
musalī ca tathā śūlī pāśī caivāṅkuśī tathā
mukundo nandajaś caiva tathā nandī naras tathā
narakajiddhariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyaḥ sātvata eva ca
tataḥ śauris tathā śūras tataḥ paścāj janārdanaḥ
bhūdharo viśvamūrtiś ca vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
balo balānujo bālo vṛṣaghno vṛṣa eva ca
haṃso varāho vimalo nṛsiṃhaś ceti mūrtayaḥ
kīrtiḥ kāntis tuṣṭipuṣṭī dhṛtiḥ śāntiḥ kriyā dayā
medhā harṣā tathā śraddhā lajjā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī
prītī ratir jayā durgā prabhā satyā ca caṇḍikā
vāṇī vilāsinī caiva vijayā virajā tathā
viśvā ca vinadā caiva sunandā ca smṛtis tathā
ṛddhiḥ samṛddhiḥ śuddhiś ca buddhir mūrtir natiḥ kṣamā
ramomā kledinī klinnā vasudā vasudhā parā
parāyaṇā ca sūkṣmā ca sandhyā prajñā prabhā niśā
amoghā vidyutety ekapañcāśat śaktayo matāḥ
dadāty ayaṃ keśavādinyāso 'trākhilasampadam
amutrācyutasārūpyaṃ nayati nyāsamātrataḥ
tad uktaṃ
dhyātvaivaṃ paramapumāṃsam akṣarair yo vinyased dinam anu keśavādiyuktaiḥ
medhāyuḥsmṛtidhṛtikīrtikāntilakṣmīsaubhāgyaiś ciram upabṛṃhito bhavet saḥ
anyatra ca
keśavādir ayaṃ nyāso nyāsamātreṇa dehinaḥ
acyutatvaṃ dadāty eva satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
yaś ca kuryād imaṃ nyāsaṃ lakṣmībījapuraḥsaram
bhaktiṃ muktiṃ ca bhuktiṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca labhate'cirāt
tathā coktam
amum eva ramāpuraḥsaraṃ prabhajed yo manujo vidhiṃ budhaḥ
samupetya ramāṃ prathīyasīṃ punar ante haritāṃ vrajaty asau
makārādikakārāntavarṇair yuktaṃ sabindukaiḥ
namaḥ parāyeti pūrvam ātmane nama ity anu
nāma jīvāditattvānāṃ nyaset tattatpade kramāt
nyāsenānena loko hi bhavet pūjādhikāravān
tatrādau sakale nyasej jīvaprāṇau kalevare
hṛdaye matyahaṅkāramanāṃsīti trayaṃ tataḥ
śabdaṃ sparśaṃ tato rūpaṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca mastake
mukhe hṛdi ca guhye ca pādayoś ca yathākramam
śrotraṃ tvacaṃ dṛśaṃ jihvāṃ ghrāṇaṃ svasvapade tataḥ
vākpāṇipāyūpasthāni svasvapade tathā
ākāśavāyutejāṃsi jalaṃ pṛthvīṃ ca mūrdhani
vadane hṛdaye liṅge pādayoś ca yathākramam
hṛdi hṛtpuṇḍarīkaṃ ca dviṣaṭdvyaṣṭadaśādikam
kalāvyāpteti pūrvaṃ ca sūryacandrāgnimaṇḍalam
varṇaiḥ saha sarephaiś ca kramān nyaset sabindukaiḥ
vāsudevaṃ ṣakāreṇa parameṣṭhiyutaṃ ca ke
yakāreṇa mukhe saṅkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset pumanvitam
hṛdi nyasel lakāreṇa pradyumnaṃ viśvasaṃyutam
aniruddhaṃ nivṛttyāḍhyaṃ vakāreṇa ca guhyake
nārāyaṇaṃ ca sarvāḍhyaṃ lakāreṇaiva pādayoḥ
nṛsiṃhaṃ kopasaṃyuktaṃ tadbījenākhilātmani
tattvanyāso 'yam acirāt kṛṣṇasānnidhyakārakaḥ
tathā coktam
atattvavyāptyarūpasya tatprāpter hetunā punaḥ
tattvanyāsam iti prāhur nyāsatattvavido budhāḥ
yaḥ kuryāt tattvavinyāsaṃ sa pūto bhavati dhruvam
tadātmanānupraviśya bhagavān iha tiṣṭhati
yataḥ sa eva tattvāni sarvaṃ tasmin pratiṣṭhitam
prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān mūlamantraṃ japan kramāt
vārau dvau caturaḥ ṣaṭ ca recapūrakakumbhakaḥ
athavā recakādīṃs tān kuryād vārāṃs tu ṣoḍaśa
dvātriṃśac ca catuḥṣaṣṭhiṃ kāmabījaṃ japan kramāt
tathā ca kramadīpikāyām
recayen mārutaṃ dakṣayā dakṣiṇaḥ pūrayed vāmayā madhyanāḍyā punaḥ
dhārayed īritaṃ recakāditrayaṃ syāt kalādantavidyākhyamātrācyukam
sanātanaḥ
tad eva kramadīpikoktyā saṃvādayan tatraiva kiṃcid viśeṣaṃ ca darśayati recayed iti
dakṣayā dakṣiṇanāḍyā dakṣiṇaḥ vidvān janaḥ
madhyanāḍyā suṣumṇayā dhārayet
evaṃ recakapūrakakumbhakākhyaṃ trayaṃ syāt
recakādiṣu triṣu krameṇāvadhikālam āha kalāḥ ṣoḍaśa
dantā dvātriṃśat
vidyāś catuḥṣaṣṭis tattatsaṃkhyakamātrātmakam ity arthaḥ
mātrā cavāmāṅguṣṭhena vāmakaniṣṭhādyaṅgulīnāṃ pratyekaṃ parvatrayasamparkakālaḥ
vāmahastena vāmajānumaṇḍalasya prādakṣiṇyena sparśakālo vā
tatrāpy aṅguliniyamo 'py uktaḥ
kaniṣṭhānāmikāṅguṣṭhair yan nāsāpuṭadhāraṇam
prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyas tarjanīmadhyame vinā
tatra teṣu prāṇāyāmeṣu pūrvaṃ recakādiṣu saṅkhyoktā
atra ca prāṇāyāmeṣv iti bhedaḥ
tatraiva
purato japasya parato 'pi vihitam atha tattrayaṃ budhaiḥ
ṣoḍaśa ya iha samācared dineśaḥ paripūyate sa khalu māsato 'ṃhasaḥ
sanātanaḥ
japasya purata ādau parataḥ ante ca iti prāṇāyāmeṣu kālaḥ
tat trayaṃ prāṇāyāmatrayam iti saṅkhyā
yo jano dinaśaḥ pratyahaṃ ṣoḍaśaprāṇāyāmān ācaret sa māsataḥ māsenaikena aṃhasaḥ pāpāt paripūyate śuddho bhavatīti sāmānyataḥ phalam
paraṃ ca sarvaṃ purvaṃ likhitam eva
tato nijatanūm eva pūjāpīṭhaṃ prakalpayet
pīṭhasyādhāraśaktyādīn nyaset svāṅgeṣu tāravat
ādhāraśaktiṃ prakṛtiṃ kūrmānantau ca tatra tu
pṛthivīṃ kṣīrasindhuṃ ca śvetadvīpaṃ ca bhāsvaram
śrīratnamaṇḍapaṃ caiva kalpavṛkṣaṃ tathā hṛdi
nyaset pradakṣiṇatvena dharmajñāne tato 'ṃsayoḥ
ūrvor vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ tathaivādharmam ānane
trike'jñānam avairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ
hṛdabje'nantapadmaṃ ca sūryenduśikhinān tathā
maṇḍalāni kramād varṇaiḥ praṇavāṃśaiḥ sabindukaiḥ
sattvarajastamaś cātmāntarātmānau ca tatra hi
paramātmānam apy ātmādyādyavarṇaiḥ sabindukaiḥ
jñānātmānaṃ ca bhuvaneśvarībījena saṃyutam
tasyāṣṭadikṣu madhye'pi navaśaktīś ca dikkramāt
tāś coktāḥ
vimalotkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yogeti śaktayaḥ
prahvī satyā tatheśānānugrahā navam smṛtā
nyaset tadupariṣṭāc ca pīṭhamantraṃ yathoditam
ṛṣyādikaṃ smared asyāṣṭādaśārṇamanos tataḥ
jñeyāś caikāntibhiḥ kṣīrasamudrādicatuṣṭayam
kramācchrīmathurāvṛndāvanaṃ tatkuñjanīpakāḥ
tathā ca brahmasaṃhitāyām ādipuruṣarahasyastotre
sa yatra kṣīrābdhiḥ sravati surabhībhyaś ca sumahān nimeṣārdhākhyo vā vrajati na hi yatrāpi samayaḥ
bhaje śvetadvīpaṃ tam aham iha golokam iti yaṃ vidantas te santaḥ kṣitiviralacārāḥ katipaye
kramadīpikāyāṃ
evaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarvānvitaś ca bhūtātmā
ṅe'ntāḥ savāsudevāḥ sarvātmayutaṃ ca saṃyogaṃ
yogāvadhaś ca padmaṃ pīṭhāt ṅeyuto natiś cānte
pīṭhamahāmanur vyaktaḥ paryāpto 'yaṃ saparyāsu
sanātanaḥ
tāraḥ praṇavaḥ
tato hṛdayaṃ nama iti padam
tataś ca bhagavān iti viṣṇur iti ca
sarvānvitaḥ sarvaśabdayukto bhūtātmā sarvabhūtātmeti
ete trayaḥ savāsudevā vāsudevasahitāḥ pratyekaṃ ṅe'ntāś caturthyantāḥ
tataś ca sarvātmanā yutaṃ saṃyogaṃ sarvātmasaṃyogam iti napuṃsakatvam ārṣam
tataś ca yogasyāvadhau ante padmaṃ yogapadmam iti
tadante ṅeyuktaś caturthyantaḥ pīṭhātmā
tadante ca natiḥ namaḥśabdaḥ
evaṃ oṃ namo bhagavate viṣṇave sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāya sarvātmasaṃyogayogapadmapīṭhātmane nama iti siddham
tathā ca śāradātilake
namo bhagavate brūyād viṣṇave ca padaṃ vadet
sarvabhūtātmane vāsudevāyeti vadet tataḥ
sarvātmasaṃyogapadād yogapadmapadaṃ punaḥ
pīṭhātmane hṛdanto 'yaṃ mantras tārādir īritaḥ
sanatkumārakalpe ca
oṃ namaḥ padam ābhāṣya tathā bhagavate padam
vāsudevāya ity uktvā sarvātmeti padaṃ tathā
saṃyogayogety uktvā ca tathā pīṭhātmane padam
vahnipatnīsamāyuktaḥ pīṭhamantra itīritaḥ
oṃ aṣṭādaśākṣaramantrasya śrīnārada ṛṣir gāyatrīchandaḥ sakalalokamaṅgalo nandatanayo devatā hrīṃ bījaṃ svāhā śaktiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ prakṛtir durgādhiṣṭhātrī devatā abhimatārthe viniyogaḥ
tathā ca saṃmohanatantre śivomāsaṃvāde
ṛṣir nārada ity ukto gāyatrīchanda ucyate
gopaveśadharaḥ kṛṣṇo devatā parikīrtitaḥ
bījaṃ manmathasaṃjñaṃ tu priyā śaktir havir bhujaḥ
tvam eva parameśāni asyādhiṣṭhātṛdevatā
caturvargaphalāvāptyai viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
catuś caturbhir varṇaiś ca catvāry aṅgāni kalpayet
dvābhyām astrākhyam aṅgaṃ ca tasyety aṅgāni pañca vai
nyasyec ca vyāpakatvena tāny aṅgāni karadvaye
tāny aṅgulīṣu pañcātha kecid varṇān svarān api
te coktāḥ
drāvaṇakṣobhaṇākarṣavaśīkṛtsrāvaṇās tathā
śoṣaṇo mohanaḥ sandīpanas tāpanamādanau
kiṃca
namo'ntaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāṅgaiḥ śiraḥ svāhānvitaṃ śikhām
vaṣaḍyutaṃ ca kavacaṃ huṃyugastraṃ ca phaḍyutam
nyasyanti punar aṅguṣṭhau tarjanyau madhyame tathā
anāmike kaniṣṭhe ca kramād aṅgaiś ca pañcabhiḥ
punaś ca hṛdayādīni tathāṅguṣṭhādikāni ca
nyasyanti yugapat sarvāṇy aṅgais taiḥ pañcabhiḥ kramāt
nyasyanti ca ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛdayādīni tanmanoḥ
hṛdayādiṣu caiteṣāṃ pañcaikaṃ dikṣu ca kramāt
ṣaḍaṅgāni coktāni sammohanatantre sanatkumārakalpe
varṇenaikena hṛdayaṃ tribhir eva śiro matam
caturbhiś ca śikhā proktā tathaiva kavacaṃ matam
netraṃ tathā caturvarṇair astraṃ dvābhyāṃ tathā matam
tataś cāpādam ā keśān nyased dorbhyām imaṃ manum
vārāṃs trīn vyāpakatvena nyasec ca praṇavaṃ sakṛt
tato 'ṣṭādaśavarṇāṃś ca mantrasyāsya yathākramam
dante lalāṭe bhrūmadhye karṇayor netrayor dvayoḥ
nāsayor vadane kaṇṭhe hṛdi nābhau kaṭidvaye
guhye jānudvaye caikaṃ nyased ekaṃ ca pādayoḥ
santo nyasyanti tārādinamo 'nantāṃs tān sabindukān
śrīśaktikāmabījaiś ca sṛṣṭyādikramato 'pare
tāraṃ śirasi vinyasya pañca mantrapadāni ca
nyasen netradvaye vaktre hṛdguhyāṅghriṣu ca kramāt
dehe ca vyāpakatvena nyaset tāny akhile punaḥ
kecit tāni namo'ntāni nyasyanty ādyākṣaraiḥ saha
svāhāntāni tathā trīṇi saṃmiśrāṇy uttarottaraiḥ
guhyād galān mastakāc ca vyāpayya caraṇāvadhi
nyāso 'tra jñānaniṣṭhānāṃ guhyādiviṣayas tu yaḥ
svasvavarṇatanoḥ kāryas tattadvarṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaiḥ
ṛṣyādīn saptabhāgāṃś ca nyased asya manoḥ kramāt
mūrdhāsyahṛtsu kucayoḥ punar hṛdi punar hṛdi
veṇvākhyāṃ vanamālākhyāṃ mudrāṃ saṃdarśayet tataḥ
śrīvatsākhyāṃ kaustubhākhyāṃ bilvākhyāṃ ca manoramām
itthaṃ nyastaśarīraḥ san kṛtvā digbandhanaṃ punaḥ
karakacchapikāṃ kṛtvā dhyāyecchrīnandanandanam
atha prakaṭasaurabhodgalitamādhvikotphullasatprasūnanavapallavaprakaranamraśākhair drumaiḥ
praphullanavamañjarīlalitavallarīveṣṭitaiḥ smarecchiśiritaṃ śivaṃ sitamatis tu vṛndāvanam
athānantaraṃ sitamatiḥ śuddhamanāḥ san vṛndāvanaṃ cintayet
kīdṛśaṃ drumaiḥ śiśiritaṃ śītalīkṛtam
kīdṛśaiḥ prakaṭam udbhaṭaṃ saurabhaṃ yasya tac ca
tad udgalitamādhvīkaṃ ca pracyutamadhu
utphullaṃ ca vikasitaṃ
sac ca uttamaṃ yat prasūnaṃ puṣpaṃ navapallavaṃ ca
tayoḥ prakaraḥ samūhaḥ
tena namrāḥ śākhā yeṣāṃ taiḥ
mādhviketihrasvatvaṃ mahākavinibaddhatvāt soḍhavyam
prakaṭasaurabhākulitamattabhṛṅgollasad iti pāṭhas tu sugama eva
punaḥ kīdṛśaiḥ praphullābhir navamañjarībhir lalitā manoharā yā vallaryaḥ agraśākhā latā vā tābhir veṣṭitaiḥ
śivaṃ maṅgalarūpaṃ nirbādhatvāt paramakalyāṇakaratvāc ca
vikāsisumanorasāsvādanamañjulaiḥ saṃcaracchilīmukhamukhodgatair mukharitāntaraṃ jhaṅkṛtaiḥ
kapotaśukaśārikāparabhṛtādibhiḥ patribhir virāṇitam itas tato bhujagaśatrunṛtyākulam
kalindaduhituś calallaharivipruṣāṃ vāhibhir vinidrasarasīruhodararajaścayoddhūsaraiḥ
pradīpitamanobhavavrajavilāsinīvāsasāṃ vilolanavihāribhiḥ satatasevitaṃ mārutaiḥ
pravālanavapallavaṃ marakatacchadaṃ vajramauktikaprakarakorakaṃ kamalarāganānāphalam
sthaviṣṭham akhilartubhiḥ satatasevitaṃ kāmadaṃ tadantar api kalpakāṅghripam udañcitaṃ cintayet
suhemaśikharāvaler uditabhānuvad bhāsvaram adho 'sya kanakasthalīm amṛtaśīkarāsāriṇaḥ
pradīptamaṇikuṭṭimāṃ kusumareṇupuñjojjvalāṃ smaret punar atandrito vigataṣaṭtaraṅgāṃ budhaḥ
tadratnakuṭṭimaniviṣṭamahiṣṭhayogapīṭhe 'ṣṭapatram araṇaṃ kamalaṃ vicintya
udyadvirocanasarocir amuṣya madhye saṃcintayet sukhaniviṣṭam atho mukundam
sūtrāmaratnadalitāñjanameghapuñjapratyagranīlajalajanmasamānabhāsam
susnigdhanīlaghanakuñcitakeśajālaṃ rājanmanojñaśitikaṇṭhaśikhaṇḍacūḍam
rolambalālitasuradrumasūnakalpitottaṃsam utkacanavotpalakarṇapūram
lolālakasphuritabhālatalapradīptagorocanātilakam uccalacillimālam
āpūrṇaśāradagatāṅkaśaśāṅkabimbakāntānanaṃ kamalapatraviśālanetram
ratnasphuranmakarakuṇḍalaraśmidīptagaṇḍasthalīmukuram unnatacārunāsam
sindūrasundaratarādharam indukundamandāramandahasitadyutidīpitāṅgam
mattabhramadbhramarajuṣṭavilambamānasaṃtānakaprasavadāmapariṣkṛtāṃsam
hārāvalībhagaṇarājitapīvarorovyomasthalīlalitakaustubhabhānumantam
śrīvatsalakṣaṇasulakṣitam unnatāṃsaājānupīnaparivṛttasujātabāhum
ābandhurodaram udāragabhīranābhiṃ bhṛṅgāṅganānikaravañjularomarājim
divyāṅgarāgaparipiñjaritāṅgayaṣṭim āpītavastraparivītanitambabimbam
cārūrujānumanuvṛttamanojñajaṅghaṃ kāntonnataprapadaninditakūrmakāntim
matsyāṅkuśāradaraketuyavābjavajrasaṃlakṣitāruṇakarāṅghritalābhirāmam
lāvaṇyasārasamudāyavinirmitāṅgasaundaryanirjitamanobhavadehakāntim
āsyāravindaparipūritaveṇurandhralolatkarāṅgulisamīritadivyarāgaiḥ
śaśvadddravīkṛtavikṛṣṭasamastajantusaṃtānasaṃtatim anantasukhāmburāśim
gobhir mukhāmbujavilīnavilocanābhir ūdhobharaskhalitamantharamandagābhiḥ
dantāgradaṣṭapariśiṣṭatṛṇāṅkurābhir ālambvāladhilatābhivītam
saprasravastanavicūṣaṇapūrṇaniścalāsyāvaṭakṣaritapheniladugdhamugdhaiḥ
veṇupravartitamanoharamandragītadattoccakarṇayugalair api tarṇakaiś ca
pratyagraśṛṅgamṛdumastakasamprahārasaṃrambhavalganavilolakhurāgrapātaiḥ
āmedurair bahulasāsnagalair udagrapucchaiś ca vatsataravatsatarīnikāyaiḥ
hambāravakṣubhitadigvalayair mahadbhirapy ukṣabhiḥ pṛthukakudbharabhārakhinnaiḥ
uttambhitaśrutipuṭīparivītavaṃśadhvānāmṛtoddhatavikāśiviśālaghoṇaiḥ
gopaiḥ samānaguṇaśīlavayovilāsaveśaiś ca mūrchitakalasvanaveṇuvīṇaiḥ
mandroccatārapaṭagānaparair viloladorvallarīlalitalāsyavidhānadakṣaiḥ
jaṅghāntapīvarakaṭīrataṭīnibaddhavyālolakiṅkiṇighaṭāraṭitair aṭadbhiḥ
mugdhais tarakṣunakhakalpitakaṇṭhabhūṣair avyaktamañjuvacanaiḥ pṛthukaiḥ parītam
atha sulalitagopasundarīṇāṃ pṛthunivivīṣanitambamantharāṇām
gurukucabharabhaṅgurāvalagnatrivalivijṛmbhitaromarājibhājām
tadatimadhuracāruveṇuvādyāmṛtarasapallavitāṅgajāṅghripāṇām
mukulavisararamyarūḍharomodgamasamalaṃkṛtagānavallarīṇām
tadatiruciramandahāsacandrātapaparijṛmbhitarāgavārirāśeḥ
taralatarataraṅgabhaṅgavipruṭprakarasamaśramabindusaṃtatānām
tadatilalitamandacillicāpacyutaniśitekṣaṇamārabāṇavṛṣṭyā
dalitasakalamarmavihvalāṅgapravisṛtaduḥsahavepathuvyathānām
tadatisubhagakamrarūpaśobhāmṛtarasapānavidhānalālasābhyām
praṇayasalilapūravāhinīnām alasavilolavilocanāmbujābhyām
visraṃsatkavarīkalāpavigalatphullaprasūnasravanmādhvīlampaṭacañcarīkaghaṭayā saṃsevitānāṃ muhuḥ
māronmādamadaskhalanmṛdugirām ālolakāñcyucchvasannīvīviślathamānacīnahicayāntāvirnitambatviṣām
skhalitalalitapādāmbhojamandābhidhānakvaṇitamaṇitulākoṭyākulāśāmukhānām
caladadharadalānāṃ kuṭnalapakṣmalākṣidvayasarasiruhāṇām ullasatkuṇḍalānām
skhalitasya skhalanayuktasya lalitasya ca pādāmbhojasya mandābhighātena īṣad bhūbhāgaprahāreṇa kvaṇitaḥ kṛtaśabdo maṇimayo yas tulākoṭir nūpuraṃ tenākulaṃ śabdavyāptam āśānāṃ diśāṃ mukhaṃ yābhyas tāsām
kuḍmalat mukulāyamānaṃ pakṣmalaṃ ca utkṛṣṭapakṣmayuktam akṣidvayasarasiruhaṃ yāsām
drāghiṣṭhaśvasanasamīraṇābhitāpapramlānībhavadaruṇoṣṭhapallavānām
nānopāyanavilasatkarāmbujānām ālībhiḥ satataniṣevitaṃ samantāt
drāghiṣṭho 'tidīrghaḥ śvāsanasamīraṇaḥ śvāsavāyus tena abhitāpaḥ santāpas tena pramlānībhavan aruṇoṣṭhapallavo yāsām
tāsām āyatalolanīlanayanavyākoṣanīlāmbujasragbhiḥ samparipūjitākhilatanuṃ nānāvinodāspadam
tanmugdhānanapaṅkajapravigalanmādhvīrasāsvādinīṃ bibhrāṇaṃ praṇayonmadākṣimadhukṛnmālāṃ manohāriṇīm
vyākośaṃ vikasitaṃ praṇayād unmade udgatamade akṣiṇī eva madhukṛnmālā bhramarapaṅktiḥ
tāṃ bibhrāṇam prakaṭayantam
śrīlocanayor itas tato bahudhā nipatanena sarvato darśanān mālety uktam
kīdṛśīm tāsāṃ yan mugdhaṃ manoharam ānanapaṅkajaṃ
tasmāt pravigalito mādhvīrasasya makarandasya āsvādanaśīlām
ata eva manohāriṇīṃ
gopagopīpaśūnāṃ bahiḥ smared agrato 'sya gīrvāṇaghaṭām
vittārthinīṃ viriñcitrinayanaśatamanyupūrvikāṃ stotraparām
idānīṃ krameṇa vittadharmamokṣakāmākhyapuruṣārthacatuṣṭayasya tathā sarvataḥ śreṣṭhasya pañcamapuruṣārtharūpāyā bhakteś ca vāñchāyāḥ pradānāṃ devādīnāṃ dhyānam āha gopeti pañcabhiḥ
asya kṛṣṇasya agrataḥ sammukhe
taddakṣiṇato muninikaraṃ dṛḍhadharmavāñcham ānāyaparam
yogīndrān atha pṛṣṭhe mumukṣamāṇān samādhinā sanakādyān
dakṣiṇe cāsya muninikaraṃ smaret
dṛḍhā dharme vāñchā yasya tam
savye sakāntān atha yakṣasiddhagandharvavidyādharacāraṇāṃś ca
sakinnarān apsarasaś ca mukhyāḥ kāmārthino nartanagītavādyaiḥ
sakāntān patnīsahitān yakṣādīṃś ca smaret
kathambhūtān nartanādyaiḥ kāmārthino nijanijābhīṣṭaprārthakān
mukhyāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ urvaśyādyā apsarasaś ca smaret
śaṅkhendukundadhavalaṃ sakalāgamajñaṃ saudāmanītatipiṅgajaṭākalāpam
tatpādapaṅkajagatām acalāṃ ca bhaktiṃ vāñchantam ujjhitatarānyasamastasaṅgam
tasya śrīkṛṣṇasya pādapaṅkajagatāṃ tadviṣayiṇīm ity arthaḥ
ujjhitataro nitarāṃ parityakto 'nyasmin bhaktivyatirikte samaste saṅga āsaktir yena tam
nānāvidhaśrutigaṇānvitasaptarāgagrāmatrayīgatamanoharamūrchanābhiḥ
saṃprīṇayantam uditābhir amuṃ mahatyā saṃcintayen nabhasi dhātṛsutaṃ munīndram
ata eva amuṃ śrīkṛṣṇaṃ mahatyākhyayā kacchapikayā svakīyavīṇayā prīṇayantam
kābhiḥ nānāvidhaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśadbhedātmako yaḥ śrutigaṇo nādasamūhas tenānvitā ye sapta rāgāḥ niṣādādisvarā meghanādavasantādirāgā vā teṣu vā grāmatrayī tatra grāmāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ samāhāras tasyāṃ gatāḥ prāptā yā manoharā mūrchanās tābhiḥ
kimbhūtābhiḥ uditābhiḥ svayam eva prākaṭyaṃ prāptābhiḥ
mahatyoditābhir iti vā sambandhaḥ
ata eva munīndraṃ munigaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ dhātṛsutaṃ śrīnāradaṃ nabhasi samyak cintayet
śrīgautamīyatantre
atha dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
pītāmbaradharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇam
raktanetrādharaṃ raktapāṇapādanakhaṃ śubham
kaustubhodbhāsitoraskaṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitam
taddhāmavilasanmuktābaddhahāropaśobhitam
nānāratnaprabhodbhāsimukuṭaṃ divyatejasam
harakeyūrakaṭakakuṇḍalaiḥ parimaṇḍitam
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ cārunūpurādyupaśobhitam
nānāratnavicitraiś ca kaṭisūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ
barhipatrakṛtāpīḍaṃ vanyapuṣpair alaṃkṛtam
kadambakusumodbaddhavanamālāvibhūṣitam
sacandratārakānandivimalāmbarasannibham
veṇuṃ gṛhītvā hastābhyāṃ mukhe saṃyojya saṃsthitam
gāyantaṃ divyagānaiś ca goṣṭhamadhyagataṃ harim
svargād iva paribhraṣṭakanyakāśataveṣṭitam
sarvalakṣaṇasampannaṃ saundaryeṇābhiśobhitam
śubhaṃ jaganmaṅgalarūpaṃ tasya kaustubhasya dhāmnā tejasā vilasantībhir muktābhir ācchannena saṃveṣṭitena hāreṇa upaśobhitam
muktābaddheti vā pāṭhaḥ
kaṭisūtreṇāṅgulīyakaiś cālaṃkṛtam
sacandrābhis tārābhir ānandaṃ sukhakaraṃ yad vimalam ambaraṃ vyoma tatsadṛśam
atra candrasthāne kaustubhaḥ
tārāsthāne kadambamālā
ambarasthāne śrīmadvakṣaḥsthalam ūhyam
svargād iva paribhraṣṭānāṃ paramasundarīṇām ity arthaḥ
tādṛśīnāṃ kanyānāṃ śrīgopakumārīṇāṃ śatena veṣṭitam
śataśabdo 'trāsaṅkhyatve
mohanaṃ sarvagopīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ ca gavām api
lelihyamānaṃ vatsaiś ca dhenubhiś ca samantataḥ
siddhagandharvayakṣaiś ca apsarobhir vihaṅgamaiḥ
surāsuramanuṣyaiś ca sthāvaraiḥ pannagair api
mṛgair vidyādharaiś caiva vīkṣyamāṇaṃ suvismitaiḥ
nāradena vaśiṣṭhena viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
parāśareṇa vyāsena bhṛguṇāṅgirasā tathā
dakṣeṇa śaunakātribhyāṃ siddhena kapilena ca
sanakādyair munīndraiś ca brahmalokagatair api
anyair api ca saṃyuktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dhyāyed aharniśam
saṅkṣepeṇa śrīsanatkumārakalpe'pi
avyān mīlatkalāyadyutir ahiripupicchollasatkeśajālo gopīnetrotsavārādhitalalitavapur gopagovṛndavītaḥ
